Chapter 502: The Missing Everlasting Immortal

Seeing the creed leader’s baffled expression, Lu Yang became even more baffled himself. “The Everlasting Immortal—your Everlasting Creed’s faith. The one called Bu Yaolian.”

The creed leader frowned. “The Everlasting Immortal is indeed our faith, but from what I’m hearing, you’re implying he’s here with us?”

“Of course. After your Everlasting Creed resurrected the Everlasting Immortal, he existed as a soul and needed to find a suitable body. Thus, you gathered all the Foundation Establishment cultivators in the creed to compete against one another to select an appropriate vessel. I emerged victorious, and you led me to meet the Everlasting Immortal.

“After that, he got beaten up inside my mental space. Big Senior Sister contacted the imperial court, wiped out your Everlasting Creed in one go, and refined you all into tiger-henchman ghosts.”

The more Lu Yang spoke, the more the creed leader frowned. Lu Yang wouldn’t lie about something like this. So is something wrong with my memory or Lu Yang’s?

The creed leader called Chef, Chef Gao, and the others over to verify whether the Everlasting Immortal had manifested in the world.

From the barbeque chefs down to the three Alluring Ghosts, all denied having met the Everlasting Immortal.

“In my memory, that competition between Foundation Establishment cultivators was organized to select promising youths as reserve cadres for our creed. You did win, but just as I was about to award you, the imperial court’s forces stormed in and arrested us all. Later, Lord Yun Zhi refined us into tiger-henchman ghosts, and we’ve since been atoning for our sins here.

“At no point was the Everlasting Immortal involved.”

Lu Yang pressed on. “And what about how you’ve kept urging me to grow the barbeque business and expand it with chain stores across the continent? Wasn’t that goal set by the Everlasting Immortal?”

The creed leader denied it again. “No, that’s not it. I simply thought that rather than muddling through life here without purpose, I might as well find a goal. Hence, I asked for your help in expanding the barbeque business, Fellow Daoist Lu. That’s why you contacted the Nine-Netherworlds Creed to assist with opening our chain stores.”

Lu Yang presented another piece of evidence to prove the Everlasting Immortal’s existence. “Then what about your Everlasting Immortal statues? They used to be so ambiguous that you couldn’t even tell the gender. After the Everlasting Immortal appeared, you replaced all the statues with ones modeled after his true appearance. It even holds a copy of the Penal Code.”

The creed leader denied it again. “That’s not what happened. I was meditating in seclusion one day when I saw the Everlasting Immortal walking toward me in a haze. He held a copy of the Penal Code in his hands and looked at me benevolently, telling me, ‘You’ve done well. All of you have done well. In a few more days, I shall be truly born.’

“After I woke up, I realized it was an immortal sending me a message through a dream, a sign of fate with immortals. Only then did I change the statues.

“However, before that day came, your Dao-Seeking Sect and the imperial court raided us.”

The Everlasting Immortal often appeared in the barbeque shop. Everyone on the commercial street knew his face, though they were unaware of his true identity. However, when Lu Yang inquired at neighboring shops, none had any memory of him. Lu Yang even stopped several senior disciples passing by. They were regulars at the barbeque shop, but all claimed they had never seen the Everlasting Immortal before.

“Does the Everlasting Immortal really not exist?” After a round of fruitless questioning, Lu Yang began doubting his own memories and wondered if someone had implanted false memories in his mind.

“Immortal Fairy, wake up. We have a problem.” Lu Yang shook the sleeping Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

After the celebration ended, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy claimed she was mentally and physically exhausted from overusing her brain and promptly collapsed into deep sleep in his mental space.

In any case, Lu Yang frankly couldn’t understand what part of sitting on the judges’ platform all day—aside from their single staged confrontation—could possibly have tired her out.

“Whaaat?” she groaned, dragging out the syllable petulantly.

With tremendous effort, she cracked one eyelid open just enough to glare at Lu Yang before immediately rolling back over. “Let this sect leader sleep a while longer...” she mumbled as her eyes closed again.

“The Everlasting Immortal is missing.”

“Wut? Our third-in-command is missing?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy bolted upright.

There are three people in our Everlasting Lineage. I’m the first-in-command, Lu Yang is the second-in-command, and the Everlasting Immortal is the third-in-command. That brings our average cultivation to half-immortal, making us a formidable force. Now that the Everlasting Immortal is missing...

...Seems like the average cultivation is still half-immortal?

It feels like the third-in-command isn’t that essential after all.

“Hold on, how did he go missing without rhyme or reason?”

Her reaction reassured Lu Yang that the issue wasn’t with his memories. Everyone else’s memories of the Everlasting Immortal were erased and supplanted with other memories.

Lu Yang reported everything he had discovered so far, from his initial suspicions to the current findings of his investigation.

“Hmm, that’s quite interesting,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused. “Sounds like a karmic spell, though such petty tricks mean nothing to me. With my protection, you won’t be affected by it.”

“Karmic spells?” The concept of karma was still too abstruse for Lu Yang’s current realm, and he had no need to understand such things yet.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy explained, “From the moment one is born—no, from the moment a soul is conceived in the womb—connections with the world are already established.”

To illustrate her point, she conjured a white paper and drew a circle. “This represents you at birth.”

She drew another circle nearby. “This is someone else.”

A line connected the two circles. “After you’re born, when others see you, a karmic bond is formed; the same holds true when you notice them.

“Between strangers, the karmic link is faint. A passing glance, and he forgets you quickly. Then, the karmic tie no longer exists.

“But suppose you were born with supernatural strength and kicked their leg broken when you were just born. He wouldn’t forget you then, and the karma between you would deepen.” As she spoke, the line connecting the two circles thickened conspicuously.

“As you grow up and interact with more people, you will establish more karmic ties with this world. Your childhood playmates and the fellow disciples and elders you’ve encountered after joining the Dao-Seeking Sect—all of them share close karmic connections with you.

“This is why some cultivators choose to cultivate secluded from the world. It’s precisely because too many karmic ties in the mundane world hinder their cultivation. When everyone forgets your existence, their karmic bonds with you disappear. And this is our third-in-command’s current situation.”

It was only now that Lu Yang realized the Everlasting Immortal had already formed this many connections with the world around him since his birth—the Everlasting Immortal had interacted with the Everlasting Creed’s higher-ups, him, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Big Senior Sister, and the merchants and Dao-Seeking Sect disciples on the commercial street. As long as these threads of karma were severed, everyone’s memories of the person would be forgotten or replaced with new memories. At that time, this person would no longer have any connection with the entire world.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “Of course, considering the third-in-command’s cultivation and how thoroughly these people have forgotten everything, the karmic spells I know of shouldn’t be able to achieve this. Either your era has developed more powerful karmic spells, or someone has attained a Dao Fruit related to karma.”

Chapter 503: The Imperial Preceptor Who Got Blasted for Ten Days

“Does too much karma really hinder one’s cultivation?”

“Hard to say. I don’t think so, but plenty of others do.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shrugged. Her views had always diverged from the mainstream. “You remember that the defining trait of an immortal is oblivion, right? Doesn’t it feel somewhat similar now?”

Only after the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reminder did Lu Yang realize it was the case indeed. In a way, the immortal trait resembled the manifestation of severing karma. “So...the immortal trait is meant to sever karma?”

“That’s right. The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others believed that only by cutting off all karma could one advance a step further in cultivation. But I disagree; I think the more karma one has, the higher their cultivation can reach.”

“Advance a step further?” Lu Yang’s eyes widened as if he had stumbled upon something monumental. “Immortals can still advance further?”

“The five of us once deduced it using five Dao Fruits. Theoretically, it’s possible, but no one has succeeded. Nobody knows if the next step truly exists. The Nine-Layers Immortal was the first to become an immortal. At the very least, none of us five managed to do it, nor did anyone before us.

“The term ‘immortal trait’ was coined by the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others. The four of them ascended to immortals first, and when they condensed their Dao Fruits, they chose oblivion as the trait of Dao Fruits. That's why they named oblivion as the ‘immortal trait’ without consulting me.

“I was the last to become an immortal, and I didn’t choose oblivion when forming my Dao Fruit. This is why I lack the immortal trait.”

Lu Yang asked, “Is that to say that the immortal trait isn’t an inherent and necessary trait of immortals, but rather the result of each immortal’s individual choice?”

“Yes. For example, that immortal who wields the national fortune also chose the oblivion trait.”

“But isn’t his Dao Fruit related to the national fortune and Great Xia? The karma he bears is heavier than anyone else’s. Why would he choose this path?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied, “Simple. He wants to advance a step further. When the time comes, he can just change the bearer of karma and shift the burden of karma to someone else.

“Didn’t you just say the origin of the third-in-command’s statue was once an irrefutable proof of his existence? There was karma between him and the statue. But now, it’s been altered to the creed leader’s dream, thereby establishing karma between the creed leader and the third-in-command’s statue. freewebnovel.com

“The third-in-command set the goal of expanding and strengthening the barbeque business. Every action the barbeque shop took was in pursuit of that goal, developing karma between the third-in-command and future deeds. But now, it’s been changed to the creed leader’s goal, which implies that the creed leader bears the karma of all those actions instead.

“This is what it means to change the bearer of karma. Replacement is another form of oblivion.”

Lu Yang vaguely felt he had grasped some clues, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had said too much. The plethora of clues left him unsure where to even begin.

“Enough of this. Let’s save the third-in-command first.”

“How?” Lu Yang was puzzled. He hadn’t even found any trace of the Everlasting Immortal yet.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy planted her hands on her hips and ordered Lu Yang, “Go fetch Lass Yun. How could subordinates slack off while this sect leader does all the work?”

Under the tyrannical authority of the acting sect leader, Lu Yang had no choice but to head to Incarceration Peak to look for Yun Zhi.

~~~

Yun Zhi was in the midst of interrogating the Black-White Venerable Lord.

When Lu Yang arrived at Incarceration Peak, Yun Zhi was lashing the Black-White Venerable Lord with a whip. Despite his elderly appearance, the man’s physique was unnaturally tough. No matter how much he howled in pain, he showed no signs of dying from the flogging.

“Little Junior Brother, is anything the matter?” Yun Zhi paused, flicking the whip in the air with a sharp crack before folding it neatly into thirds in her hand, her movements executed with practiced ease.

“Here's the thing...” Lu Yang recounted his discoveries and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s conjecture.

The Black-White Venerable Lord listened in horror, his heart almost leaping out of his chest. I’ve spent my entire life studying the nature of the Imperial Preceptor’s Incipient Dao Fruit to no avail; how did they infer it in mere sentences?

From the sound of it, the Dao-Seeking Sect also has a half-immortal, and the Imperial Preceptor is currently locked in a gruelling battle with him?

And why does our target for this mission—Golden Core cultivator Lu Yang—know all this?

Just what kind of monstrous place is the Dao-Seeking Sect?

“Senior, please come out.” Yun Zhi summoned the Everlasting Immortal Fairy impassively.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was like a child who had done something wrong, cowering in the presence of Yun Zhi. Wait, that’s not right. I am the acting sect leader. What’s there to be afraid of?

Yun Zhi calmly looked at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, who had her head lowered. “Senior, I believe I’ve told you before that Lu Yang is still young and that his cultivation is insufficient. Matters relating to immortals and Dao Fruits are far beyond his reach. You shouldn’t speak of such things, lest he bite off more than he can chew and affect his cultivation. This time, you’ve said too much.”

“I was wrong.” As the acting sect leader, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy knew how to give and take, admitting her faults without hesitation.

“Senior, may I know how you intend to locate the Everlasting Immortal, given that his karma has been erased?”

Naturally, Yun Zhi still remembered the Everlasting Immortal’s existence.

“Hehe, others might be hard to track down, the third-in-command? Easy.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy smirked, proud of her own Dao Fruit.

She instructed Lu Yang to retrieve the statue of the Everlasting Immortal from the barbeque shop before proceeding to recite the third-in-command’s title and name.

“Everlasting Immortal Bu Yaolian.”

~~~

Inside a temporarily constructed pocket space, two figures stood panting.

“Damn, he’s a tough nut to crack. What on earth is this grandson’s Incipient Dao Fruit?” The Everlasting Immortal possessed a vast collection of memories from all the Everlasting Creed’s followers, yet none had prepared him for a battle of this level. Even now, he still couldn’t figure out the Imperial Preceptor’s Incipient Dao Fruit.

Ten straight days of self-detonation had pushed even his Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit to its limits.

A complete Everlasting Dao Fruit could withstand infinite self-detonations, but the Everlasting Immortal’s Incipient Dao Fruit had only coalesced half a year ago. It was still a far cry from the complete Everlasting Dao Fruit. To have held his own against the Imperial Preceptor, whose Karma Incipient Dao Fruit had been formed ten thousand years ago, was truly a remarkable feat.

The Everlasting Immortal was in a sorry state, but the Imperial Preceptor fared worse. He had lost count of how many times he had been blown up these past ten days. Not a single part of him remained unscathed.

Despite having faced stronger foes, it was his first time meeting one this troublesome. He had tried to flee multiple times, but once he erased his karma and vanished, the Everlasting Immortal would self-detonate, destabilizing the space so violently that not even a rift could be opened.

“What cursed luck is this to have bumped into the Dao-Seeking Sect’s true guardian!” Even the Imperial Preceptor’s famed composure shattered under such circumstances.

“True guardian? I’ve only been at the Dao-Seeking Sect for half a year.”

“Half a year? An almighty half-immortal powerhouse like yourself is holed up in this tiny place? What could possibly be worth staying for? Look, I admit my mistake; I shouldn’t have attacked you. How about this? No discord, no concord—friends are often made after a fight. If you have nowhere else to go, you can join us Great Yu. I have a way to help you restore your physical form!” The Imperial Preceptor assumed the Everlasting Immortal had remained here to recover. There’s no need for us to fight to the death; we can cooperate.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy eyed him suspiciously, finding him treacherous. “I’m a prisoner, yet you’re trying to instigate me into escaping?”

“Prisoner?” The Imperial Preceptor’s blood ran cold. Who would imprison a half-immortal?

Suddenly, the Everlasting Immortal froze, then smiled. I sense the first-in-command calling for me.

Taking advantage of the Imperial Preceptor’s brief stupor, he lunged forward and trapped him in a tight embrace.

The Imperial Preceptor cursed inwardly. Oh no! I gave him a chance to self-detonate at point-blank range!

Until now, he had relied on his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit to evade the blasts from a safe distance. If he had taken a few direct hits at close range, he would have long died from the explosions.

To his surprise, instead of self-detonating, a spatial door opened behind the Everlasting Immortal, and he stepped backward with the Imperial Preceptor still in his grip.

Thud! Both half-immortal powerhouses fell onto Incarceration Peak simultaneously.

The Imperial Preceptor stared blankly at the cold-faced Yun Zhi and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinning wickedly beside her.

Chapter 504: We Three

The Imperial Preceptor was perplexed. The temporary pocket space where he fought the Everlasting Immortal had been constructed by him. Aside from himself—the master of this space—no one should have been able to open an exit and escape.

Yet now, without his permission, the Everlasting Immortal had dragged him out of the space.

Is this the power of his Incipient Dao Fruit?

At the moment, this seems like the only plausible explanation.

The Black-White Venerable Lord was stupefied. He couldn’t help but think the person who had just appeared resembled the Imperial Preceptor. However, the bloody nose and battered face before him bore hardly any semblance to the Imperial Preceptor in his memory.

As soon as the Everlasting Immortal saw Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and Yun Zhi, a wave of uncanny familiarity washed over him, and his very soul throbbed with pain in response.

However, he quickly remembered that he was now one of their own. The Imperial Preceptor was the one who was supposed to get pummeled.

“First-In-Command, Second-In-Command! You’ve finally come to save me!” Tears streamed down the Everlasting Immortal’s face.

These past ten days had genuinely been brutal for him. He was on his own and blew himself up repeatedly to blast the Imperial Preceptor. His Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit had withered, and his soul had dimmed. Recovery would not be easy.

Logically speaking, so long as the creed leader and the others had noticed his disappearance and called his title and true name before the statue, he could have escaped the temporary space.

Yet he waited for ten days without hearing them call out to him.

He surmised that if the Imperial Preceptor could make him forget about the Imperial Preceptor’s existence, he could also have made the creed leader and the others forget about himself.

“Look at how disgraceful you are. Ten days, and you still couldn’t win?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy eyed the bawling Everlasting Immortal with disdain, halting him when he was three steps away from her.

With a casual flick of her fingers, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy revived the third-in-command’s dimmed soul as if granting it new life. In an instant, it was fully restored. Even the withered Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit swelled with renewed vigor.

“Go back and train properly,” she chided. “My Dao Fruit shouldn’t be this useless. All you know is self-detonation.” With her ample experience in self-detonation, it only took a single glance at the Imperial Preceptor’s pitiful state for her to deduce that this was the aftermath of the Everlasting Immortal’s repeated self-detonations.

“Yes!”

“That’s more like it. Alright, go hide in the back now.”

The Everlasting Immortal scurried behind his first-in-command and second-in-command.

“Brother, what crime did you commit to get beaten this badly?” the Everlasting Immortal asked curiously, his face full of gossip. He was now brimming with infinite energy.

The Black-White Venerable Lord, “...”

The Imperial Preceptor’s hawk-like eyes sharpened as he heard the Everlasting Immortal refer to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Lu Yang as “first-in-command” and “second-in-command.”

Does that mean the so-called Everlasting Lineage consists of three people, with him ranked third?

And our target, Lu Yang, is ranked second?

He felt that the Everlasting Lineage’s waters ran terrifyingly deep. This is no place to linger. I must flee quickly.

If even the third-in-command is this hard to deal with, with the first-in-command and second-in-command here, what hope of surviving do I have if a real fight breaks out?

Acting decisively, he immediately activated the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, erasing his existence. With so many people around, they wouldn’t dare self-detonate recklessly and harm innocent bystanders!

His lips curled into a faint smirk as he boldly strode past the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Even if our plan at the Dao-Seeking Sect had failed, as long as Shifu and I live, Great Yu can still be restored!

Smack! As the Everlasting Immortal Fairy watched the Imperial Preceptor walk right past her, grinning like a madman as though she was beneath his notice, she instinctively raised her hand and slapped him.

The Imperial Preceptor twirled halfway through the air before crashing headfirst to the ground with a thud.

“The Imperial Preceptor is an idiot?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused aloud. People usually don’t flee like this either.

Is this all he has to offer? The Imperial Preceptor that the Great Yu cultivators had praised as peerless in intellect?

By comparison, I’m clearly the smarter one.

“He’s probably an idiot.” Lu Yang agreed solemnly. Anyone who had concocted a plan like infiltrating the Dao-Seeking Sect couldn’t have had a high IQ.

The Imperial Preceptor lay sprawled on the ground, dumbfounded. How is this possible? I’d even activated my Karma Incipient Dao Fruit. How could anyone still detect me?

Unless...

An immortal?!” His eyes widened as the gravity of the situation finally struck him. The Everlasting Lineage’s first-in-command is an immortal?!

What kind of joke is this? Since when has any immortal throughout history borne the title of “Everlasting?”

“Soul-Breaking Needle!” He drew his last remaining Soul-Breaking Needle—the weapon that had once sundered the Everlasting Immortal’s soul!

Aiming at the Everlasting Immortal, he shot the needle with blinding speed, its tip imbued with the attribute of “oblivion.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy casually caught the needle between two fingers and examined it curiously. “What’s this thing? Oh, an immortal treasure that can split souls. Ah, it has a pretty ingenious design. Let me test its power.”

She tried pricking herself.

The needle shattered.

She remained unharmed.

“Ahhh? That’s it?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy pouted. This plaything might work on a half-immortal, but it’s useless against an immortal with a powerful soul like me.

The Imperial Preceptor’s blood ran cold at the sight. My proudest Soul-Breaking Needle couldn’t even hold her back! Even Shifu, the first imperial preceptor, refused to take a hit from these needles!

He closed his eyes slowly, wrestling inwardly. When they snapped open again, his gaze was deranged. “Immortal, don’t think capturing me means you’ve won. Today, I’ll show you why a ten-thousand-year half-immortal isn’t to be trifled with. Even if it costs my life, I’ll rip away a piece of your soul!

“I offer my life as sacrifice to Great Yu!”

Blood poured from his orifices as he sacrificed his lifespan for a temporary surge of power. This was also a feature of his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit—karma demanded equivalent exchange.

A half-immortal’s lifespan spanned at least a hundred thousand years. As his lifespan slipped away rapidly, he felt the day of his end drawing closer, yet his body grew stronger. If he fought the Everlasting Immortal now, he was confident he could survive the self-detonation and capture his opponent alive. Unfortunately, there was no turning back; this move was irreversible. After the surge in power, he would only have a few years left to live.

Space shook, and spirit qi scattered. It felt like his soul was pricked by needles as an inexplicable fear took root in his heart.

The Everlasting Immortal and the Black-White Venerable Lord paled, their hearts pounding. They could sense a fatal threat from this move.

“You all forced my hand. Behold my ultimate move...”

Crash! Seeing the Imperial Preceptor charge up, Yun Zhi kicked him squarely to the ground.

The buildup naturally dissipated into nothingness and went down the drain.

The sacrificed lifespan was also absorbed by heaven and earth, never to be returned.

“How is this possible?! This move can’t be interrupted!” the Imperial Preceptor shrieked in disbelief. Throughout this mission to the Dao-Seeking Sect, none of my decisions worked out, and now even my suicide move has been interrupted!

Lu Yang sighed, walking to the Imperial Preceptor and pointing at him. “Just surrender obediently. With the three of us here, even the Heaven Mandate Immortal would admit defeat, let alone you.”

The Imperial Preceptor inhaled deeply and shot Lu Yang a death stare. Since escape is impossible, and battle is impossible, I’ll drag you to die with me!

He activated another function of the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit—Curse.

“I, Jin Buqun, hereby swear: You shall endure the Eight Sufferings—birth, aging, sickness, death, unfulfilled desires, encounters with hatred, partings from loved ones, and the five clinging-aggregates.[1] You shall face the Seven Calamities—fire, water, Rakshasa, blades and staffs, ghosts, shackles, and vengeful enemies. In life, your cultivation will stagnate; in death, your soul will disintegrate!”

1. This is one of the Eight Sufferings in Buddhism. Clinging is a source of suffering, and five aspects result in this. The five aggregates are: form, feeling, perception, mental formations, and consciousness. ☜

Chapter 505: Curse Backlash

Curses were but one manifestation of karma. For most, casting a curse required one to pay a corresponding price. For example, the price of Meng Jingzhou’s self-taught Single’s Curse Fist was the need to preserve yang energy before immortal ascension.

However, since the Imperial Preceptor wielded the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, he didn’t need to pay such a price.

The Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings were a concept proposed by the Buddhist sects. It encompassed all worldly misery and stood as the pinnacle of curses. Compared to this, Meng Jingzhou’s Single’s Curse Fist wasn’t even fit to tie its shoes.

After a series of defeats, realization finally dawned upon the Imperial Preceptor. With the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and Yun Zhi present, escape was impossible.

Since I can’t escape, I’ll drag one down with me!

Among his foes, Lu Yang had the lowest cultivation. Furthermore, he was the reason the Great Yu cultivators had come to the Dao-Seeking Sect. Every failed plan bears a trace of Lu Yang’s involvement.

The capture of the Black-White Venerable Lord also meant that the rest of his subordinates who had infiltrated the Dao-Seeking Sect had faced a similar plight.

Complete wipeout!

Rather than saying it was the Dao-Seeking Sect that thwarted Great Yu’s resurgence, it’s more accurate to say it was Lu Yang, this stumbling block, who got in the way!

It doesn’t matter even if I get captured. Great Yu still has Shifu and the slumbering cultivators from the mid to late Great Yu era. There’s still hope for resurgence.

Then I just have to eliminate Lu Yang!

He cast upon Lu Yang the most painful and ruthless curse imaginable. Let alone the Golden Core Stage, even if Lu Yang were at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage, he’d no doubt die!

In the Imperial Preceptor’s vision, shackles fell from the heavens, assembling themselves midair. Wrought from blood and punishment, they descended upon the mortal realm to deliver the most excruciating punishment possible.

These shackles were a manifestation of the curse, invisible to even those proficient in karmic spells. Only the Imperial Preceptor, a half-immortal who devoted himself to studying karma and condensed the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, could witness all of this.

The heavy shackles produced a resonant clatter like the sound of Dao with each collision.

You dared to get so close to me? Now it’s too late for regrets!

The Imperial Preceptor observed their expressions with keen interest, eager to see their visages twisted in regret and sorrow—regret for underestimating him and sorrow for Lu Yang’s inevitable doom.

Instead, he saw Lu Yang’s expression remain unchanged, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy looking utterly baffled, and Yun Zhi’s face as impassive as ever.

Not a trace of the regret or sorrow he had hoped for.

As the shackles closed in on Lu Yang, he suddenly erupted with golden light, revealing two thick threads of karma coiled around him, one connecting him to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy and the other to Yun Zhi. The moment the shackles touched him, they rebounded violently straight back to the Imperial Preceptor.

The Imperial Preceptor could only watch in horror as his curse backfired, letting out a roar in indignation. “NO!!!”

What’s with the karma on this brat? It’s just two threads of karma, yet they had completely warded off my proudest curse?!

The one who had slapped me is an immortal—how could an immortal share such a deep karmic bond with a mortal?!

And the other one who interrupted my spell—her karmic tie with Lu Yang had also deflected the curse!

For karma alone to repel my curse... that means she’s also an immortal!

These two breathtakingly beautiful women are immortals!

What kind of joke is this? How could a tiny sect like this possibly harbor two immortals?! In his twenty thousand years of life, the Imperial Preceptor had never heard of any sect with two immortals. Not even our Great Yu Dynasty had achieved that!

What on earth is this Dao-Seeking Sect? Even calling it a dragon's lair or a tiger’s den wouldn’t be enough to describe the perils of this place. Invading the imperial palace would have been safer than setting foot here!

The Imperial Preceptor felt a burst of flames in his heart, scorching him until he writhed on the ground. At the same time, it was as if a globe of water had encased his head, drowning him like a helpless immortal.

The curse backlash afflicted him with two of the Seven Calamities: fire and water.

“What’s going on?” Lu Yang was bewildered. One moment, the Imperial Preceptor had been glaring at me viciously and spouting a bunch of incomprehensible incantations. The next moment, he’s rolling on the ground, howling ceaselessly as if he is begging for death.

“Curse backlash,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied. “He tried to curse you with the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings, but with me protecting you, the curse couldn’t touch you. The curse backfired on him, and he’s suffering from it now.” She glanced at the Imperial Preceptor like he was an idiot. As I thought, he’s not very bright.

The Black-White Venerable Lord watched as the Imperial Preceptor’s trump cards were effortlessly neutralized one after another. His heart sank to the bottom. freewebnovel.com

The Dao-Seeking Sect’s waters truly run deep.

“Big Boss, do you want to protect me too?” The third-in-command, Everlasting Immortal, sidled up to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy with a sycophant smile.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot him a sidelong glance and waved him off. “Shoo shoo shoo, why should I protect you? If you ever get cursed, just self-detonate a few times and you’ll be more or less fine.”

The Everlasting Immortal slunk away, resuming his chat with the Black-White Venerable Lord. “Brother, how did you get caught? Did you sneak into the Dao-Seeking Sect with that idiot rolling around on the ground? Didn’t you know the Dao-Seeking Sect is my First-In-Command’s turf? Back in the day, even the Four Ancient Immortals didn’t dare barge in here carelessly. When they did visit, they treaded lightly, not even daring to breathe too loudly.”

The Black-White Venerable Lord, “...”

Damn it, just stop speaking. The more you talk, the more I regret everything.

The Everlasting Immortal continued, “Thankfully, I defected to the Dao-Seeking Sect early. Otherwise, I would be getting tortured just like you.” He was glad he had cowardly surrendered the moment he realized the Everlasting Immortal Fairy outranked him.

The Black-White Venerable Lord asked, “So, are you now the Dao-Seeking Sect’s guest elder or elder?”

“Prisoner.”

The Black-White Venerable Lord, “...”

Lu Yang clapped his hands cheerfully. “No matter what, we’ve finally rounded up all the Great Yu cultivators in one fell swoop. A cause for celebration!” Lately, my luck has been awful. I’d run into Great Yu cultivators every time I went out. This time, I finally don’t have to worry about that anymore.

“Hehe, and that’s all thanks to my brilliant leadership as the acting sect leader.” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy planted her hands on her hips, unable to stop grinning from ear to ear.

“The Immortal Fairy is wise and brilliant! With the Immortal Fairy here, the Great Yu cultivators are nothing to fear!” Lu Yang continued clapping and spared no effort in flattering her.

“Rounded up in one fell swoop?” The Black-White Venerable Lord felt a sense of dread at Lu Yang’s words.

Lu Yang turned to him with a cheeky smirk and casually said, “You know Wu Youdao, the sixth Yu emperor, right? He’s here too. The Immortal Fairy and I caught him together.”

“You captured His Majesty?!” The Black-White Venerable Lord’s eyes nearly bulged out of his skull. After the battle at Hanshui City, he had lost contact with Wu Youdao. He had assumed Wu Youdao and the others were recuperating from severe injuries somewhere. Never had he imagined they’d been captured by the Dao-Seeking Sect!

This Lu Yang truly is our Great Yu’s greatest obstacle!

I’d originally thought Lu Yang’s interference in Hanshui City was simply exposing Huang Ming’s existence. I didn’t expect that even His Majesty’s capture was his doing!

Yun Zhi paid no attention to Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s back-and-forth adulation. She was prepared to interrogate the Imperial Preceptor, who was still shrieking in agony on the ground.

“I ask, you answer.”

“AAAAAHHHH!”

“How many cultivators does Great Yu have in total?”

“AAAAAHHHH!”

“After this failure, does Great Yu have any backup plans?”

“AAAAAHHHH!”

It wasn’t that the Imperial Preceptor was refusing to confess. The torment from the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings was simply so unbearable that he couldn’t force out a single word.

Yun Zhi sighed. Despite having interrogated countless people, it’s my first time encountering a situation like this.

Chapter 506: The Imperial Preceptor Is Probably Beyond Saving

Incarceration Peak was shrouded in silence all year round, save for the occasional plangent wails of prisoners. Their howls usually didn’t last for long. A few cries, and they would spill everything. Those who stubbornly refused would simply be refined into artifact spirits.

Today, however, was different. This particular prisoner had been shrieking for a full hour with no signs of stopping. Due to his high cultivation level, his throat never went hoarse no matter how much he screamed.

“So what do we do now?”

Lu Yang, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, and Yun Zhi stared helplessly at the still-wailing Imperial Preceptor.

Even Yun Zhi found him too noisy and set up a soundproofing array so he could scream all he wanted inside without bothering anyone outside.

Instantly, everything became peaceful.

Lu Yang shook his head in disappointment. It wasn’t easy capturing a key figure of Great Yu, yet he turns out to be a tough nut to crack. He’d rather suffer from the curse than divulge even a shred of intel.

Yun Zhi had tried numerous curse-breaking methods, but none worked on the Imperial Preceptor.

Removing just one of the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings could easily be resolved by a spell from Yun Zhi. However, the Imperial Preceptor was afflicted by all of them, along with curses that stagnated his cultivation in life and disintegrated his soul in death. This was an unprecedentedly great curse. Even the Imperial Preceptor himself, the wielder of the Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, couldn’t remove it.

“Immortal Fairy, why don’t you lend him an Incipient Dao Fruit and let him self-detonate a hundred times to remove the curse?” The wielder of a complete Dao Fruit commanded absolute authority over their corresponding Incipient Dao Fruits; they could bestow or revoke them at will.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “That won’t do. He already has an Incipient Dao Fruit inside him. No one can possess two at once.

“Besides, even if he doesn’t have his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, I still can’t give him mine. It’s not like Incipient Dao Fruits are clothing you can just put on and take off whenever you feel like it.

“An Incipient Dao Fruit represents rules. To wield one, you must first comprehend the corresponding set of rules to some degree. This idiot knows nothing about my Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit. If I give it to him directly, his soul wouldn’t be able to withstand its might and disintegrate.”

After the Imperial Preceptor’s repeated blunders, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy wondered whether his brain worked at all. Did he become a half-immortal through sheer luck?

“Hold on, Immortal Fairy. By that logic, I don’t have any comprehension of the Everlasting Dao Fruit either, right? Yet you’ve been saying you could give me your Everlasting Incipient Fruit.” Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy constantly clamoring about forcing one upon him.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy looked at Lu Yang in shock. “Second-In-Command, what are you talking about? Under my long-term guidance and subtle influence, your comprehension of the Everlasting Dao Fruit far outclasses the Third-In-Command’s.”

Lu Yang, “...”

When did that happen? Why don’t I know?

“Did you think I made you second-in-command just because we’re close? How absurd! I am impartial and just. Ranking within the Everlasting Lineage is determined by strength!”

Hearing an opportunity for promotion, the Everlasting Immortal eagerly scooted over. “Big Boss, rest assured! I will devote myself to comprehending the Dao Fruit and strive to become the second-in-command!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy eyed him with disdain and waved him off impatiently. “Shoo shoo shoo, why are you butting in? If you dare try to become the second-in-command, I will strip you of your Incipient Dao Fruit.”

The Everlasting Immortal cast an envious glance at Lu Yang before slinking away in defeat. freewebnovel.com

“Can the power of national fortune break curses?” Lu Yang recalled how his creed’s holy son, Meng Jingzhou, had once been cursed by a vile scoundrel and was unable to interact with women. In the end, it was only with the national fortune’s aid that he managed to remove the curse.

Yun Zhi nodded. “That’s a plausible solution.”

She hooked her forefinger; the Imperial Preceptor, who had been writhing on the ground in pain, found himself writhing in the air instead.

“I’m heading to the imperial palace. Wait for me at Incarceration Peak.” With that, Yun Zhi rose and departed for the palace. Since they planned to use the national fortune, going straight to its source was naturally the most convenient.

The prisoners locked up in Incarceration Peak were the most vicious and fiendish individuals. Merely standing there would make the faint-hearted tremble in fear.

Lu Yang felt no such fear. Everyone on Incarceration Peak—new or old—knew him. The newcomers were dragged in by him, while the old-timers had watched as he dragged the newcomers in. If anyone should be afraid, it was the prisoners who feared Lu Yang.

The prisoners whispered among themselves, careful not to let Lu Yang overhear. With only their souls remaining and their powers and spiritual consciousness sealed, the prisoners had developed their own method of communication to avoid detection.

The cells of Incarceration Peak were forged from refined ores designed to seal souls and meant to be indestructible. The prisoners would speak against the metal bars, letting the vibrations carry their words, then rely on the keen senses of their souls to perceive the message.

“Oh my heavens, did you see that fight earlier? A half-immortal powerhouse attacked Lu Yang, yet he instantly collapsed to the ground despite Lu Yang not lifting a finger!”

“This Lu Yang is unfathomable. He looks like a mere Golden Core cultivator, but his true strength definitely goes beyond that.”

“Have you noticed? Ever since Lu Yang joined the Dao-Seeking Sect, the number of people at Incarceration Peak has increased exponentially. First, it was just Fusion cultivators, then it was Transcendent Tribulation cultivators, and now even a half-immortal has been captured! How is that something a Golden Core cultivator could pull off?”

“I’ve never met a half-immortal in my life. I didn’t expect to see one here instead.”

“Is this the Battle of the Great Era? Even someone as strong as a half-immortal can be reduced to a prisoner.”

The more the prisoners discussed, the more alarmed they grew. They found Lu Yang an enigma of terror, someone they must not provoke under any circumstances.

Unaware of the prisoners’ hushed chatter, Lu Yang seized the opportunity while Yun Zhi wasn’t around to resume his high-level discussion with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Immortal Fairy, if immortals need to sever karma to advance a step further, wouldn’t the Imperial Preceptor’s Karma Incipient Dao Fruit give him a significant advantage?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy emphasized, “It’s not that immortals need to sever karma to advance a step further—it’s that the Heaven Mandate Immortal and others believed they needed to do so.”

“Fine, let’s say the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others did believe so. Then if the Imperial Preceptor upgrades his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit into a Karma Dao Fruit, wouldn’t that allow him to sever karma at will and ascend to a being beyond immortals?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head. “You can’t think of it like that. The moment the Imperial Preceptor condensed his Karma Incipient Dao Fruit, he developed tens of thousands of karmic connections with the concept of ‘karma.’ Upgrading it into a Karma Dao Fruit would only bind him closer to this ‘karma’ concept, merging them into one. If he becomes one with ‘karma,’ how is he going to sever it?

“I presume he had heard somewhere that immortals attach great importance to karma, which led him to pursue condensing a Karma Incipient Dao Fruit. Little did he know that he was walking onto the wrong path and making the most elementary mistake.

“There are no shortcuts to becoming an immortal. Trickery and opportunism won’t get you anywhere.

“Speaking of which, although a realm above immortals may indeed exist, none of us five ever paid it much mind.”

“Why’s that?”

“Because there was no need! We were already immortals—our lifespans were infinite, we were unbeatable, and life was good. Why would we insist on pursuing some higher realm?”

Lu Yang felt that the Everlasting Immortal Fairy made a lot of sense.

Chapter 507: Advanced Golden Core Stage

If it were Lu Yang, he figured that if he became an immortal, he would probably be more of a salted fish slacker[1] than the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, spending his days sunbathing, flipping from front to back and back to front, then sleeping on the sun at night. Beyond immortals lay a higher realm, and beyond that were even higher realms. If one kept cultivating endlessly, where would it ever end?

“Immortal Fairy, you once said that replacement is also a form of oblivion. In that case, when the authorship of your recipes was transferred to the Heaven Mandate Immortal, could that have been a method of replacement too?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes lit up, and she patted Lu Yang’s shoulder. “Eh, now that you mention it, that makes sense! Someone might have killed me and used some method to erase all traces of my existence, attributing everything I’d done to the Heaven Mandate Immortal. I initially thought that this grandson Heaven Mandate Immortal was envious of my talent and stole my credit while I was gone!

“Ah, a teachable young kid!”

“It’s ‘a teachable young talent.’”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s brain must have been addled by food poisoning to claim credit for your work.

He asked, “Then, among the four immortals, was anyone capable of erasing your existence?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, running through each of the four immortals’ abilities but found no match. “No, none of their methods could have achieved that.”

They continued discussing for a while longer, but it still yielded nothing fruitful.

It wasn’t entirely fair to say the Heaven Mandate Immortal had killed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. Perhaps the Qilin Immortal and the others had also seized her authorship. Immortals’ items were already rare, but the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s belongings were even scarcer, unless they could uncover the inheritance the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had buried in the North Star. It would surely contain records of ownership that might offer clues.

Just as the two were discussing what to do after the tenure as acting sect leader ended and retirement began, Yun Zhi returned with the Imperial Preceptor in tow. Although no sound could be heard, the Imperial Preceptor’s contorted form and agonized expression made it apparent the curse was still unbroken.

“Big Senior Sister, couldn’t the power of national fortune remove the curse?” freewebnovel.com

“It could, but the Xia Emperor refused,” Yun Zhi replied as she casually tossed the Imperial Preceptor aside.

“Why? Didn’t Old Meng and Sect Leader Qiu have their curses lifted?” Lu Yang was puzzled.

“To be precise, it wasn’t removed—it was distributed.”

“Distributed?”

“Using the national fortune’s power, the curse was spread evenly among the entire populace. The result was that everyone would marry fifteen minutes later than they would have in their original fate. This degree of distribution is acceptable.

“But the Imperial Preceptor’s curse is too severe. If it were to be shared with everyone, the consequences would be unthinkable.”

Lu Yang understood now. No wonder the Xia Emperor had refused. I wouldn’t have agreed either.

“So now...” Lu Yang glanced at the still-writhing Imperial Preceptor.

“Let him scream for now. We’ll deal with it once we find a solution.”

“Alright then.”

Letting him be was the only option.

A soul search wasn’t feasible. As the Imperial Preceptor was still mired in the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings, his mind was a muddled wreck, making it impossible to extract anything of value.

Refining him into an artifact spirit was also out of the question. Not only was Fifth Elder incapable of forging a half-immortal treasure, but even if he could, the product would only be a cursed treasure with significantly diminished efficacy.

Yun Zhi reminded Lu Yang, “The yin energy at Incarceration Peak is too dense. Staying here for too long is harmful. You should head back first.” She then turned to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Senior, you performed pretty well as acting sect leader this time. I’m very pleased.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy touched her nose, slightly giddy with smugness. “It’s merely a sect. With my talents, I could even be emperor! Just watch, I’ll catch a few more Transcendent Tribulation cultivators and continue as acting sect leader.”

Yun Zhi informed them, “I’ll be heading to the hideout the Black-White Venerable Lord disclosed. According to him, another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator remains in slumber. Only the Imperial Preceptor knows where this cultivator is, but I’ll try to search for clues at the hideout.”

After seeing them off, she summoned the grand-shifu watching over Incarceration Peak.

“Grand-Shifu, this is Great Yu’s second imperial preceptor, Jin Buqun. He’ll be imprisoned here for now. Be cautious; he has condensed an Incipient Dao Fruit, likely one related to karma.”

In the past, the grand-shifu had believed that his mighty Transcendent Tribulation cultivation made him more than capable of overseeing Incarceration Peak, allowing him to contribute to the sect even after retirement.

Now, he realized he had grossly overestimated himself. Keeping Incarceration Peak in check is too difficult for me.

“Don’t worry, Grand-Shifu. He’s trapped in the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings. He’s barely able to keep himself alive, let alone break out of prison.”

To reassure him further, Yun Zhi set up an additional array over the Imperial Preceptor’s cell before departing for the secret domain where the Imperial Preceptor’s faction lurked.

~~~

Once Lu Yang was away from Incarceration Peak, he felt the weight on his shoulders lighten considerably.

The celebration has concluded without a hitch, the Heavenly Court Creed’s reputation has been built, Great Yu’s Imperial Preceptor and gang have been captured, and the vouchers for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s two-month stint as acting sect leader have expired.

Time to cultivate!

~~~

Three months passed.

Lu Yang sat cross-legged, the Qingfeng Sword and Mingyue Sword hovering at his sides and emanating faint sword qi. His Unbeatable Golden Core rotated steadily, absorbing spirit energy until a vortex formed in his dantian, spinning faster and faster.

Two fingers pointing toward the sky, he uttered softly, “Break!” With that, his aura gushed out like an unstoppable deluge.

The Qingfeng Sword and Mingyue Sword collided, their sword qi intertwining and carving fresh marks into the earth. The sword qi was fiercer and sharper than ever, as if nothing could hold them back.

“Advanced Golden Core Stage...”

It had been two years since he joined the sect.

Lu Yang rose with a smile, sensing the changes in him. The current him could effortlessly defeat the him three months ago.

For three months, he dedicated himself to cultivation without stepping out of the sect, even when Meng Jingzhou came looking for him. After the celebration, his fame soared. Everyone knew of Lu Yang from the Dao-Seeking Sect, the number one Intermediate Golden Core cultivator who had fought the Heavenly Court Creed’s young creed leader to a draw. Some had even disregarded his status as the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple and came knocking to propose marriage, a testament to their strong resolve.

There was another reason Lu Yang hadn’t left the sect. If I go out and run into another Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, wouldn’t the Immortal Fairy become acting sect leader again?

The looting of the Great Yu cultivators’ inheritance was still proceeding methodically. Yun Zhi had first raided their hideout and hauled back everything of value. After that, the major sects began their operations, with two or three sects teaming up to search for a single Great Yu cultivator’s stash.

The Dao-Seeking Sect dispatched First Elder to lead the excavation of the Black-White Venerable Lord’s hoard. As the Black-White Venerable Lord was a powerhouse at the Advanced Transcendent Tribulation Stage, his treasures were innumerable, dazzling Lu Yang until his head spun.

A few days ago, Lu Yang received word that after three grueling months of enduring the Seven Calamities and Eight Sufferings, the Imperial Preceptor had finally succumbed—his soul disintegrated, meeting a wretched and tragic end.

Chapter 508: Theoretically Speaking, I’m Now a Nascent Soul Cultivator

“Congratulations! Advanced Golden Core Stage at last!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clapped enthusiastically, her face crinkling with delight. “Your cultivation speed is not bad, just a tad slower than mine. I’d say you’re keeping pace with the likes of the Nine-Layers Immortal and Qilin Immortal.”

Cultivation speed wasn’t the most critical factor in immortal ascension, but it was a telling indicator of one’s potential.

“Seeing you cultivate so diligently reminds me of how the Nine-Layers Immortal and the others used to cultivate in a frenzy, as if their buttocks were on fire. Now that was dedication.”

Lu Yang nodded. Competition in the ancient era was intense. Falling a step behind meant falling behind in everything. Their tireless cultivation was simply a reflection of the harsh environment then.

Nowadays, although it’s said that the Great Era is upon us, with numerous talents emerging as in ancient times, the drive for cultivation still falls short. Slackers like Meng Jingzhou frittered their days away and squandered time on pointless missions, thus neglecting their cultivation. Disgraceful.

“It’s a pity. No matter how hard they trained, they never caught up. I kept defeating them despite their higher levels.

“Speaking of which, while they couldn’t beat me, their escape skills improved dramatically. A few times, I nearly couldn’t catch up to them.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, I bet the Nine-Layers Immortal and the others cultivated so desperately just to reach your level and suffer fewer beatings.

“At my current cultivation speed, it’ll take at most half a year for me to reach the Nascent Soul Stage.” Since beginning his cultivation, Lu Yang had never encountered bottlenecks. The Sword Spirit Root emphasized unstoppable momentum, soaring to the heavens in one go and breaking through all barriers.

“Actually, you could consider yourself a Nascent Soul cultivator now,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy said sagely.

“Why?”

“What’s the hallmark of the Nascent Soul Stage?”

Lu Yang had long memorized the answer. “Cultivating a nascent soul within the dantian and manifesting an infant.” This was the cultivation world’s official definition of the Nascent Soul Stage.

Yun Zhi had once cultivated multiple golden cores within her dantian, then chose one to shatter and form a nascent soul while keeping the others intact. By the cultivation world’s standards, she was already considered a Nascent Soul cultivator and no longer a Golden Core cultivator then.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied, “Exactly. I exist as a primordial spirit now. So long as I reside in your dantian, doesn’t that make you a Nascent Soul cultivator? Moreover, you’re capable of challenging opponents beyond your level outside the Dao-Seeking Sect; you possess genuine combat power of the Nascent Soul Stage.

“You’ve got both the hallmarks and power of the Nascent Soul Stage. If you’re not a Nascent Soul cultivator, then who is?”

Lu Yang, “...” freewebnovel.com

I don’t have any objections, but I suspect other Nascent Soul cultivators may disagree.

“Don’t doubt me. This was precisely how the earliest Nascent Soul Stage was defined when ancient forebears first mapped cultivation realms. When our forebears reached the Golden Core Stage but found no other path forward, someone refined a demon beast’s primordial spirit into their dantian. This granted them unrivalled power that could crush any Golden Core cultivator. The ancient forebears named this cultivation realm the Nascent Soul Stage.

“However, this came at a price. Severely shortened lifespans and the incompatibility between demon beasts’ primordial spirits and human bodies easily led to sudden deaths.

“Gradually, someone shattered their golden core and discovered that a tiny figure would dart out. This was their primordial spirit. And thus, the modern Nascent Soul Stage was established.”

Just as the first Golden Core cultivators had used demon cores as a replacement, humanity’s initial exploration of the Nascent Soul Stage also relied on the power of demons. The method of substituting one’s golden core with a demon core still existed today, though the cultivation world called these practitioners “False Core” cultivators.

“So that’s what happened.” Realization hit Lu Yang. For once, the Immortal Fairy has shared legitimate ancient secrets even I won’t get to use.

Suddenly, Lu Yang vaguely heard the noise of fighting in the distance. “That direction...the mountain gates?”

Lu Yang was shocked. Why would there be fighting at the mountain gates? Is someone attacking the Dao-Seeking Sect? Even the Imperial Preceptor wouldn’t dare attempt something so brazen.

“Let’s go see!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly suggested, eager for entertainment.

Descending the mountain, Lu Yang bumped into Meng Jingzhou, who was also heading to investigate.

“What happened?”

“No idea. That’s why I’m going to take a look.”

“Let’s go together.”

“Sure.”

~~~

The fighting sounds grew fiercer, drawing not just the two of them but also crowds of senior disciples making their way to check on the situation at the mountain gates.

The nearer they got, the more violent the sounds became.

Upon reaching the gates, they found multiple Fusion cultivators battling in the sky, their techniques and movements ruthless, swift, and fluid, demonstrating the might of Fusion cultivators.

Lu Yang recognized one of the Fusion cultivators. He was called the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Hey hey hey, what’s going on? I just came back to the sect for a bit. Was camping outside the sect gates to ambush me necessary?” the Taciturn Daoist Priest shouted as he dodged repeatedly. Despite his flustered state, his movements remained nimble, and not a single attack landed on him.

“Who would have nothing better to do than to camp here for you? You walked into the trap yourself!” The other Fusion cultivators coordinated perfectly, their relentless assaults giving the Taciturn Daoist Priest no chance to catch his breath.

“Great Wind, rise!”

A raging hurricane swept through, stirring up boundless clouds of dust and sand. Even the gigantic boulders on the ground were lifted into the air. The tornado of debris barreled toward the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest flicked out his horsetail whisk, slicing through the sandstorm.

“Then why are you here at my Dao-Seeking Sect?”

“We came to propose marriage to your disciple, Lu Yang. But since we happened to see you at the gates, this esteemed one feels that the marriage proposal is no longer important. It can wait until we beat you up.”

The other Fusion cultivators nodded, thinking the same way.

Lu Yang pieced it together. My shifu finally returned to the sect, only to encounter the marriage proposal delegation. The moment they saw him, their anger flared, prompting them to attack him together.

How should I say this? I have absolutely no intention of helping Shifu.

The other senior disciples observing the battle similarly showed no inclination to intervene. Perhaps battles between Fusion cultivators were a rare sight—everyone was too absorbed in studying this rare display to step in.

Tao Yaoye, in particular, studied with rapt attention. This is a bona fide combat between Fusion cultivators, far more vicious than ordinary battles. It’s perfect material for my Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

At the sect’s celebration, she had showcased the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage’s applications, receiving numerous good reviews. After the celebration concluded, she began aggressive promotion under the sect’s support, and it had already started to take shape.

The target audience was mortals and low-level cultivators. The admission fees were affordable, but when tallied up, it raked in more money than the royalties from Lu Yang’s flying carriage patent.

Among the younger generation, Meng Jingzhou was the wealthiest in spirit stones, followed by Tao Yaoye, with Lu Yang only coming in third. As Man Gu was the Barbarian Tribe’s treasured scion, his considerable pocket money secured him fourth position. In fifth place was Li Haoran, though this was temporary. Once he married Su Yiren and shared marital assets with her, his financial ranking would skyrocket to second place.

Finally, the Taciturn Daoist Priest seized an opening and transformed into a streak of sword light, flying into the sect. The Fusion cultivators here to propose marriage could only give up on their pursuit and depart with disappointment.

Covered in dust and thoroughly disheveled, he struggled to steady his breathing. I was just passing by the sect and thought I’d visit! Who could have imagined enemies waiting at the sect’s entrance?

“Shifu, what grudge do they hold against you?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“Hard to say.”

“Hard to say.”

“Too many enemies. I’ve lost track.”

Chapter 509: The Taciturn Daoist Priest Returns to the Sect

Lu Yang watched with furrowed brows as the Fusion cultivators flew away, his mind restless.

“What’s wrong? Can’t bear to see them leave? Hope they’ll come to propose marriage?” Meng Jingzhou teased with a grin.

Since the celebration ended, a steady stream of marriage proposal delegations had come knocking for Lu Yang, a sight that filled Meng Jingzhou’s heart with envy. Seeing Lu Yang gaze wistfully at the departing procession, Meng Jingzhou couldn’t stop the corners of his mouth from turning upward.

Lu Yang shook his head, voicing his concerns. “I’m worried they’ll realize they can ambush Shifu by proposing marriage to me. If that happens, even more people will come to propose marriage.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Should’ve kept my damn mouth shut.

Lu Yang felt that given his master’s talent for making enemies, it wouldn’t be all that surprising if news came one day that he’d died a sudden death somewhere out in the wild. For a Fusion cultivator to not remember what he’d done to offend people speaks volumes about the problem.

To prevent such incidents, Lu Yang kindly suggested, “Shifu, have you considered writing your will in advance? I’m afraid you won’t have time when you’re about to die.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest gave his little disciple a meaningful look, feeling that Lu Yang’s way with words was beginning to show a hint of the same flair his second disciple had displayed when forming that strange Yin-Yang Golden Core.

“You’ve met your second senior brother?”

“Second Senior Brother? No, isn’t he in the Golden Buddhist Kingdom?” Lu Yang was baffled by the question.

“Never mind.”

A considerable crowd of disciples had gathered to watch the commotion around the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Previously, he had been forced into a decade-long seclusion, never once showing his face. Later, Yun Zhi was deceived by Lu Yang’s schemes and released the Taciturn Daoist Priest to promote the Dao-Seeking Sect through storytelling in the outer world. From then on, the Taciturn Daoist Priest never returned to the sect. freewebnovel.com

Disciples from the previous two cohorts had only heard of this sect leader’s existence, but none had ever seen him in person. Even among Lu Yang’s cohort, only he and Meng Jingzhou had met the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran had never seen him either.

“I heard the sect leader is back. Let me see, let me see!”

“Isn’t the sect leader Yun Zhi?”

“I finally get to see the real sect leader! When I was out on missions and introduced myself as a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect, people would first ask if I was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciple. Only after confirming I wasn’t would they let me in.”

“None of you have seen the sect leader before?”

“You have?”

“Yes.”

“We’re all from the same cohort. Where’d you see him?”

“On a wanted poster.”

The disciples jostled for a better view of what the living, breathing Taciturn Daoist Priest looked like. If outsiders were to witness this scene, they might easily be misled into thinking that the Taciturn Daoist Priest was deeply beloved by his disciples.

“Junior Brother, you’re back.” First Elder arrived belatedly, or rather, waited to show himself after the beating was over.

If even Lu Yang could arrive right away, how could First Elder be any slower?

First Elder recognized the Fusion cultivators who had beaten the Taciturn Daoist Priest. Back when he and the Taciturn Daoist Priest were amateurs at building tombs, they accidentally dug into someone’s ancestral grave. The family mistook them for grave robbers and came down to investigate. With no time to escape, the duo spent the night hiding in a coffin with the old ancestor.

Once the matter came to light, the family hunted everywhere for the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

Since they were in the wrong, First Elder found it inconvenient to step in. Letting the Taciturn Daoist Priest take the beating worked just as well. And the other elders shared the same sentiment.

The Fusion cultivators who had just beaten the Taciturn Daoist Priest earlier were people the Taciturn Daoist Priest and the elders had offended before, so none of the elders found it convenient to step in.

“Just passing by the sect and thought I’d visit,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest lamented. I was just gone for a year, and the acting sect leader position has changed hands four times.

First was Yun Zhi as acting sect leader, then it was Lu Yang for three days, then Yun Zhi again, followed by Lu Yang for two more months, and now it’s Yun Zhi once more. The frequent changes in the sect’s leadership are proof of how chaotic the management within the sect is.

“I thought you’d provoked enemies again and came back to hide,” First Elder shot back.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest didn’t like the sound of that. “What are you saying! I’ve always taken responsibility for my own actions. When have I ever run away?”

First Elder spoke in a slow, unfriendly tone. “Then what about the time you pretended to be a woman and wrote love letters to Old Four, making him lovestruck and giggle like he had lost his soul? And after it was exposed, why did you shove those unfinished love letters under my pillow?”

In his youth, Fourth Elder had a pen pal named Ye Qianqian. The two had never met in person and communicated solely through letters. In her letters, Ye Qianqian stated she had witnessed Fourth Elder casually chatting and smiling as he slew demonic cultivators with his brush and ink. This sight captivated her, prompting her to write to him.

Charmed by Ye Qianqian’s sweet words, graceful handwriting, and the subtle affection woven between the lines, Fourth Elder got hooked in no time.

When Ye Qianqian mentioned that her hometown had been struck by a flood that submerged all the crops, Fourth Elder immediately sent a reply along with some spirit stones.

Unfortunately, even the most meticulous plans could run into accidents. One day, the matter was exposed. Fourth Elder discovered that someone among his senior and junior brothers had been masquerading as Ye Qianqian. Furious, he stormed through the sect, combing through them one by one.

Sensing trouble, the Taciturn Daoist Priest hastily slipped the unfinished letters under First Elder’s pillow.

Unsurprisingly, Fourth Elder got into a brawl with First Elder. It was only afterward that they uncovered the Taciturn Daoist Priest as the true culprit.

“Fourth Senior Brother is a Confucian cultivator who follows the path of a gentleman, rigid and slow-witted. When out in the world, he’s easily duped by women. Rather than let him get tricked by women, I figured I'd better trick him first to keep the benefits within the family—ah, no, I mean, remind him to be more cautious.” This was the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s explanation before his beating.

First Elder shuddered at the memory. Scholars can really be ruthless when they get serious.

“Since you’re back, let’s hold a meeting. I have something to discuss with you.” First Elder summoned the group: Yun Zhi, the eight elders, the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang, Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, Li Haoran, and Qin Yanyan.

Yun Zhi was in the sect. She had watched her master get beaten without the slightest intention of intervening. Her reasoning was sound: “I’m not at the Fusion Stage—I can’t defeat them.” It was clear that she truly didn’t want to lend a hand.

All the members of the Heavenly Court Creed assembled. Everyone looked at each other silently with heavy thoughts weighing on their minds, creating the perfect atmosphere.

In truth, it was inconvenient to speak because Sixth Elder was present.

After listening to First Elder’s recount of the events through their spiritual consciousness, even the Taciturn Daoist Priest, famed for his deception skills, was dumbstruck. “So you guys are behind all the recent fuss about the Heavenly Court Sect lately?”

“It’s us—you included,” First Elder corrected.

“...Let’s not talk about how you conscripted me into the Heavenly Court Creed as a heavenly king protector—well, it’s not like I’m against being a protector—but why name me ‘Growth Heavenly King’ just because I improved the ‘Size At Will’ spell?!”

Grandpa Ba shrugged, making his point with reason. “We had no other choice; you were absent. Besides, our Heavenly Court Creed values democracy. Everyone but you approved this title of yours.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest flew into a rage, veins bulging. “Democracy my ass! Who’s the creed leader—Big Senior Brother or you? I demand a fair judgment!”

“Your eldest disciple.”

“...Growth Heavenly King is a pretty good name.”

Chapter 510: Self-Taught Genius

The Taciturn Daoist Priest sighed. Lu Yang is truly my dear disciple. He could cook up something like the Heavenly Court Creed without anyone teaching him.

Back at the Golden Core Stage, I only sabotaged and scammed fellow Golden Core cultivators. Yet here is Lu Yang, also at the Golden Core Stage, already duping the full spectrum—from Transcendent Tribulation old ancestors and three Great Diabolic Creeds to low-level cultivators and common folk. His ability to manipulate everyone from all walks of life is genuinely astonishing.

Originally, I’d planned to secretly pass down my entire arsenal of deception arts to Lu Yang behind Yun Zhi’s back. But now, it seems unnecessary.

I’m his shifu, yet I can’t pass on my proudest skills—I can’t tell whether it’s fortunate or unfortunate.

“Since I’m a heavenly king protector, it’s only right that I contribute to our creed,” the Taciturn Daoist Priest declared with a strong sense of duty, eager to capitalize on his talents. “I can spread word of our creed in the outside world.”

“No,” Fourth Elder immediately vetoed the proposal. “Your infamy in the cultivation world spreads far and wide. You’re like a rat scurrying through the streets; everyone wants to take a swing at you. Mortals and low-to-mid-level cultivators might not know you, but which high-level cultivator doesn’t recognize you?

“When you were promoting our sect in the outside world, your main audience was mortals and low-to-mid-level cultivators. But the Heavenly Court Creed’s goal is to deceive our enemies hiding in the dark, all of whom are high-level cultivators. If we have you as the face of our publicity, it would only undermine our credibility.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, “...”

Setting aside those heavily subjective and objective assessments, I have to admit Old Four has a point.

Eighth Elder added, “In my opinion, the Heavenly Court Creed should refrain from public appearances for now. Frequent visibility would make others suspect us of putting on an act. The superior strategy is to remain unseen and let our enemies rely on scraps of information to speculate and imagine how formidable our Heavenly Court Creed is.”

The less information they have, the more our enemies’ imaginations will run wild. Moreover, the Heavenly Court Creed’s strength is undeniable. Even if we don’t act, people would misinterpret it as us operating some grand scheme in the dark. The ones sweating will be our foes. As the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s first mentor, Eighth Elder had his unique philosophy on the art of deception.

While Lu Yang listened to the elders debate, he was struggling to keep the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s increasingly inflated ambitions in check within his mental space.

“Hey hey! Your shifu’s back! Quick, tell him to hand over the position of sect leader to me!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy excitedly smacked the edge of her bed, urging Lu Yang to reveal his treacherous ambitions and usurp power.

“Immortal Fairy, that would be difficult.”

“What’s difficult about it? Your shifu doesn’t look like he wants to be sect leader.”

“The issue doesn’t lie with my shifu, but with Big Senior Sister. She’s held the sect’s reins for eleven years and has long been intoxicated by authority, unwilling to let go of power so easily. Letting you serve as acting sect leader twice was merely her way of taking a break. Even if my shifu steps down, she’s the most likely successor.”

“Then what do we do?”

“As long as you defeat Big Senior Sister, the sect leader position is ours for the taking!” Lu Yang had no choice but to intervene. He was worried that if he actually dared suggest becoming the sect leader, his shifu might really hand the position over without hesitation.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded, finding Lu Yang’s reasoning sound. “No need to rush this matter. It’s not that I fear Lass Yun, but because I think she’s doing a pretty good job for now. Once I’ve recovered my power and returned to my peak, I’ll contend for the position of sect leader!”

“You are amazingly shrewd, far-sighted, and tenacious, Immortal Fairy. Your talents will undoubtedly shine brightly in the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“I think so too,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy concurred.

The Heavenly Court Creed’s impromptu meeting concluded swiftly. Frankly, there wasn’t much to discuss beyond informing the Taciturn Daoist Priest, who was already a member but didn’t know it himself.

After the meeting, the Taciturn Daoist Priest called Lu Yang. “Little Yang, stay a while.”

“Shifu, is something the matter?”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest placed his horsetail whisk on his arm and stroked his white beard. “It’s nothing major. I just felt like I’ve never properly taught you since taking you as my disciple. Now’s a good chance to teach you how to comprehend the Sword Dao.”

Lu Yang was overjoyed. While many in the sect were familiar with sword spells, few were truly proficient. Lu Yang’s sword moves were rudimentary, and his comprehension of the Sword Dao had essentially relied on his innate talent.

Despite being master and disciple for two years and both bearing Sword Spirit Roots, formal lessons only began now.

“Show me your swords.”

Lu Yang drew the Qingfeng Sword and the Mingyue Sword.

“You keep your swords in your identity jade tablet?”

“Is there a problem?” Lu Yang was bewildered. He had seen other cultivators do the same. Is a sword cultivator supposed to maintain close contact with his sword and tend to it meticulously to make it easier to wield in battle?

“There’s a big problem. At your age, I often faced ambushes. To counter them, I always kept my sword on me. If I’d stowed it away like you do, wouldn’t that have made me react slower in times of danger?”

“Was Great Xia’s public order that terrible in your youth?” Lu Yang was stunned. Since entering the world of cultivation, he had never been ambushed. I didn’t expect things to be so chaotic in Great Xia two thousand years ago.

“Although others say Great Xia’s public order was just as great as it is now, based on personal experience, it was absolute chaos then!”

“Did you report the ambushes to the authorities then?”

“It was too complicated. I usually didn’t report to the authorities.”

Lu Yang could understand him. Such is the darkness of officialdom.

“How was it complicated?”

“Mainly because I’d ambushed them first. Taking it to the authorities wouldn’t do anything good for us both.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest took the sword. Both blades slid halfway from their sheaths, and the gleaming light happened to reflect directly into his eyes.

He lavished praise on the two swords. “Good swords! One was gifted by Little Yun, who added seals to it for you, and the other was carefully forged by Old Five.”

His horsetail whisk had been crafted by Fifth Elder. Though it appeared to be a nondescript horsetail whisk, it actually encompassed countless sword qi to catch opponents off guard.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest reluctantly returned the swords to Lu Yang. Little Yun is really biased. No matter how many times I’d begged for the Qingfeng Sword, she refused to give it to me.

“Perform your sword moves. Let’s assess your progress.”

“Yes.”

The sword’s hilt aligned with his chest, sword qi swirling along the blade like a coiling dragon wrapped around a pillar, its momentum like a soaring rainbow.

With a loud cry, Lu Yang rotated his wrists, and his swords moved like a startled swan—swift, fierce, and unstoppable.

Breaking Word Mantra, Pointing Word Mantra, Flicking Word Mantra... Foundational sword moves came alive in Lu Yang’s hands, connecting seamlessly into one fluid motion.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest, “...”

...Is this really a level one can achieve through self-study?

He felt the results couldn’t have been better even under his personal tutelage.

Lu Yang sheathed his swords and placed the Qingfeng Sword vertically behind his back before bowing slightly to the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

“Shifu, is there anything in my sword moves you think needs improving?”

Lu Yang was on tenterhooks. I’d taught myself all my sword moves. Although I’m satisfied with them, maybe it’s riddled with flaws in Shifu’s eyes.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest paused for a moment before saying earnestly, “Next time, remember to leave a few flaws in your sword moves for me to point out.”

Chapter 511: Sword Opens Heaven Gates and Person and Sword as One

As a genius sword and spell cultivator, Lu Yang’s talents were beyond question.

In spells, his talents rivaled Yun Zhi’s.

In swordsmanship, he vaguely showed signs of surpassing the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest remarked, “Initially, I planned to teach you the proper execution of fundamental sword moves, but it seems that’s no longer necessary.” Fundamental sword moves formed the bedrock of swordsmanship. The slightest deviation in angle could drastically alter the resultant power.

“The sword techniques I’ve mastered all demand a higher cultivation than yours, so I can’t teach you yet. ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords’ requires immense spirit energy reserves. While yours are exceptional for the Golden Core Stage and surpass even most Nascent Soul cultivators’, they still fall short of that threshold. When you reach the Nascent Soul Stage, I’ll be able to impart this technique to you.”

Traditionally a sword move for the Divine Transfiguration Stage, One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords unleashed a single sword that multiplied into ten thousand blades, blotting out the sky like a legion. It was a technique every sword cultivator dreamed of mastering.
