However, considering Lu Yang’s talent in the Sword Dao and his immense spirit energy reserves, performing it at the Nascent Soul Stage was possible for him.

“You’ve also mastered flying on swords by yourself.

“It’s too early for you to learn ‘No Sword Beats A Sword’ now. You could be easily led astray. Besides, with your Qingfeng Sword, there’s no way ‘no sword’ can beat ‘a sword.’

“The baseline for ‘Ten Thousand Swords Return to One’ is the Divine Transfiguration Stage. You’re nowhere close.

“As for my ultimate move, ‘Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate,’ it’s even harder. Don’t dream of executing it if you’re not at the Fusion Stage.”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest listed various sword moves that were unsuitable for Lu Yang to learn now.

“Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate? Did you comprehend that yourself, Shifu?” Lu Yang had never heard of such a move.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest sighed as he shook his head. “Forced by circumstances; not my wish.”

It’s an implicit confirmation. Lu Yang gazed at the Taciturn Daoist Priest with envy.

The techniques of sword cultivators were actually few. Most of them, like ‘Person and Sword as One’ and ‘One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords,’ were passed down from ancient times. Sword cultivators studied these moves faithfully. However, the same sword move could manifest with wildly different power based on one’s comprehension.

Those who created their own sword moves were exceedingly rare. The only other creator he knew was the Sword Tower’s Supreme Lord.

That said, numerous sword styles existed in the cultivation world, including Falling Rain, Hundred Flowers, Dawnbreaker, and Carefree. Some sword cultivators' naming sense wasn’t up to standard, and many sword spells had the same name. Lu Yang knew at least four types of “Carefree Sword Spells.”

“Forced by circumstances?” When Shifu created this move, he was likely already a Fusion cultivator. There should have been few who could have rivalled him.

Could it be that Shifu provoked too many enemies? And they ambushed him? Besieged by a hundred peers, it would be hard to escape even for someone as strong as Shifu. Faced with the relentless assaults, he was battered and on the verge of death, but he attained enlightenment at this life-and-death moment and comprehended the sword strike that saw through life and death—Sword Opens Heaven Gates!

The moment this sword appeared, it even tore open a rift in the heavens!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest stroked his white beard. “That happened over a thousand years ago. Back then, I did something wrong, and your grand-shifu confined me to Heaven Gate’s Peak for a decade. You know me, I’m a secular cultivator. How could I tolerate not going out?

“But I had no other choice. Your grand-shifu’s cultivation was higher than mine, and he specialized in sealing spells. He sealed the entire mountain peak. I knew it couldn’t go on like this. Wouldn’t I really have to be locked away for ten years?

“In that moment, I entered an enlightened state and sat in meditation on the spot. My body turned into a crucible that harbored every comprehension of the Sword Dao I had—refining, transforming, tempering, and polishing them until I unleashed a sword strike that split open the seal on Heaven’s Gate Peak!

“Thus, I named this move ‘Sword Opens Heaven’s Gate.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Shifu...why is this process nothing like what I’d envisioned?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy chimed in. “Speaking of sword cultivators, I encountered one before becoming an immortal. He was terrifyingly powerful, a strong adversary, and truly the most formidable combatant of his cultivation realm.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s story of comprehending sword moves reminded her of this past event.

“Please share the details, Immortal Fairy.” Lu Yang’s interest was piqued when he heard it involved someone of his ilk. It’s rare to hear about ancient sword cultivators.

“That sword cultivator was called Liu Ningxuan. Peerless in both qin and sword, his honorific title was Qin Sword Venerable Lord. You know the move ‘Person and Sword as One,’ don’t you? He invented it.”

Lu Yang’s eyes widened. Person and Sword as One was a renowned sword technique that amplified one’s combat power in the shortest time possible. It was said that this move had been passed down from ancient times, though no one knew from whom it had originated. He didn’t expect to hear the answer from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“That fellow Liu Ningxuan could fight pretty well. Like all sword cultivators, his faith was the sword in his hand. Wielding it changed his entire essence, qi, and spirit; it was especially intimidating. With his sword in hand, he pierced dimensions, shattered voids, and slashed through time.”

Lu Yang inhaled sharply. These feats sound powerful, far from what I can achieve now. This senior called Liu Ningxuan must have also been the cream of the crop among ancient sword cultivators, or even the number one sword cultivator of ancient times.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy continued, “When he unleashed his sword, even someone as strong as me would rather retreat than face it head-on. That said, he still couldn’t match me in the end and fell by my hand.”

“You’re amazing, Immortal Fairy! How exactly did this Qin Sword Venerable Lord lose?”

“That battle was truly perilous. Our intense combat threatened to destroy heaven and earth and shook multiple stars. Perhaps he sensed a life-and-death threat from me, and under such tremendous pressure, he somehow gained a higher comprehension of the Sword Dao.

“He realized he couldn’t defeat me with his original techniques and needed innovation. Building upon his comprehension of the Sword Dao mid-battle, he elevated ‘Person and Sword as One’ to an unprecedented realm. Merging with his sword, he transformed into an immortal sword, his aura exploding like the primordial separation of heaven and earth.”

Lu Yang listened with twinkling eyes, immersed in imagining this cosmic-level battle, and eagerly asked, “What happened next?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy scratched her head with a troubled expression. “Next? There was no ‘next.’ After becoming one with the sword, he found the fusion too complete for him to transform back.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Immortal Fairy, have you never encountered any normal opponents during your path to immortal ascension?

Right then, the Taciturn Daoist Priest slapped his forehead as he remembered something, interrupting Lu Yang’s thoughts about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s glorious history.

“I’ve just remembered! There’s one move I can teach you.”

“Which one?”

“Person and Sword as One! This is a signature move passed down from ancient times. It can unleash incredible power instantly, making it perfect for overcoming stronger opponents or mounting a last-ditch counterattack...”

“Not learning it,” Lu Yang refused decisively.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest was puzzled, unable to understand why his youngest disciple would reject it so firmly and abruptly. Since he’s unwilling to learn Person and Sword as One, it seems there aren't any other sword moves he can learn at his cultivation stage now.

“Fine then, I’ll teach you how to comprehend the Sword Dao.”

Chapter 512: The Purpose of Comprehending the Sword Dao

“For your sword techniques to possess such power, it shows you already have some preliminary understanding of the Sword Dao. But to better comprehend the Sword Dao, you must first understand its fundamental essence.

“The so-called Sword Dao is the Great Dao’s supreme principles embodied within the sword. As for what those principles are, we’ll talk about that later.

“Have you ever wondered why your spirit root is called a Sword Spirit Root? Since a Sword Spirit Root exists, could there also be Saber Spirit Roots, Spear Spirit Roots, Staff Spirit Roots—or simply, weapon spirit roots?”

Lu Yang shook his head. The question had never crossed his mind. He simply felt that wielding the sword came naturally to him, as if he was born to be fated with the sword.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest continued, “The Sword Spirit Root is a mutation of the Metal Spirit Root. Metal Spirit Roots excel in the manipulation of minerals and offensive power, while the Sword Spirit Root abandons mineral manipulation and evolves its offensive power to the limit.

“Your Sword Spirit Root doesn’t signify that you’re innately fated with swords, but rather that you possess the most formidable offensive method—weapons. And among all weapons, the sword is the best vessel. Only by using the sword can you unleash your spirit root’s full potential.”

Lu Yang was puzzled. “But the spells I cast seem as powerful as my sword techniques.” If the Sword Spirit Root can really maximize one’s offensive power, shouldn’t the Sword Dao be the strongest?

Noticing Lu Yang’s perplexed expression, the Taciturn Daoist Priest paused for a moment before replying, “This proves an ancient saying.”

“What ancient saying?”

“Geniuses defy reason. All experience comes from those who came before, but these people haven’t seen it all. For example, none of them has ever encountered someone like you.

“Besides, if the Sword Spirit Root is truly the most powerful, why did none of the Four Ancient Immortals use swords? Why hasn’t anyone with a Sword Spirit Root become an immortal?”

Lu Yang refuted inwardly, Actually, there was one such person who could have become an immortal. It’s just that their mastery of Person and Sword as One was so perfect that he strangled that possibility with his own hands.

To be deemed a “strong adversary” by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage speaks volumes about his prowess. The last person regarded as a “strong adversary” was that peerless genius who turned “Law Follows Words” into a passive ability.

Moreover, it’s not like immortals didn’t use swords. The Qilin Immortal frequently used swords. My Mingyue Sword had been reforged from one of his swords.

“Comprehending the Sword Dao requires a clear goal. Let me ask you, Little Yang, what’s your purpose in comprehending the Sword Dao?”

This question stumped Lu Yang for a long while. Ever since he began cultivating and using the sword, he had never considered his purpose. He had simply drifted along, cultivating without direction.

Slowly closing his eyes, he immersed himself in his ocean of memories, recalling the events that had transpired since he joined the sect.

After joining the sect, I made many friends. Although we often sabotaged and scammed each other, those were just jokes between friends. When I encountered problems, I’d look for my senior brothers and sisters for help, and they readily lent me a hand. Big Senior Sister mentored me, assisting me in building a solid foundation. She may be reticent, but I can feel her concern toward me...

When Lu Yang’s eyes reopened, they met the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s gaze with unwavering certainty as he voiced the answer in his heart.

“To protect!”

I want to protect everything beautiful in this world!

The Taciturn Daoist Priest thwacked Lu Yang’s head.

“Protect my ass! Who needs your protection—me or Little Yun?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Upon further thought, that is true. Meng Jingzhou and the others are peerless prodigies, while my senior brothers and sisters are stronger than me. I have to count on their backing when I’m outside. As for Big Senior Sister, nothing needs to be said. And there’s Shifu too. His enemies are far beyond me. It doesn’t seem like he needs protection either?

“Stop thinking about all this nonsense all day long! Didn’t you hear me? The sword is the most offensive weapon—the goal of comprehending the Sword Dao is naturally pursuing the ultimate offense!”

Lu Yang nodded docilely, admitting he had overthought.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest barked, “A sword cultivator needs to be pure! The purer your pursuit, the better your comprehension of the Sword Dao!

“The axiom ‘One Sword Breaks All Spells’ hints at the method of comprehending the Sword Dao!

“Also, think about your Breaking Word Mantra! Why is it the most powerful among all word mantras? Isn’t it because the character for ‘break’ represents the Sword Dao’s purpose?!”

As Lu Yang reflected on his journey of comprehending the Sword Dao, he realized it was indeed as his master had said. In the past, his focus had been singular, simply thinking about how to grow stronger through the Sword Dao—nothing more.

Unknowingly, this had aligned him with the highest method of comprehending the Sword Dao.

Although it seemed accidental, part of him had suspected this, having inferred it from the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s reactions. When I was comprehending the Sword Dao, she didn’t point out my errors and correct my method, which meant that I was doing it the right way.

What Lu Yang didn’t know was that while he was listening attentively to the lesson, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy was equally attentive, nodding frequently and receiving huge gains herself.

“So that’s what the Sword Dao is about,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy murmured in realization. Sword cultivators were rare in the ancient era. The Qin Sword Venerable Lord was the only sword cultivator I encountered.

My golden finger cheat is fantastic! Since my resurrection, I’ve been lounging around all day with nothing to do. I also get to witness all kinds of interesting matters in the modern cultivation world by following my golden finger around. Not only does my golden finger help with handling my tasks, but more importantly, whenever he obtains fortuitous opportunities, I’d benefit from them too.

A win-win arrangement indeed.

With his shifu’s guidance, Lu Yang felt he had gained an epiphany. The veil that had shrouded his cultivation until now was lifted, leaving his mind brilliantly illuminated. Sitting in the lotus position, he attempted to follow the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s instructions in comprehending the Sword Dao.

“Pursue the ultimate offense...”

Sensing the aura of Sword Dao emanating from Lu Yang’s meditation, the Taciturn Daoist Priest nodded slightly. This little disciple’s comprehension ability never ceases to amaze me.

Since that’s the case, it’s about time I take my leave.

He had originally intended to stop by the sect for a brief visit. His cultivation path was in the outer world, amidst the mundane realm. Since I’ve imparted the quintessential aspects of the Sword Dao to Lu Yang, this trip can be considered fulfilling.

With a flick of his horsetail whisk, he strode through the sect gates. freewebnovel.com

The moment he stepped outside, he saw countless marriage proposal processions blocking the mountain gates, their members’ lips curling into eerie grins of excitement at the sight of him.

“The intelligence was accurate! This rascal has really returned to the Dao-Seeking Sect!”

“Old Taciturn scoundrel, you’ve finally come out!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s hair stood on end as a barrage of assaults barreled toward him.

“Bodhi Alms Palm!” An emerald hand larger than mountain ranges descended from the sky, its mass beyond measure.

“Heavenly Devil Dissolution Great Spell!” A cultivator wreathed in black energy exploded with vigorous fighting spirit.

“Hundred Solutions to All Martial Arts!”

“Cosmos Creation Array!”

“Thunder Demise!”

BOOM! BOOM! BOOM!

Mountains trembled; space quivered.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest silently retreated into the sect.

My cultivation travels can wait another day.

Chapter 513: Plan to Lure the Tiger From Its Mountain

“Damn it, that old Taciturn scoundrel escaped too quickly!”

“It’s your fault for attacking too early! I told you to wait until he walks out of the Dao-Seeking Sect before making a move! But no, you couldn’t resist striking the moment you saw him. Anyone would run in that situation!”

“I couldn’t help it. Seeing my enemy got me too agitated.”

“Well, what do we do now?”

“I have an idea, but I’m not sure if it’ll work.”

“What is it?”

“Have you forgotten? We’re here to propose marriage...”

~~~

Recalling the barrage of assaults that had nearly rained down on him, the Taciturn Daoist Priest shuddered. If those attacks had landed, I might have lost either a layer of skin or my life, or both.

“Seriously, that bunch of people from the merchant guilds, is this any way to treat a customer? They wouldn’t even sell me insurance!” The Taciturn Daoist Priest fumed. Are they even merchants? What kind of merchant refuses to earn money? I wanted to buy their most expensive insurance coverage!

~~~

“So this is the correct way to comprehend the Sword Dao.” Emerging from his epiphany, Lu Yang felt his understanding of the Sword Dao had elevated to another level. The Young Creed Leader Lu who fought me to a draw three months ago is no longer a match for me!

Opening his eyes, he saw Yun Zhi approaching him with a stack of red, festive envelopes.

“What are these?”

“Invitations from the marriage proposal processions. They wish to enter the Dao-Seeking Sect and discuss matters of marriage with you in person.”

Lu Yang picked one at random. It came from the White Horse Temple, a first-class sect. “...Am I really this popular?” If Meng Jingzhou sees this, he’d probably grind his molars to dust from envy.

“Your popularity is one factor. The main reason is they want to enter the search to search for Shifu.”

“Shifu hasn’t left yet?” Lu Yang was surprised. Given Shifu’s restless nature and inability to sit still, I had assumed he’d depart immediately after teaching me.

Then again, I can’t exactly say he’s unable to sit still. The old man has obediently completed every prison sentence and sat still in his cell until he was released.

“He originally wanted to leave but was blocked at the gates.”

Truth be told, Lu Yang found this development utterly unsurprising. If anything, he felt it was only natural. From what I know, information on Shifu’s whereabouts commands astronomical prices on the black market—assuming it’s even available at all. The slightest hint of his location would be snapped up instantly, a testament to his popularity.

In the same logic, news of Shifu’s return to the sect would spread like wildfire. Furthermore, all his enemies are at the Fusion cultivator, each capable of flying at terrifying speeds. If some specialize in spatial spells, they could come even faster.

Perhaps “protection” as a purpose for comprehending the Sword Dao isn’t entirely impossible.

Others don’t need protection—I just need to protect myself.

“Then what should we do?” Faced with the pile of invitations, Lu Yang could feel a headache coming. They are here to propose marriage. Chasing them away will reflect poorly on the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“Two options,” Yun Zhi analyzed as she set down the invitations. “First, we quickly grant them entry to the sect. Once they find Shifu, their goal is achieved.”

Lu Yang shook his head. This definitely won’t work. “And the second?”

“Hand Shifu over.”

Lu Yang, “...”

The second option is worse than the first one. “Isn’t Shifu adept at transformation spells? Can’t he turn into someone else and slip out?”

Yun Zhi shook her head, vetoing it. “The White Horse Temple brought their prized treasure, the Demon-Revealing Mirror. It can see through all disguises. Even if it can’t see through Shifu’s disguise, and he successfully slips out, they wouldn’t know that and would continue camping outside the gates to propose marriage to you.”

“Let’s just hand Shifu over,” Lu Yang blurted out.

~~~

Recognizing the extreme risks involved in handing the Taciturn Daoist Priest over, the two first sought out Seventh Elder at Pill Cauldron Peak.

“Junior Niece Yun and Junior Nephew Lu?” Seventh Elder was caught off guard by their visit. It was rare to have both of them looking for him together. “Is anything the matter?”

Since the matter concerned their master, they couldn’t be too straightforward, so Lu Yang chose his words carefully. “If—and I’m just saying if—if a very powerful Fusion cultivator has many enemies at the Fusion Stage and is unlucky to be surrounded, say fifty or sixty of them...

“Is there any pill that could help him survive such a siege?”

Lu Yang didn’t think there was any hope, but to his surprise, Seventh Elder nodded. “Legends speak of a type of pill called ‘Child-Gifting Pill’ in ancient times. You’ve even seen its pill formula before, Junior Nephew Lu. As long as this unlucky Fusion cultivator consumes it and gets pregnant, out of basic human decency, his enemies would probably show him some mercy and not beat him to death.”

Lu Yang pressed on. “...This Fusion cultivator is male. Is there any other way?”

“You can also pray for his corpse to be intact. After tens of thousands of years, the corpse might develop sentience—a form of resurrection. But this is just a legend. Who knows if it’d still be the same him?”

“Do you have anything more practical?”

“I do. This Fusion cultivator in question is definitely a wicked person who has committed all kinds of evil. Report to the authorities to have him arrested. Although he’ll lose his freedom, at least he won’t lose his life.”

Lu Yang and Yun Zhi thought it was a decent solution.

“Hmm, you two are here?” The Taciturn Daoist Priest was looking for Lu Yang and Yun Zhi in the pill-concocting chamber and used the chance to ask Seventh Elder for several bottles of top-grade healing pills. “Perfect timing. I was just about to inform you that I’m leaving.” freewebnovel.com

Lu Yang was astonished. I haven’t even steeled myself to place righteousness before family and betray my shifu, yet he’s already leaving?

“Aren’t you afraid of those people at the gates?”

“Defeating them is out of the question, but I have another plan.”

“Which is?”

“I’ve asked Big Brother to leave the Dao-Seeking Sect and create some commotion in the neighboring province. When those people think I’ve sneaked out of the sect, they’ll rush there in a frenzy, giving me an opening to leave the sect.” The Taciturn Daoist Priest grinned triumphantly. I’ve roamed the world for two thousand years; thinking of catching me is wishful thinking.

~~~

Things went exactly as the Taciturn Daoist Priest had planned. As the big brother of the Dao-Seeking Nine, First Elder didn’t often do things that drew him much hatred; at least, he didn’t have any enemies among the marriage proposal processions this time.

In the neighboring province, First Elder impersonated the Taciturn Daoist Priest to deliver the latest chapter—Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect: Chronicles of Meng Jingzhou. He narrated how Eldest Young Master Meng led a chaste life and devoted himself wholeheartedly to cultivation, avoiding women entirely. Eldest Young Master Meng even went so far as to place a curse on himself that prevented him from seeing females for a long time—truly a feat that earned great respect.

Upon learning that the “Taciturn Daoist Priest” was in the neighboring province, and recalling his skills in concealment, his enemies didn’t suspect anything as they immediately set off.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest seized this opportunity to slip out of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

After he left, Lu Yang sighed. This idea had crossed his mind, and it could be considered the safest approach, but he wasn’t willing to let the Taciturn Daoist Priest use it. For some reason, I couldn’t help but feel like letting Shifu leave the sect safely would go against my conscience.

~~~

A few days later, someone unexpected approached Lu Yang.

“Senior Brother Lu, can you accompany me on a mission?” Tao Yaoye invited him with a gleeful grin.

Chapter 514: My Shifu Is the Taciturn Daoist Priest, so I’m Naturally Also a Secular Cultivator

“A mission?” Lu Yang was nonplussed. Why would she suddenly ask me to join her on a mission?”

“Mmm. Senior Brother Lu, you’re knowledgeable and well-traveled. Taking on sect missions must come naturally to you.

“Do you remember our first mission together? The one where we caught that Painted Skin Demon? If you hadn’t been there to give that demon athlete’s foot, it would likely have gotten away.

“Since then, I’ve gone out to do a few missions alone. Although I completed them, the process was fraught with twists and turns. Luck played a big role. So I thought, maybe I could ask you to go on a mission together this time?”

Lu Yang was stunned. “The sect only requires every disciple to do two missions per year. You’ve already met your quota, right? Besides, with the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage selling so well, even Nascent Soul cultivators aren’t as wealthy as you. You don’t need that many contribution points either. Why take on extra missions?”

Tao Yaoye made a few exaggerated gestures of martial arts poses. “To slay demons and vanquish evil, of course! As disciples of a righteous sect, isn’t eliminating injustice in the world our duty?”

“...Fair point.”

“So, will you come with me, Senior Brother?” Tao Yaoye clasped her hands behind her back, slightly leaning forward with hopeful eyes.

Lu Yang pondered. These three months, I’d focused on breaking through to the Advanced Golden Core Stage, rejecting even Meng Jingzhou’s multiple invitations. If I agree to Junior Sister Tao’s invitation now, wouldn’t it seem like I’m valuing beauty over friendship?

“I’ll go.”

My shifu is the Taciturn Daoist Priest, a secular cultivator—naturally, so am I. As a secular cultivator, it’s unwise to be consistently in seclusion. Gaining experience through missions in the world outside is perfectly normal.

“Wonderful!” Tao Yaoye beamed.

“Wait a moment, let me ask Old Meng whether he wants to come.”

Tao Yaoye smiled knowingly. “I’ve already asked Senior Brother Meng. He’s currently in seclusion and can’t leave.”

“I see. Let’s go then.” Lu Yang was a bit disappointed; he had been hoping to ride the carriage.

Fortunately, the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s schemes had lured away the marriage proposal processions. Otherwise, if Lu Yang stepped out now, he would be swarmed by Fusion experts recommending to him their disciples, daughters, and granddaughters...

~~~

Aboard the flying vessel, Lu Yang inquired about their mission.

“The mission is from Squire Song’s house in Yuanhe County of Qingshui Commandery in Yun Province. They possess a strange painting that emits eerie sounds every midnight. Several passing cultivators had visited Squire Song’s home, but they couldn’t do anything about it. The last cultivator said ordinary cultivators couldn’t handle the painting and suggested that Squire Song seek help from immortal sects.”

“I see.”

~~~

The flying vessel docked in Qingshui Commandery. After disembarking, they rented two horses and headed to Yuanhe County.

Upon arriving in Yuanhe County, they patted the horses, sending them trotting back to their owner.

Tao Yaoye asked, “Shall we head straight to Squire Song’s house?”

Lu Yang shook his head. “No rush. Let’s ask around to gather some information about Squire Song first—his background, character, and household situation.”

“Alright.”

Tao Yaoye had changed drastically since joining the sect. While she was peerlessly beautiful when she first entered the sect, she bore a hint of youthful immaturity. Now eighteen, her graceful poise and playful charm prompted countless passers-by to turn their heads for a second look.

The two carried themselves with an air that set them apart; one glance was enough to tell they weren’t to be trifled with. As a result, no one dared to harass Tao Yaoye along the way.

“Boss, two bowls of wontons please; extra vinegar in mine.” Lu Yang chose a street stall.

“Coming right up!”

The wontons were soon served. Tao Yaoye took a bite and whispered, “Senior Brother, this stall’s wontons taste pretty average.”

“Average is exactly what we’re going for. It’s nearly mealtime, yet hardly anyone’s eating here. That tells you plenty about how average it tastes.”

“Then why are we eating here?”

“It’s because the business is slow that the boss is willing to chat with us...” He turned to the stall owner. “Boss, how long have you been running this stall?”

“It’s been almost thirty years now. Not to brag, but everyone in Yuanhe County knows my wontons. You two aren’t from around here, are you?”

“We’re physicians from the neighboring Panlong Commandery. Someone from the Song Family is sick, so they asked us senior brother and junior sister to take a look. But we’re unfamiliar with the area and haven’t located Squire Song’s residence yet.”

“Oh, you’re looking for Squire Song? His residence is not far from here. Head straight down this road, go past an intersection, then turn left—it’s just down that street.”

Lu Yang naturally knew the Song Residence was nearby. He had deliberately chosen this wonton stall within its vicinity. He kept his head down and took small bites, though a sip of the soup made him wince. So sour.

When Lu Yang stopped talking, the stall owner became chatty instead. “Physicians, who in the Song Family is ill? Squire Song himself?” Bringing over physicians from a neighboring county shows just how grave the illness is—this is worthy of becoming mealtime gossip.

Lu Yang shook his head with a smile. “That I can’t disclose.” He then seemed to have recalled something and casually asked, “Are you familiar with the Song Family?”

“The Song Family rose to prominence only twenty years ago, mainly through Squire Song’s efforts. He’s also quite the figure. He passed the county-level imperial examination and became a xiucai scholar, but never earned any higher titles. His life was uneventful, and he drifted along until middle age. That was when he lost his wife and son, leaving him perpetually frowning in gloom.”

“Out of the blue one day, something clicked, and this fellow began doing business. I’ve no idea how he did it, but his wealth grew by the day, and he became much more spirited. Later, he remarried and had three sons and a daughter.

“Squire Song can be considered a kind person. He has built two learning halls and donated many books.”

Tao Yaoye nodded thoughtfully. From the looks of it, Squire Song seems to be a good person. The only suspicious point is how he suddenly gained an epiphany and started doing business.

But this is probably irrelevant to our current mission.

“Eh, if it isn’t Senior Brother Lu Yang?” someone exclaimed with a trace of delight. The voice was melodious and tender, with a coyness that could melt one’s bones.

Lu Yang turned around in surprise. “Junior Sister Lan Ting?”

Lan Ting had spotted a familiar figure from a distance, though she only confirmed it was Lu Yang after approaching the wonton stall.

Seeing Lan Ting walk over, Tao Yaoye immediately stood up, positioning herself between Lan Ting and Lu Yang. She enthusiastically greeted Lan Ting, “Junior Sister Lan, what brings you here?”

Lan Ting’s beautiful smile made it hard for one to look straight at her. “Ah, Junior Sister Tao! I only saw Senior Brother Lu just now. I’m so sorry.”

“As cultivators, we must keep our ears open in all directions and our eyes sharp on all sides. Junior Sister Lan, you still have some way to go in your cultivation.”

“That’s not quite right, Junior Sister Tao. Cultivators heighten their awareness to watch out for danger. But what danger could I face here?” With a radiant smile, she continued, “Besides, with Senior Brother Lu Yang here, what danger could we possibly run into? Junior Sister Tao, you’re underestimating him.”

Hearing the conversation between the two girls, Lu Yang felt he should say something.

“Boss, another bowl of wontons please.”

Chapter 515: Trust the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to Know Best

“Perfect, one bowl for each of us.” Lu Yang cheerfully pushed the third freshly cooked bowl of wonton to Lan Ting.

Lan Ting cast an inadvertent glance at Tao Yaoye before sitting down quietly with the grace of a noble young lady and picking up a wonton with her chopsticks.

Since Senior Brother Lu Yang chose this stall, it must have its unique charm... It tastes awful.

Lan Ting stared at the bowl in shock. These are the worst wontons I’ve ever eaten.

Objectively, this bowl of wontons was only below average, not the absolute worst. But Lan Ting was born into an ancestral clan, where she was accustomed to gourmet cuisines. After joining the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, though the dishes had become plainer, the flavors remained supreme in the cultivation world. These wontons were already considered below average in the mortal world, so it was only natural that she found them hard to stomach.

The owner grinned inwardly when Lu Yang ordered another bowl. Everyone in Yuanhe County knows my wontons taste terrible. It’s only outsiders who get tricked.

I’ve sold wontons for almost thirty years, and my customers are all outsiders.

Lu Yang was lucky he had plenty of vinegar in his bowl to mask the taste of the wontons. Regardless, he had to finish what he ordered, and the trio forced down all three bowls.

Wiping his mouth, Lu Yang remembered he hadn’t touched on the important matters yet. “By the way, Junior Sister Lan Ting, what brings you here? A mission as well?”

“Mmm. Someone called Squire Song sought help from our Moon Laurel Immortal Palace. He said his family owns a strange painting—it can’t be burned, discarded, or torn. In the middle of the night, it even emits eerie sounds. It’s very dangerous.”

Tao Yaoye chimed in. “Senior Brother Lu and I are on the same mission. He was worried I couldn’t complete it alone, so he accompanied me.”

Lu Yang couldn’t quite make sense of it. What Junior Sister Tao said isn’t exactly wrong, but I can’t help but feel strange.

“It appears that this Squire Song sought aid from both our sects,” he observed.

This was commonplace. Those seeking help were uncertain which immortal sect was reliable, so to play it safe, they would issue the same request to several immortal sects. This was why disciples of the Five Great Immortal Sects frequently crossed paths on missions.

For instance, the Taciturn Daoist Priest and Luo Hongxia had run into each other on the same mission in their youth. Lan Ting had heard the story from her master.

The two were tasked with dispelling a ghost and stayed at an inn for three days, but they simply couldn’t find where the ghost was. In the end, they discovered it under the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s bed. The ghost had been watching the Taciturn Daoist Priest through the floorboards while he slept.

Afterward, the Taciturn Daoist Priest insisted that the ghost split the lodging costs with him.

The ghost cited Great Xia’s laws, arguing that it wasn’t classified as a living being and thus exempted from paying accommodation fees.

The Taciturn Daoist Priest also cited Great Xia’s laws, stating that ghosts held no rights, so cultivators were free to kill them as they pleased.

Then, the ghost obediently paid its share of the lodging fees and was apprehended.

“Senior Brother Lu, Junior Sister Tao, have you investigated Squire Song’s case?”

Tao Yaoye summarized their findings. “This is what Senior Brother Lu Yang and I have uncovered together.”

“Senior Brother Lu Yang is impressive! You’ve only just arrived in Yuanhe County, yet you’ve already uncovered so much. I’m sure Junior Sister Tao has also contributed considerably. I arrived three days earlier, but I’ve only learned a little more than you have.

“Unfortunately, I’m just one person. If Senior Brother Lu Yang helps, I’m sure we could uncover much more.”

Tao Yaoye pretended she didn’t hear the undertone in Lan Ting’s words and asked calmly, “What have you discovered from your investigation, Junior Sister Lan Ting?”

“Squire Song’s fortune took a turning point twenty years ago. At the time, his family had fallen on hard times and barely had any silver left. In a desperate move, he staked everything on his business ventures, only to fail and lose it all. Some saw him walking into the mountains, looking like he intended to end his life. However, half a day later, he emerged from the mountain, no longer dazed and clutching a painting in his arms.

“You all know the rest of the story. Squire Song suddenly gained a shrewd business acumen. Wealth poured in endlessly, and his family lived blissfully.” Lan Ting shot Tao Yaoye a smug glance. Well, what do you think? You two haven’t found this crucial piece of information yet.

After listening to Lan Ting’s account, Tao Yaoye affectionately grasped her hand. “Junior Lan Ting, you’re so amazing! You uncovered so much by yourself. Looks like you’re doing just fine on your own.”

Lan Ting’s face was wreathed in smiles as she linked arms with Tao Yaoye. “What are you saying? As the old saying goes, ‘Many hands make light work.’ It’s a pity Senior Brother Lu Yang came with you. Had he joined me, we would have completed the mission by now.”

Tao Yaoye questioned, “Are you implying you’re better than me, Junior Sister Lan?”

Lan Ting refuted, “Don’t twist my words, Junior Sister Tao. After all, I arrived three days earlier. If Senior Brother Lu Yang had also arrived at the same time I did, given his abilities, wouldn’t he have completed the mission?”

Tao Yaoye admitted, “True. With Senior Brother Lu Yang’s skills, he alone could complete the mission.”

Arm in arm, the two girls wore smiles of reunion, behaving as close as sisters.

Lu Yang didn’t pay attention to their subsequent conversation. He had been mulling over Lan Ting’s findings. “As I thought, the problem lies with the painting.

“Come on, let’s visit Squire Song.”

~~~

On their way to Squire Song’s residence, Lan Ting repeatedly glanced at Lu Yang.

“Junior Sister Lan Ting, is there something on my face?”

Lan Ting smiled. “Nothing at all. I just find you incredible, Senior Brother. You’ve become the sect’s successor at such a young age, even presiding over the sect’s celebration. As far as I know, this is unprecedented in history! I pale so much in comparison.”

“You flatter me. I became acting sect leader purely because of luck.” I’m not being modest. I became the acting sect leader entirely because of my bad luck in resurrecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

Noticing Lan Ting’s dejection, Lu Yang comforted her, “You’re already remarkable, Junior Sister Lan Ting. I saw your match with Old Meng. You were simply too nervous; that wasn’t a true display of your abilities.”

Hearing Lu Yang’s encouragement reignited her smile. “You’re right. I should be more confident. After all, I represent our immortal palace’s Golden Core cultivators.

“Junior Sister Tao and I bonded instantly, and I originally thought we could meet on the arena stage, but alas, things didn’t turn out as I’d hoped, and we never got a chance to spar.”

Tao Yaoye softly muttered, “You’re this fond of combat, Junior Sister Lan? From how gentle you usually act, I thought you were the young lady of a noble family.”

Lu Yang couldn’t shake the feeling that something was off and consulted the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. “Immortal Fairy, don’t you think there’s something odd about how Junior Sister Tao and Junior Sister Lan are acting?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had also been observing them from the mental space for a while now. These two lasses’ mannerisms and tones are indeed unusual. “I can’t help but find this scene familiar... I remember now! The dragon and phoenix prodigies once behaved like this, flattering each other and appearing united. At the time, their goal was to make me take them in as disciples.”

Lu Yang prompted her to continue. “So Junior Sister Tao and Junior Sister Lan are acting like this because...”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared with conviction, “It’s definitely also because they want you to take them in as disciples! After all, you put on a spectacular display of combat prowess at the celebration!”

“Makes sense.”

Chapter 516: Locked-Room Murder Mystery

Lu Yang and his companions arrived at Squire Song’s residence with little trouble.

Lu Yang knocked politely, and a young nobleman opened the door. He was a mortal with no cultivation. His face was deathly pale, and he had dark circles under his eyes, likely from lack of sleep.

“You three are...?” The young nobleman eyed Lu Yang’s group warily.

“The three of us are immortal sect disciples. Squire Song invited us to resolve the matter of the painting.”

“Ah, you are immortal sect disciples!” The young nobleman’s eyes widened. The Song Family had reached out to the immortal sects as a last resort and harbored little hope. I didn’t expect the high and mighty immortal sects to really send people over!

“I am Lu Yang. These are my junior sisters, Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting.”

“Lu Yang?! The same Lu Yang who’s unbeatable among Golden Core cultivators?”

The young nobleman was even more astonished upon hearing Lu Yang’s name. Although he was a mortal, he belonged to a wealthy family and knew a thing or two about the cultivation world. In the past three months, no cultivator’s name had been mentioned more than Lu Yang’s. Along with the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s aggressive promotion, Lu Yang’s reputation had soared to legendary heights.

Although the cultivation world hailed Lu Yang as the number one in the Intermediate Golden Core Stage, the young nobleman had heard it as the number one in the entire Golden Core Stage. To him, the difference was negligible.

“I, Song Tian, pay my respects, Daoists. Please, come in.” Song Tian ushered them inside with utmost courtesy.

After Song Tian’s introduction, Lu Yang learned that Squire Song’s full name was Song Jinju, and Song Tian was his eldest son. Now that Squire Song was advanced in years, Song Tian managed most of the family’s business. It was through his business dealings with cultivator friends that he had heard of Lu Yang’s exploits, confirming the tales in the pingshu storytelling were true.

Aside from Song Tian, Squire Song had two other sons and a daughter. The second son, Song Qing, was a scholar. The third son, Song Qi, idled about all day and was a typical wastrel, leaving Squire Song frustrated and disappointed. The youngest daughter was named Song Lian’er, while his wife, Madam Song, had passed away from illness five years prior.

“Master immortals, please save our Song Family! That painting is too sinister. I haven’t slept for nights. It’s definitely become a demon spirit. We’ve moved houses twice, yet the painting followed us every time!” In Song Tian’s eyes, Lu Yang’s trio was nothing short of saviors. The gloom that had weighed on him these days was lifted instantly.

Escorting the trio to the main hall’s upper seats, he had the maidservants serve tea and summoned the steward to fetch Squire Song from his study. Meanwhile, Song Tian himself went to call the rest of the family over.

The Song Family had been living in fear all this time. Now, with immortal sect disciples intervening, they could finally breathe easy.

Lu Yang picked up his teacup and ignored the scalding heat as he drank half of the tea in one go. Drinking boiling water is nothing. I’d even bathed in it before I began cultivating.

Setting the cup down, he casually said, “There’s a pall of yin energy in the Song Residence.”

Tao Yaoye nodded. “Indeed, and it’s thick enough that a demonic entity is likely hiding in the residence.” That said, judging by the intensity, the yin energy currently posed no threat to the trio.

Their sharp senses picked up the Song Family’s siblings approaching from a distance, chatting while walking.

“Big Brother, no offense, but how many cultivators has our family invited already? Every one of them failed terribly. What makes you so sure they’ll be reliable this time?” The disrespectful tone suggested it was the third son, Song Qi.

“Don’t talk nonsense, Third Brother. This time, Big Brother has invited immortal sect disciples, figures equal in standing to the imperial court! They’re true immortals; dealing with mere evil spirits should be a breeze for them.” From the lecturing cadence, it was probably the second son, Song Qing.

“And didn’t you hear Big Brother? Among the cultivators this time is a Daoist named Lu Yang. Even an incompetent and idle layabout like you must’ve heard the pingshu story, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect. From what I know, the author is the sect leader of an immortal sect and a first-rate expert in this world! His accounts may sound fantastical, but they must be true!

Song Qi reminded him, “Quit showing off your so-called knowledge, Second Brother. You couldn’t even pass the county-level imperial examinations and become a xiucai scholar. Father has raged at you several times, saying all your studying went down the drain. Don’t you remember?”

“You!”

“I just hope they can take the painting away successfully. Ever since Young Master Zhou learned about our family’s situation, he hasn’t dared to meet me freely.” The timid voice could only belong to the youngest daughter, Song Lian’er.

“Little Sister, you still haven’t cut ties with that brat? Have you forgotten what Father told you? That boy is a good-for-nothing, all talk and no substance. It’s not you he fancies but our Song Family’s wealth!

“Listen to your Second Brother’s advice and break up now. If Father finds out you’re still in contact with him, be careful of him breaking your legs!”

“No, Young Master Zhou loves me!”

“Enough, we’re about to meet the Daoists. All of you, behave, especially you, Third Brother. You better not make any wrong move in front of them, else Father won’t spare you!”

Amidst the Song Family’s siblings' chatter, they finally arrived in the main hall.

Lu Yang downed the remaining half of his tea and smacked his lips. Just right for rinsing my mouth; I need to wash away and forget the taste of those wontons.

The Song Family’s interpersonal relationships are a little complicated. After the Song Family siblings arrived, it took Lu Yang only a glance to match them to the voices from before.

They had already met the eldest son, Song Tian.

The person clad in neat Confucian robes, a hand resting at his waist, was the second son, Song Qing.

The short and sulky one was the Third Son, Song Qi.

The girl avoiding eye contact with Lu Yang was the youngest daughter, Song Lian’er.

“Greetings, Daoists.”

Song Tian commanded significant authority in the family. When he instructed his younger siblings to be obedient, none dared to misbehave before Lu Yang, including the third son Song Qi.

“Is Father not back yet?” Song Tian was puzzled. Judging by the time, Father should have arrived by now. freewebnovel.com

Amid Song Tian’s confusion, a figure stumbled into the main hall, gasping for breath. “Young Master, Young Master, bad news!”

Song Tian helped the steward, an ominous feeling arising inside him. “What’s wrong? Where’s Father?”

“The patriarch has passed away!”

“What?!”

The siblings were appalled, and the youngest daughter Song Lian’er nearly fainted on the spot.

Even Lu Yang’s group hadn’t anticipated their host dying before they had even met him.

“Come on, let’s go take a look!” Given that he was the eldest brother, Song Tian swiftly regained his composure and ordered the steward to lead them to the study.

The study door was tightly shut. The steward guided them to a side window with a gaping hole. Through it, they could see Squire Song lying on the ground inside, blood pooling around him, no signs of breathing.”

As the steward led everyone to climb through the windows, he explained, “I went to the study to call for the patriarch, but regardless of how long I shouted, there was no reply. In addition, the doors and windows were locked. This was the patriarch’s habit, which he said gave him a sense of security. I had a bad feeling and broke in through the window. The moment I entered the room, I saw the patriarch lying on the ground.”

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting exchanged contemplative glances.

Locked doors and windows, impossible for outsiders to open, and the victim dead inside—this is a classic locked-room murder mystery.

Lu Yang remained silent, lost in his thoughts.

Chapter 517: Culprit

“Don’t touch anything at the scene!” Song Tian barked, stopping everyone from acting carelessly. If the scene was disturbed, finding the killer would become nearly impossible.

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting carefully examined the study’s layout. It was plainly furnished—two bookshelves, two paintings hung on the wall, and a few yellow talismans to ward off evil. Aside from that, there was only a desk, wooden chairs, a tea table, and a vase on top—nothing out of the ordinary for a study.

The door was tightly shut. According to the steward, the windows had been securely locked from the inside, making it impossible to open them from the outside.

“This is...” The window was tattered, but Tao Yaoye noticed a small hole punctured in one corner.

The steward explained, “Before breaking the window, I poked a hole to check if something had really happened to the patriarch.”

“It was definitely you, Big Brother! You killed Father!” The second son, Song Qing, roared in fury as he seized Song Tian by the collar, his bloodshot eyes like a crazed dog.

Song Tian scowled. He shoved his second younger brother away and angrily rebuked, “What nonsense are you spouting?”

“I’m not spouting nonsense! Don’t think I don’t know—ever since you took over Father's business, it’s been nothing but losses. Not long ago, you made a failed investment and lost a huge sum. You didn’t dare tell Father because you were scared he’d fly into a rage and strip you of managing the family’s business!

“Well, now that you’ve killed Father, you’re the primary successor. The family business is all yours!”

Song Tian exploded in anger. “Rubbish! If we’re talking about motive, yours is far worse! You failed the county-level imperial examinations multiple times. Father was so furious that he broke your leg, even swearing you’d never receive a single bit of the inheritance unless you earned a title! Once, I heard from your drinking buddies that you vowed to kill him!”

“You bribed my friends!”

“Your friends were the ones who sold you out for money.”

Song Lian’er trembled as she pointed at Squire Song’s corpse. “Stop arguing! Look, Father’s eyes are still open. He died with unresolved grievances!”

Sure enough, Squire Song’s head was tilted, his lifeless eyes fixed on the tea table.

The youngest son, Song Qi, followed the gaze and spotted a blue-and-white porcelain vase on the table.

“Blue-and-white porcelain vase...blue-and-white...blue and ‘Qing’... Second Brother Song Qing![1] This is the clue Father left before dying! Second Brother, you killed him!”

Song Qing snapped, “Ridiculous! You’re accusing me over something so baseless? Father’s right hand is extended with one finger—clearly pointing to Big Brother!

“Moreover, if we’re listing motives, everyone here has one!

“Third Brother, you resented Father for cutting off your allowance, which caused you to lose face in front of your worthless friends. Killing Father and inheriting a portion of the family fortune would naturally solve your money problems!

“And Little Sister, Father demanded you cut ties with that Zhou boy, but you refused to comply, continuing to keep in touch with him in secret. With Father dead, no one will stop you from marrying him!”

Song Qing laid bare each sibling’s little secrets—all had a motive for murder.

Tao Yaoye interjected sharply, “When was the last time each of you saw Squire Song?”

Song Qing replied, “I saw Father in the courtyard when I was doing my morning reading. After that, I returned to my room to study. That was five hours ago.”

The third son, Song Qi, stammered, “Two hours ago, I came to the study to take some money. As I left, I ran into Father entering, and he scolded me.”

Song Lian’er answered, “One hour ago, I brought a bowl of tea to Father in the study.”

The steward echoed, “I happened to be outside the door when the young miss brought the tea. I never saw the patriarch again after that.”

Lan Ting nodded. “In that case, Squire Song died less than one hour ago. What were all of you doing an hour ago? Can anyone vouch for you?”

The eldest son, Song Tian, spoke first. “I was at the shop reviewing account books. The clerks can all prove it.”

The second son, Song Qing, said, “I was studying. No one saw me, but I have a habit of reading aloud. The maidservants passing by would probably have heard me.”

The third son, Song Qi, elaborated, “I was drinking and watching dances at the brothel with friends—the Wang Family’s second son, the Kong Family’s eldest son, and people from the Sun Family were with me. But I drank too much and passed out. When I woke up, I was already at home. I have no idea who sent me back.”

Tears welled in Song Lian’er’s eyes. “After delivering the tea to Father, I stayed in my room until Big Brother came looking for me.”

“Can anyone testify for you?”

Her voice dwindled. “No.”

Tao Yaoye keenly sensed something amiss. “Wait, you said you delivered tea to Squire Song. Where’s the teacup?”

There was only a blue-and-white porcelain vase on the tea table—no tea set at all. She couldn’t have waited for Squire Song to finish the tea and take the teacup away.

Song Lian’er faltered, unable to utter a single word.

“Little Sister, say something!” The third son, Song Qi, urged, sweat beading on his brow.

Finally, Song Lian’er steeled her resolve. “The steward said there’s no rift between father and daughter that can’t be reconciled. He encouraged me to speak to Father about Young Master Zhou. I brought tea for Father to ask for his approval of my relationship with Young Master Zhou, but he lost his temper immediately and threw the cup to the floor. The steward cleaned it up. After that, I went back to my room and cried the whole time.”

Song Tian frowned at the steward with a trace of reproach. “If that’s the case, why didn’t you mention this, Steward? Moreover, you should’ve known that based on Father’s attitude, he would never have consented to Little Sister’s matter!”

The steward met Song Tian’s gaze briefly, then flinched away.

“Look into my eyes! Speak, what exactly are you plotting?!” Song Tian demanded loudly.

Seeing everyone’s hostile gazes on him, the steward sighed, knowing there was no escaping this. “Truth is, the young miss’s beloved is my illegitimate son, so I had hoped to bring them together and make their relationship work, but I didn’t expect the patriarch to oppose it so vehemently.”

Song Lian’er stared at the steward blankly, caught off guard by the relationship between the steward and Young Master Zhou. So all this time, his words of encouragement weren’t about supporting me to pursue my love and happiness? Her gaze grew vacant; something inside her heart seemed to have shattered.

Tao Yaoye murmured, “That is to say, it’s most likely that Song Lian’er and the steward worked together. The steward probably shot a poisoned ice needle through the window and killed Squire Song. Then, under the pretense of inspection, he pierced the paper window to cover up the needle hole.”

Lan Ting shook her head and offered her insight. “If that was true, how could the steward guarantee that the Eldest Young Master would send him to find Squire Song? Keep in mind, the steward didn’t know we were coming.

“In my opinion, it could have been the second son, Song Qing. He claimed he was studying in his room, but he could easily fake an alibi by purchasing a recording orb from the merchant guilds that continuously plays his voice!”

The two debated softly, though it led nowhere. Finally, both turned to Lu Yang.

“Senior Brother Lu, who do you think is the culprit?”

Lu Yang didn’t answer. Walking over silently, he crouched beside Squire Song and took out a Soul-Restoration Pill. He had bought it from the Great Mission Hall out of concern for potential mishaps during his journey to Wilderness Province, but he never got to use it.

As the pill dissolved in Squire Song’s mouth, he gradually stirred awake, though his expression was dazed.

Lu Yang explained, “Squire Song isn’t dead; his soul was extracted. I used the Soul-Restoration Pill to pull his soul back.”

As someone who had his body frequently taken over, Lu Yang was far more experienced than his two junior sisters in matters of souls.

“Squire Song, the three of us are from immortal sects. Who extracted your soul?”

Though disoriented, Squire Song’s gaze grew firm at Lu Yang’s words. “It was the painting.”

Lu Yang turned to the others. “See? We’ve found our culprit.”

The Song siblings, “...”

The steward, “...”

Chapter 518: The Unbeatable Golden Core’s Combat Method

After Squire Song was revived, he couldn’t shake the feeling that the atmosphere at home had turned peculiar. I remember the family being harmonious before my “death.” I was dead for less than an hour, and there’s already a subtle air of hostility among my children?

Especially my youngest daughter. She’s kneeling on the floor and bawling with her hands covering her face. Is she mourning my death? How filial.

It’s a pity I would never allow her to marry that Zhou brat, no matter what. After all, they’re siblings by blood.

Squire Song decided to set aside his family issues for the time being. The most important thing right now is to deal with the matter of the painting.

His appearance was ghastly, his face and clothes stained with blood. This was the result of his bodily functions failing and causing him to cough up blood when his soul was ripped away.

“Many thanks for saving my life, Daoists!”

“You’re too polite, Squire Song. May we know what’s going on with the painting?”

With a heavy sigh, Squire Song sank into a chair and began his tale. “Twenty years ago, after failed business ventures, I wanted to commit suicide by jumping from a cliff. Unexpectedly, a branch caught me mid-fall, saving my life. Beneath me jutted a stone ledge. I landed there and found a cave.

“Something in its depths called to me. Unafraid of death then, I followed the voice and discovered it was a talking painting. It claimed it could assist me in business and make me a tycoon, so I brought it out of the cave.

“With the painting’s aid, doing business came effortlessly to me. A few successful investments made me the county’s number one magnate. It was also how I married, had children, and enjoyed a blissful family life.”

At this point in Squire Song’s story, Lu Yang and his companions glanced silently at the Song siblings and the steward.

“Go on?”

Squire Song continued, “Over the past few months, the painting has demanded my life every night. Terrified, I tried drowning it and burning it, but nothing worked! Even when I threw it into the wilderness, it would reappear in my home by dawn!”

His eyes were stricken with fear and panic. The painting had tormented him relentlessly, leaving him restless and disoriented. Throughout the last two weeks, he had often jolted awake in the middle of the night.

Lu Yang stroked his chin. Now that’s something new. “Come, take us to see this painting.”

Squire Song led the three of them through a maze of corridors before triggering a hidden mechanism inside a small room. An underground passage opened before them, showing nothing but pitch-black darkness below.

The secret chamber was packed with gold, silver, and jewels. They were precious to mortals, but to Lu Yang, even the tassel on his sword’s hilt was worth more. Among the treasures, one chest stood out. It was made of iron and wrapped with layers of talismans.

Squire Song tore the talismans away and opened the chest, revealing the painting scroll within. “This was the thing that yanked my soul away.”

The memory of what had just happened still caused Squire Song to shudder. Had it not been for Lu Yang’s Soul-Restoration Pill, he would have likely met a grim fate.

“Just as I thought.”

The closer they got to the painting, the thicker the gloomy aura around it.

Lu Yang unfurled the scroll. It was an ink landscape painting depicting a woman washing clothes by the river.

Suddenly, the painting warped. The washerwoman seemed to come alive, her head slowly turning to gaze at the people outside the painting.

“Cultivators again?”

Water seeped from the painting, droplets floating into the air and coalescing into the appearance of the washerwoman.

“So you are the one who pulled his soul back?” The washerwoman stared at Lu Yang with a hostile expression, her pretty features now contorted.

“Cultivator, do not meddle in affairs that don’t concern you.”

The washerwoman sensed an overwhelming threat from Lu Yang’s trio. These three are different from past cultivators. It’s best to avoid a fight and urge them to leave instead.

She pointed at Squire Song and coldly uttered, “Twenty years ago, he promised me that if I helped him become a tycoon, he would offer me his soul. Now, twenty years have passed. He now has a happy family, thriving business, and immense wealth as the top local magnate. It is time for him to honor his promise!”

“Is this true?” Lu Yang turned to Squire Song, unsurprised. Squire Song had clearly omitted crucial details earlier. Otherwise, why would a painting help him with his business without expecting anything in return?

There is always a price.

It’s the same principle as the incident with the water ghost we’d met in Hanshui City. He had helped people commit insurance fraud so that he could get salt.

Squire Song nodded in shame.

“You see?” The washerwoman sneered, casting a disdainful glance at Squire Song. “The pact was made willingly without deceit. Now I’m just asking you to fulfil your promise—how is that wrong of me?”

Lu Yang slowly shook his head, regarding her with a pitiful gaze. “Have you read Great Xia’s penal code?”

“Great Xia Penal Code?”

A faint smile played on Lu Yang’s lips as he activated his Unbeatable Golden Core. “The Great Xia Penal Code states that a victim may lawfully consent to another party infringing upon certain legally protected interests, such as the disposition of property, or acts resulting in minor or serious bodily harm. However, any consent given to acts resulting in death shall be deemed invalid.

“Of course, not all promises that result in death are void. Life-and-death duels entered willingly, for instance, remain valid. But your actions don’t belong to any of these rare cases.

“If you had been more studious and learned about Great Xia’s legal history, you’d know that many diabolic magical treasures in history lured people into exchanging their lives in return for the fulfillment of their wishes, thereby achieving the goal of refining their souls.

“The Minister of Justice at the time became aware of this issue and thus added this specific provision to the laws of Great Xia, precisely to prevent artifacts like you from engaging in such conduct.”

Lu Yang sighed and looked at the washerwoman as if she was a legal illiterate. “Looks like legal education still hasn’t reached where it should.”

Ever since learning how often his shifu wound up behind bars, Lu Yang had devoted every spare moment to studying the law, determined not to follow in his shifu’s footsteps. Now, it seems like my efforts aren’t completely in vain.

Most people, despite learning a great deal of law, were at a loss when it came to choosing the right statute to apply, usually finding themselves in a dilemma.

But Lu Yang was different. He had the Unbeatable Golden Core. Activating it during battle could allow him to quickly sift through his legal knowledge and pinpoint the most relevant statute to apply.

However, it should be noted that the Unbeatable Golden Core couldn’t select legal statutes that Lu Yang hadn’t studied, since the victory conditions it provided were based on Lu Yang’s knowledge.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy clicked her tongue in awe from the mental space. Despite being the creator of the Unbeatable Golden Core, I’d never imagined it could be used like this.

Tao Yaoye secretly transmitted an auditory message to Lan Ting. “Junior Sister Lan, did you know about this statute?”

Lan Ting shook her head blankly. “No, our sect doesn’t teach this.”

The two saw the same bewilderment reflected in their eyes, feeling an invisible chasm separating them from their Senior Brother Lu.

“You’ve seized Master Song’s soul, which violates the criminal law and amounts to attempted murder. You’ll have to come with us.”

The washerwoman sneered, unfazed. “Don’t think you’re the only one who has studied criminal law. Let me tell you, I’m a magical treasure, so the law doesn’t apply to me at all!”

Lu Yang glanced up at the washerwoman. “Oh? That’s even better. Since you’re a masterless magical treasure, it doesn’t matter even if I damage you.”

Lan Ting’s expression turned odd. Why does this conversation sound more and more familiar?

“Arrogant! Do you really think I’m afraid of you three puny cultivators?!”

Chapter 519: Watch Me Confess for You!

The washerwoman had no desire to fight Lu Yang and his companions, but that didn’t mean she could not fight them. Yet they dream of defeating me? Do they really think I’m some fragile clay figurine?!

The painting scroll hovered in the air, gushing forth an endless torrent of water like a cascading waterfall, rapidly filling the entire hidden chamber.

Seeing this, Lu Yang grabbed Squire Song by the collar and bolted outside. While Lu Yang would be fine, Squire Song was a mortal. Trapped in that chamber, he would drown in less than a minute.

The moment the four of them reached the surface, a thunderous boom erupted behind them. The small room constructed over the hidden chamber broke apart as the water from the painting surged upward like artesian water, frothing and churning violently. The washerwoman stood atop the water column, gazing down at Lu Yang imperiously.

A few droplets of water touched Lu Yang’s lips, and he looked as if he had stumbled upon something astonishing.

“This is...fresh water!”

Tao Yaoye: “?”

Lan Ting: “?”

What is Senior Brother Lu Yang saying?

Why is he even tasting the water to test if it’s salty or fresh? And isn’t it perfectly normal for it to be fresh water?

Sensing the stares of his junior sisters, Lu Yang coughed awkwardly and pretended nothing had happened. After the incident with the water ghost in Hanshui City, he had developed a habit of checking whether an opponent used salt or fresh water.

With a flick of her sleeve, the washerwoman split the rising spring beneath her into three water serpents that lunged toward the trio.

Unfazed, Lu Yang unsheathed his Qingfeng Sword. Sword qi soared skyward and sliced through the water serpents. Normally, such a strike could cleave the water serpents in two, but this slash contained countless tiny sword qi, each continuously puncturing individual droplets and leaving no chance for them to reform into serpents.

Tao Yaoye opened her Thousand Illusions Umbrella, its crimson canopy acting like a shield. The water serpent crashed against it and instantly fell apart.

The sash coiled around Lan Ting’s waist fluttered with the breeze, stretching longer and longer until it ensnared the water serpent charging at her. The water serpent writhed violently on the ground, shaking the earth in its struggle to break free.

“Well, well, well, I’ve truly underestimated all of you!” The washerwoman was secretly alarmed. This ambush of mine would have pushed even Nascent Soul cultivators into a disadvantage, yet these three brats had blocked it.

“Scatter!”

At her command, the three water serpents dissolved like melting snow, scattering into puddles before condensing once more, transforming into a waterwall that was seven to eight zhang tall.

The waterfall crashed down, engulfing all three.

“Return!”

As the word left her mouth, Lu Yang’s trio, the painting’s water, and the washerwoman vanished, leaving only a dazed Squire Song and the fallen painting scroll behind.

~~~

“We’re inside the painting?” Lu Yang looked down at his hands, now devoid of skin, bone, or blood. They were rendered stark black and white yet lifelike in their detail.

He had become a figure within the painting, his entire being now composed of ink and wash.

“I don’t see Junior Sister Tao and Junior Sister Lan. Did we get separated? That washerwoman does have a bit of brains.”

It wasn’t his first time encountering such a tactic. Back when the senior disciples had taken turns thrashing him, one female disciple skilled in the Painting Dao had used this move against him.

The solution was simple—defeat the caster, and one would break free from an ink-wash painting state.

Of course, if the caster defeated Lu Yang, Lu Yang could still break free. Though how he knew that was better left unmentioned.

~~~

“We’re inside the painting?” Lan Ting swiftly concluded after assessing her surroundings.

The sudden appearance of the washerwoman made Lan Ting vigilant.

The washerwoman raised a hand, stopping Lan Ting. “Don’t move. I mean no harm. Little lass, tell me your wish, and I can help you grant it. In exchange, the price is that you must spare my life.”

From the earlier exchange, the washerwoman gauged that it was impossible for her to defeat three at once, so she might as well eliminate them one by one.

Wishes and prices were rules set by the creator of the painting scroll. Even the washerwoman was bound by them. If she promised a wish but failed to fulfil it, she would receive punishment. Correspondingly, if she fulfilled the wish, her combat power would be elevated to a higher level.

“Any wish works?” Lan Ting still eyed her warily.

“Speak freely. As long as it’s within my means, it shall be done.”

Blushing faintly, Lan Ting probed, “Like...confessing to Senior Brother Lu Yang and having him accept me?”

The washerwoman sized Lan Ting up, noticing her pretty features and excellent figure. This is precisely what men like.

“That’s not difficult.”

With a swirl, she took on Lan Ting’s appearance. “Watch me confess for you!”

~~~ freewebnovel.com

A similar scene unfolded with Tao Yaoye.

The washerwoman was utterly baffled. What kind of charisma does this male cultivator have to make these two beauties fall head over heels in love with him?
~~~

“Senior Brother Lu Yang, I’ve finally found you!”

Splitting herself into two, the washerwoman turned herself into Lan Ting and Tao Yaoye, feigning distress as they rushed toward Lu Yang.

The “two girls” flung themselves at Lu Yang, leaving him completely nonplussed.

I’ve never encountered a situation like this before.

“Tao Yaoye”’s eyes glistened with tears, her face flushed like peach blossoms. Pressing against his chest, she gazed at him seductively. “Senior Brother Lu Yang, actually, I’ve always...”

“Lan Ting” cut in urgently, “Actually, I’ve also...”

Lu Yang extended a hand, interrupting them. “Junior sisters, how could your senior brother not understand your feelings? But we are fellow disciples; we cannot do such things. They’re improper and go against ethics. How would the world view us?”

“Tao Yaoye” declared with a steadfast gaze, “Senior Brother, I’m not afraid of what the world thinks!”

“Lan Ting” nodded fervently. “Exactly! Senior Brother, what does the world’s opinion have to do with us? We live for ourselves; why care about what others think? Can they dictate everything?”

Lu Yang grew increasingly troubled, finding this matter inappropriate. “But my cultivation is lacking, and my experience is shallow. I fear I’m not as perfect as you two imagine.”

“That’s not a problem, Senior Brother. It’s fine even if you aren’t perfect.”

Lu Yang shook his head. “That still won’t do. Even if I agree, how could Sixth Elder and Palace Leader Luo allow something this preposterous?”

“They will!”

Lu Yang thought he had been tactful enough, yet it did nothing to waver the two, so he could only say, “But you both possess immortal physiques, while I have a Sword Spirit Root and know nothing about immortal physiques. Even if you become my disciples, I wouldn’t be able to teach you.”
