“That’s right. Didn’t you witness my grand display in the finals, where I emerged as the number one Intermediate Golden Core cultivator? That’s why you wanted me to be your shifu?”

Having lived two lifetimes with no romantic experience, Lu Yang could hardly make sense of the behaviors of females, and neither could the Unbeatable Golden Core aid him here.

However, he had the Everlasting Immortal Fairy as his golden finger cheat. Upon awakening, she had claimed that as a woman, she understood women best and could help me court the woman I like.

Even if she’s unreliable in other aspects, surely she understands this better than I do.

The washerwoman, “...”

The failed confession meant she didn’t fulfil the wish. Her aura withered, and she could no longer maintain control of the painting scroll, expelling all three.

She stared at Lu Yang as if she was facing a formidable foe. “I’ve truly underestimated you! To think you saw through my rules!”

Lu Yang’s head was full of question marks. He didn’t know what the washerwoman was talking about at all.

And how did I suddenly come out?

Weren’t we supposed to defeat the caster?

Chapter 520: The Elusive Washerwoman

With the rules broken, the washerwoman’s momentum largely waned. Seizing the opening, Lu Yang struck first.

“Slashing Word Mantra!”

Enlightened by the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang’s understanding of the Sword Dao had ascended to new heights, and his Slashing Word Mantra now carried unprecedented might.

Cleaved in two, the washerwoman let out a shrill scream and dissolved into two streams of ink that retreated into the painting scroll.

Within the painting, her features were contorted with resentment as she glared at Lu Yang, yet she dared not show herself again. Despite her intentions to kill, the earlier battle had proven that she struggled against Lu Yang alone, much less all three.

“Cultivator, I admit you’re stronger than me. I’ll take it that you’ve won this time!” With that, painting floated into the air, preparing to flee.

“Think you can escape?”

The painting scroll was fast, but Lu Yang’s sword was faster. With another strike of the Slashing Word Mantra, he sent the painting plummeting from the air, though it remained unharmed.

He clicked his tongue. The painting scroll’s quality is better than I’d thought. I can’t sever it at my current level.

“Cultivator, you’re indeed very strong, but don’t push things too far. If you spare me now, I guarantee I’ll never return or harm Squire Song. But if you keep hindering me from leaving, you may be able to protect the Song Family for now, but can you protect them forever?”

Lu Yang sneered, prodding the scroll with his sword tip. “Don’t think I’m ignorant. Magical treasures like you have their own rules. Since you helped Squire Song achieve his goal, you must receive payment. If you don’t, it would at best destabilize your foundation or at worst erase your consciousness.”

The washerwoman fell silent, stunned by how swiftly Lu Yang had seen through her rules. But she couldn’t admit it. “A bunch of nonsense!”

Lu Yang couldn’t be bothered to argue with the washerwoman. In any case, we have to take the painting scroll away and ensure Squire Song’s safety.

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting chose to trust Lu Yang’s judgement. Tao Yaoye stepped forward and used her identity jade pendant to absorb the painting scroll.

But it soon flew out of it.

“You think this thing can trap me?” The washerwoman scoffed. Although I’m a masterless magical treasure that can be absorbed into any storage ring anytime, I can manipulate the painting scroll to escape the storage ring anytime. No one can dream of capturing me!

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting attempted twice more with their identical jade tablets, but the painting would escape every time.

They exchanged grim looks. If they couldn’t take the painting scroll with them, it would likely take revenge on Squire Song’s family once they left.

“Let me try.”

When Lu Yang grasped the scroll, the washerwoman initially thought nothing of it until a suction force from his palm caused her expression to shift drastically.

Lu Yang performed Village in Palm, sucking the painting into his palm. freewebnovel.com

“It succeeded? Senior Brother Lu, what technique is this?” The two girls were floored.

“A spatial mighty ability—Sleeve Cosmos,” Lu Yang replied aloofly.

“Don’t think you can trap me just because you know a spatial mighty ability!” The washerwoman’s voice rang from his palm as she escaped again.

Lu Yang scratched his chin and reactivated Village in Palm, absorbing the washerwoman back in before pressing his palms together.

Completely oblivious, the washerwoman assumed it was the same trick as before. She controlled the scroll to fly from her left palm to her right, then back again, but she couldn’t find a way out no matter how she tried.

“Strange, where’s the exit?”

Fortunately, it wasn’t the first day she had developed sentience. Having witnessed numerous cultivators and spatial abilities over time, she knew the greatest weakness of such abilities was their rapid spirit energy consumption. With Lu Yang’s current cultivation, he can sustain it for at most three to five minutes.

“Senior Brother, can we consider this a success now?” Tao Yaoye curiously stared at Lu Yang, who had his palms pressed together. The more she looked, the more she felt that he resembled a monk in prayer.

“Not yet. Maintaining Sleeve Cosmos drains a lot of spirit energy. I can only sustain it for about fifteen minutes.”

“Then what do we do?” Squire Song asked anxiously. Judging by the washerwoman’s attitude, she’ll undoubtedly seek vengeance against my family once she’s freed.

And to think I was once secretly in love with her.

“No problem. Consuming Great Rejuvenation Pills can extend the duration of the ability. Two hours won’t be an issue.”

“But two hours isn’t enough time to return to the sect.” Lu Yang fretted, beginning to brainstorm solutions.

Lu Yang shook his head. “I’ve already thought of a solution.”

~~~

“Dear guest, are you certain you wish to sell a painting-type magical treasure that carries an artifact spirit?” The administrator at the Luodi Merchant Guild inquired politely, his eyes practically gleaming.

Every magical treasure that carried an artifact spirit could fetch astronomical prices.

It’s just that this particular customer’s appearance is somewhat odd. His palms are pressed together in prayer, while the two female cultivators flanking him act like protectors, occasionally feeding him a pill.

Is this some Blissful Chan cultivator?[1]

It couldn’t be helped. With his hands occupied, Lu Yang couldn’t consume the pills himself, so he had no choice but to enlist his junior sisters’ help in feeding him the pills.

Squire Song had originally volunteered for the task, but the glares from Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting scared him off.

“Daoist Lu, are you sure this will work?” Squire Song whispered, his voice still laced with apprehension.

Yuanhe County’s location was remote, its local customs improper, and incidents similar to the wonton stall overcharging customers happened routinely, discouraging the Luodi Merchant Guild from establishing a branch there.

Thus, the group had traveled to Qingshui Commandery.

“Of course.”

“But what if the painting scroll escapes and returns to my home?”

“Then you’d profit! You could sell it again.”

“Makes sense.”

That said, Squire Song couldn’t help but feel that something was amiss. Even if Lu Yang couldn’t trap the washerwoman for long, he believed the merchant guild could surely manage it. If they can’t even restrain a mere magical treasure, how can they still call themselves a merchant guild?

Upon hearing they had a sentient magical treasure for sale, the merchant guild immediately summoned their most senior appraiser to authenticate the item.

“This magical treasure of mine runs pretty fast,” Lu Yang warned.

The merchant guild’s branch manager laughed heartily, gesturing around the room. “This room is protected by twelve types of arrays from inside to out. I’d genuinely like to see what kind of magical treasure could possibly escape!”

Lu Yang separated his palms, and the washerwoman shot out astride the scroll with a whoosh.

Bang!

She slammed headfirst into the wall before falling to the ground.

The elderly appraiser picked up the painting scroll and activated a secret spell. Rings of miniature arrays appeared before his eyes, allowing him to analyze the scroll’s construction.

Stroking his white beard, the appraiser smiled with fascination. “Interesting. It’s crafted from Divine Transfiguration-grade materials, though the crafter’s skill was lacking and failed to bring out the materials’ full potential. Despite that, this magical treasure still developed an artifact spirit, which is remarkably rare; not just that, it even encompasses rules.

“Three million spirit stones. How does that sound?” The appraiser quoted gleefully.

Lu Yang pondered briefly before removing his identity jade tablet and handing it to the appraiser. “I’m from the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

“Five million spirit stones.” The appraisal revised his offer immediately.

Lu Yang continued, “I’m Lu Yang. My brother is the Meng Family’s eldest young master, Meng Jingzhou. As for my two junior sisters behind me, one is also from the Dao-Seeking Sect, and the other is from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.”

“Six million spirit stones.” The branch manager increased the price on the spot.

Fearing Lu Yang would reveal more information, he hastily added, “We really can’t go higher. Let us at least earn a little.”

Even as the continent’s largest merchant guild, the Luodi Merchant Guild wasn’t above driving hard bargains.

Although Lu Yang lacked expertise in this field, he could leverage his identity to prevent them from lowballing him.

1. Though Buddhist sect cultivators are typically supposed to lead ascetic lives, the “Blissful Chan” or “Joyous Chan” usually refers to dual cultivation in novels. ☜

Chapter 521: Teacher Tao

“Here, your spirit stones.” After leaving the merchant guild, Lu Yang handed the storage ring from the merchant guild to Squire Song.

Squire Song nearly dropped the storage ring in shock. This is six million spirit stones! Yet he’s giving it to me just like that?!

“No no no, I can’t possibly accept so much. Ten thousand, ten thousand is enough.” As a mortal, Squire Song dared not gamble on whether Great Xia’s law enforcement could intimidate those who would covet his sudden wealth if word got out.

Declining wouldn’t be appropriate either. I’ll just accept a teeny bit.

Seeing Squire Song’s reaction, Lu Yang knew the latter had his own concerns. He didn’t press the matter and sent him back to Yuanhe County. He then split the remaining sum, giving two million to each of his two junior sisters.

Lu Yang had never placed much importance on spirit stones. Between his patent royalties and barbeque shop dividends, only ancestral wealth like Meng Jingzhou’s or visionary entrepreneurs like Tao Yaoye could rival his financial standing among the younger generation.

Moreover, he had little use for spirit stones.

For magical treasures, he possessed the Qingfeng Sword gifted by Yun Zhi and the Mingyue Sword once wielded by the Qilin Immortal.

For cultivation items, such as natural treasures, great pills, and spirit soils, he could redeem them anytime at the Great Mission Hall or pluck a few root whiskers from the ginseng doll. freewebnovel.com

For cultivation techniques, the scripture library had everything he needed.

Such were the privileges of being in a major sect. Cultivation resources were abundant, allowing disciples to focus solely on cultivation.

The Great Mission Hall was set up not to burden disciples with tasks, but to send them down the mountain and wander the world to punish evil and uphold justice, preventing them from losing their emotions due to endless cultivation. The Dao-Seeking Sect had never advocated the concept of supreme detachment—transcending all emotions and being unruffled by them.

Judging by the Ancient Five Immortals, especially the Qilin Immortal, Lu Yang doubted any had achieved the state of supreme detachment.

The most prominent faction preaching supreme detachment was the Heartless Creed.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shared, “I’ve met several individuals who claimed to follow the path of supreme detachment. They say their heart and mind are wholly devoted to the Dao, but their actions are really ruthless. Three killed their wives or children to prove their Dao, and two refined entire clans into magical treasures, sparing none of their family members. Furthermore, their faces were perpetually emotionless, as if everyone owed them spirit stones. However, they were frail in battle—one self-detonation from me was all it took to wipe them out.

“In my opinion, they hadn’t achieved true supreme detachment.”

“That doesn’t count?” Lu Yang was puzzled. What they did already sounds ruthless enough.

“Of course not. For starters, would they dare go naked? Wearing clothes means they still have a sense of shame. How can one be considered to have achieved supreme detachment if they still feel shame?”

Lu Yang mulled over it. That’s indeed the case. I didn’t expect the seemingly guileless, adorable, and dimwitted Everlasting Immortal Fairy to offer such penetrating insights.

~~~

On the way to Qingshui Commandery after departing Yuanhe County, Lu Yang remembered he was a sword cultivator who could fly on swords instead of riding horses.

The Qingfeng Sword hovered three feet off the ground. Lu Yang jumped onto it with hands clasped behind his back, his robes fluttering as he stood there in all his glory. “Now this looks more like a sword immortal.”

He had heard of a special duel format between sword cultivators. Two sword cultivators would stand face to face and charge at each other while flying on their swords, with the one knocked off losing. He felt he could probably only use a flying carriage if he participated.

“Lu Yang, a Divine Transfiguration cultivator has set their sights on you all,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy warned.

“A Divine Transfiguration cultivator?” Lu Yang braked his flying sword, hairs standing on end.

With a thunderous explosion, a figure dispersed the smoke and dust, blocking the trio’s path.

“Such audacity! How dare you sell this esteemed one’s magical treasure to the merchant guild?! Are you tired of living?!”

The figure’s aura waves made the three of their hearts tremble. Even the Unbeatable Golden Core was blaring warnings for Lu Yang to flee immediately. From their chilling aura, matching that of the painting scroll’s lineage, it was clear they were a seasoned old monster who had secretly slaughtered countless lives.

“Your magical treasure?” Tao Yaoye was bewildered. If the painting scroll has a master, how could it be stored in a storage ring?

Lu Yang thought about it from another perspective and pieced things together. “You feared Great Xia would track you down through the magical treasure, so you erased your imprints from it. After the magical treasure refines people, you plan to appear to reap the benefits?”

“You’re a clever one.” The chilling figure was surprised at how quickly Lu Yang had figured out the truth.

Though that won’t change their impending fate.

“Judging by the jade pendants at your waists, two of you are from the Dao-Seeking Sect and one is from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace?”

“You recognize our identities, yet you still dare attack us?”

The chilling figure chuckled darkly. “So what if you’re from immortal sects? Even if you die here, no matter how mighty they are, the immortal sects won’t be able to detect me!”

Lu Yang narrowed his eyes. Is this genuine ignorance or bravado? When something befalls immortal sect disciples, immortal sects can calculate their karma; there’s no way the culprit can get away.

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting silently gripped their weapons like they were facing a formidable foe, preparing to launch an assault at any moment.

“You dare harm our boss’s guests? Die!” Another icy voice rang from above.

It was a figure wielding a nine-section whip[1] that was ablaze with eerie ghost fire. The nine-section whip lashed toward the chilling figure, the azure ghost fire pursuing its target relentlessly like maggots clinging to bones.

Both parties engaged in a fierce battle, dishing out various magical treasures. Under a hundred exchanges, the nine-section whip’s wielder subdued the chilling figure.

“The few of you, come with us. Our boss would like to meet you.” The nine-section whip’s owner stared at Lu Yang’s trio coldly, his tone brooking no refusal. Though he was also at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, the ease with which he defeated the chilling figure showed he was outstanding even among cultivators of the same realm.

Tao Yaoye’s hands grew clammy. I’ve seen this person with the nine-section whip before. It was when I visited the barbeque shop with Senior Brother Lu Yang. He was standing behind Vice Creed Leader Shi, likely his right-hand man.

I think he was called... Huo Huashen?

Why would people from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed seek us out? What do they want with us? Tao Yaoye dared not continue down that line of thought.

Although Lan Ting didn’t know Huo Huashen, she could sense from his aura that he wasn’t someone to be trifled with. Should we run? But he’s clearly much more powerful than we are. How could we escape?

“Who’s your boss? What do you want with us?”

Huo Huashen shot Tao Yaoye a frosty glance. “You’ll know when you’re there.”

Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting looked at Lu Yang with pleading eyes, and the latter nodded. “Let’s go see.”

~~~

The journey passed in suffocating silence. Huo Huashen walked at the front, leading the three to a small pavilion. It was extremely isolated, with no nearby villages, shops, or even passers-by.

In the small pavilion sat a lone figure, dressed in black like a bottomless abyss. A single glance at him felt like plunging into a frozen pit; he was truly like a great devil with countless lives on his hands.

He was none other than Shi Huagu, one of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s three vice creed leaders.

“Boss, they’re here. I’ve already verified that no one else will come.”

“Got it. Stand behind.”

Huo Huashen gave an affirmative reply and stood behind Shi Huagu, as quiet as a statue.

“You must be Teacher Tao,[2] the creator of Dreamlike Bubble Mirage. Your reputation precedes you. I finally get to meet you in person today. With the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage’s insane popularity, you must have earned a great deal of spirit stones, truly a cause for celebration.”

Tao Yaoye’s blood ran cold, and her back was drenched in cold sweat. So I was the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s target all along?

Are they targeting the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage? Are they trying to rob me or demand the patent?

“It’s just mortals watching, so the earnings aren’t much,” Tao Yaoye said, bracing herself.

“The earnings aren’t much? Teacher Tao, you shouldn’t say that.”

“What exactly do you want?”

”Humans die for wealth; birds perish for food. With your intelligence, Teacher Tao, surely you can guess what I want?” The corners of Shi Huagu’s mouth curved upward into a cold smirk.

“Teacher Tao, can you use the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage to help us promote our barbeque business? We have sufficient budget, and the price is negotiable.”

1. The jiujie-bian is a soft weapon in wushu. ☜

2. The term ‘xiansheng’ can have multiple meanings, such as teacher, mister, or a master in an arts-related field. ☜

Chapter 522: Promotion Method

Tao Yaoye paused for two full seconds before uttering a single word. “What?”

She hadn’t misheard Vice Creed Leader Shi; it was just that his words didn’t quite match the earlier atmosphere.

Lan Ting was equally dumbfounded. Given the tension just moments ago, even if Huo Huashen and Vice Creed Leader Shi had pressed two big machetes against their necks and demanded their money, she wouldn’t have been surprised.

Lu Yang, however, had seen this coming. In fact, he had anticipated this scenario when Tao Yaoye invented the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

Back when Tao Yaoye first accompanied Lu Yang to the barbeque shop to get in contact with Vice Creed Leader Shi, Lu Yang had reassured her that there was no need to be nervous around people from the Nine-Netherworlds Creed, for they would be the ones begging her for help in the future.

At the time, Tao Yaoye didn’t understand what he meant.

Lu Yang had initially considered using his Heavenly Court Creed identity to suggest that Vice Creed Leader Shi seek Tao Yaoye out for a collaboration. But on second thought, he felt that doing so would make it seem like the Heavenly Court Creed placed too much importance on a barbeque business, which could easily raise Vice Creed Leader Shi’s suspicions, so he abandoned the idea.

Looks like Vice Creed Leader Shi’s mind is somewhat sharp enough to think of collaborating with Junior Sister Tao even without my prompting.

Vice Creed Leader Shi assumed his abruptness had startled them and offered a faint smile. “Teacher Tao, have you heard of ‘One More Time Barbeque Shop?’ My surname is Shi, and I’m the boss.”

Seeing Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting still dazed, Lu Yang feigned shock with deliberate exaggeration. “You mean that One More Time Barbeque Shop that’s been all the rage lately, with chains spread across the continent and everyone raving about it after eating there?!”

“And this must be Prodigy Lu. To be capable of fighting the Heavenly Court Creed’s young creed leader to a draw, you’re truly the pride of modern-era cultivators.” Vice Creed Leader Shi’s words were sincere.

I know Young Creed Leader Lu’s background best. He is the personal disciple of Dou Heavenly Sovereign and the designated successor to the next creed leader. Even ancient immortals feared him, a true testament to his remarkable talents.

Who would’ve thought someone as powerful as Young Creed Leader Lu would meet his match?!

“I have long heard of your reputation, Teacher Tao. To have created something as innovative as Dreamlike Bubble Mirage and stir waves across Great Xia, you’re truly a promising young talent.”

Vice Creed Leader Shi lamented inwardly, This is the gap between people. Look at Tao Yaoye—she’s not even twenty, yet she is already a tycoon, and this is just the beginning. Meanwhile, I’ve muddled through two thousand years, am ten billion in debt, and get struck by lightning monthly.

“The one who brought you here is my subordinate, also the manager of our first barbeque branch. His surname is Huo. He’s not good with words, so I instructed him not to speak carelessly. I hope he didn’t say anything out of line on the way here.”

Tao Yaoye thought, He didn’t say anything out of line—he didn’t speak at all, which was even more unnerving.

“Boss Shi, how exactly would this promotion with the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage work?”

“Here’s the thing. Before the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage begins, isn’t there a brief waiting period? I’d like to use that time to promote my barbeque business.”

Tao Yaoye hesitated. “But that segment is only a minute long. Is that enough time for promotion?”

“A minute is enough. We’ll prepare a one-minute promotional illusion,” Vice Creed Leader Shi replied with a smile. He had long done his research.

From his experience running the business, he had summed up two key factors for success: first, a good reputation, where the flavor and service must be up to standard to attract returning customers; second, effective promotion to build the name.

The Dreamlike Bubble Mirage’s explosive growth far outstrips that of our barbeque business. With countless people viewing it daily, it’s a perfect avenue for publicity. It’ll definitely be much more effective than placing ads in the Luodi Merchant Guild’s intelligence reports!

Vice Creed Leader Shi had multiple reasons for choosing this method of promotion. Strong promotional impact is one thing, but another factor is Tao Yaoye’s identity—a disciple of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Opportunities to collaborate with the Dao-Seeking Sect are hard to come by. This is the perfect chance to establish ties with them!

Look at how the Everlasting Creed had exhausted all means to plant spies and plot schemes just to infiltrate their mountain gates. Building a connection with the Dao-Seeking Sect is no small feat.

If this succeeds, our Nine-Netherworlds Creed could openly collaborate with the Dao-Seeking Sect while secretly collaborating with the Heavenly Court Creed. This gives us fallback plans with both the righteous and the demonic paths, allowing us to maneuver, adapt, and seize every advantage!

“As for the fees, Teacher Tao, we’re open to negotiation.” Vice Creed Leader Shi went all in. This is vital for promoting our barbeque business and forming a link with the Dao-Seeking Sect. I can’t afford to be stingy with spirit stones.

Fearing Tao Yaoye might refuse, he had even arranged for actors to pose as the washerwoman’s master and ambush Lu Yang’s group midway so Huo Huashen could swoop in as their savior. That way, they would owe him a favor, making refusal unlikely.

Under such circumstances, they wouldn’t even demand an exorbitant price.

In truth, a little scrutiny would have revealed the flaws in this incident. The one who ambushed Lu Yang’s trio was at the Divine Transfiguration Stage, while the washerwoman had spent twenty years just to harvest the soul of a mortal like Squire Song. Even if diabolic cultivators were cautious and killed discreetly, such efficiency was absurdly low.

Lu Yang noticed the loophole but chose not to expose it.

It was because there was no need to. The barbeque business was their own venture. Even if Vice Creed Leader Shi hadn’t employed such tactics, Lu Yang would still have wanted to promote the barbeque shop through the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage.

Tao Yaoye was conflicted. This was her first time encountering a situation like this, and she didn’t know how much she should ask for. She secretly shot Lu Yang a glance, pleading for his aid. With Vice Creed Leader Shi here, she dared not communicate with their spiritual consciousness, lest their messages be intercepted.

Lu Yang wasn’t sure of market rates either, for this was unprecedented. Leaning forward slightly, he smiled. “Boss Shi, how many spirit stones are you willing to offer? And for how long do you plan to buy the promotional rights?”

Shi Huagu didn’t expect them to throw the difficult question back to him. He gritted his teeth. “Ten million! I’ll buy one year of promotional rights!”

Ten million was a sum an ordinary Divine Transfiguration cultivator had to spend a lifetime accumulating, while those from ancestral clans could amass more.

“Boss Shi, you sure know how to jest.” Lu Yang smiled faintly and placed the storage ring from the merchant guild on the stone table. “The three of us can earn six million from a single mission. Ten million isn’t quite enough, right?”

Lu Yang wasn’t bragging. Based on his rewards from past missions, the six million he obtained this time was considered little. His last mission involved accompanying Li Haoran on an outing to unwind, during which he incidentally found the Heavenly Court Creed. The mission before involved slaying a tiger demon and dealing with the tiger-henchman ghosts, during which he incidentally infiltrated the Everlasting Creed.

Both missions yielded gains that can’t be measured with spirit stones, which means they far surpass the rewards this time.

“Twenty—no, thirty million!”

Vice Creed Leader Shi could feel his heart dripping with blood. No one has advertised with the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage before. If this fails, thirty million would go down the drain.

Lu Yang remained at ease. “Fixed price: fifty million—take it or leave it. One-minute opening advertisements, plus scenes of people eating at One More Time Barbeque Shop within the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage for a year.”

Vice Creed Leader Shi was stunned. He hadn’t considered such a promotional method. If it really works, fifty million might be worth it.

Thinking of the barbeque shop’s booming business and the overwhelmingly rich Heavenly Court Creed, Vice Creed Leader Shi steeled himself. “Deal. Fifty million it is!”

“You’ll be glad you chose to partner with us, Boss Shi.”

Chapter 523: Pay-Your-Debts-With-Your-Life Lightning

“This storage ring contains ten million spirit stones—consider it a deposit. Please keep it well, Teacher Tao.” Vice Creed Leader Shi’s heart ached. He had originally planned for this ten million to purchase the promotional rights. However, with just a brief exchange, it had been reduced to a mere down payment. “I will need to go back to gather the remaining forty million. Please allow half a month.

“We also haven’t finished producing the one-minute promotional illusion. It will be handed to Teacher Tao alongside the forty million spirit stones in two weeks. This is a wooden token for communication.” He passed a palm-sized wooden tablet to Tao Yaoye, identical to the one he had previously given Lu Yang.

“Once all the spirit stones are ready, we will get in touch with you through this wooden token, Teacher Tao.” His attitude was nothing but attentive. Just as Lu Yang had said, it was the Nine-Netherworlds Creed begging Tao Yaoye for a favor—she was the one who held all the leverage.

“Alright, I have other matters to attend to, so I won’t keep you any longer.” Vice Creed Leader Shi slowly rose to his feet and shot a meaningful glance at Huo Huashen, signaling for the latter to escort Lu Yang’s trio out.

Huo Huashen nodded in understanding. He retrieved a bottle of eye drops from his storage ring and handed it to Vice Creed Leader Shi.

Shi Huagu didn’t know how to respond. “I meant for you to escort them out!”

If not for his exceptional talent and the possibility of him becoming vice creed leader or even creed leader given enough time, I would have hacked this brat to death long ago!

Huo Huashen grumbled inwardly, How could you blame me for this? Your meaningful glance can have several meanings. Who could understand?

After Huo Huashen led the trio away, they had walked for barely two li when a sudden clap of thunder boomed behind them, jolting all of them. Turning back, they saw roiling storm clouds above Vice Creed Leader Shi’s location. Thunder rumbled and lightning flashed, like a doomsday scene unfolding before them.

This was a lightning tribulation deadly even to Fusion cultivators. Despite the distance, the pressure it emanated was palpable.

“Wait, why don’t I feel any pressure?” Lu Yang was perplexed, noting how his two junior sisters and Huo Huashen had paled under the residual might of the thunder.

Why do I not feel anything at all?

“Naturally, it’s because of me,” declared the Everlasting Immortal Fairy as she puffed out her chest with pride.

“You’re that powerful, Immortal Fairy?” Lu Yang was stunned. Since when did the Immortal Fairy command such respect?

“Of course! Most lightning tribulations trace back to the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit. Wouldn’t lightning tribulations have to show me some respect?”

The lightning tribulation wasn’t the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s creation. His contribution was simply in developing and promoting its variations.

Lu Yang was amazed. I didn’t know that even lightning tribulations have to give face to the Immortal Fairy.

Looks like the Heaven Mandate Immortal was deeply traumatized by her.

“From the looks of it, this is probably the ‘Pay-Your-Debts-With-Your-Life Lightning’ whipped up by the Heaven Mandate Immortal, designed to fry deadbeats.”

Lu Yang recalled something. Hadn’t Huo Huashen taken Qin Haoran’s “inheritance” from me? And wasn’t that inheritance related to debt notes...?

He confirmed that the Huo Huashen beside him was a living person and sighed inwardly. Seems like Vice Creed Leader Shi must value Huo Huashen immensely to shield him from this and keep him alive.

“Speaking of which, isn’t this lightning tribulation’s name a bit too plain?” From my impression, shouldn’t lightning tribulations be called “Supreme Purity,” “Purple Heaven,” “Six Ding,” “Six Jia,” or whatnot?

If you’re calling it “Pay-Your-Debts-With-Your-Life Lightning,” why not just call it “Debt Note Lightning?”

Heaven Mandate Immortal, did you even try?

“I also think the name works,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented.

Lu Yang’s expression cleared, as if the fog had parted before his eyes. “So it was you who named it, Immortal Fairy! No wonder it carries a sense of primal simplicity. Upon reflection, it encompasses great principles. As the saying goes, ‘pay what is owed.’ If one actually pays their debts, how would they encounter lightning tribulations? Thus, only those who refuse to pay their debts have to pay with their lives. Immortal Fairy, the name you gave it is truly profound and thought-provoking. In just a few words, it conveys multiple layers of meaning and invites repeated contemplation!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy beamed with a smile befitting her age. “Hehe, I didn’t think that much about it.”

A Fusion cultivator undergoing tribulation was a rare sight. The four of them paused to watch for a while. Huo Huashen had actually seen it several times before; he was simply accompanying Lu Yang’s trio.

In truth, they were just there for the spectacle. This lightning tribulation could threaten even Fusion cultivators. At the trio’s current cultivation realms, they still couldn’t discern the arcane essence behind Vice Creed Leader Shi’s tribulation.

As for the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, she had personally witnessed the whole process of the Heaven Mandate Immortal creating this lightning tribulation, so there was nothing for her to see.

Leaving Vice Creed Leader Shi to endure the lightning tribulation alone, Huo Huashen escorted the trio to their flying vessel.

Before parting, Huo Huashen decided he should voice his thoughts and not keep them bottled up. “If the three of you ever get the chance, do visit our barbeque shop. It may not rival the exotic delicacies in immortal sects, but our barbeque skewers taste pretty good.”

“Sure.”

~~~

Inside the flying vessel’s cabin, Lan Ting still hadn’t fully processed everything.

How did an ordinary mission escalate into being intercepted by the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s vice creed leader, then a business proposal, a windfall of ten million spirit stones, and finally a polite send-off?

Lan Ting didn’t lack money, but she had never seen anyone make money like this.

She was born into the Lan Family, whose name carried no regional prefix. Most ancestral clans bore such regional prefixes, such as “Qing Province Yan Family,” “Liang Province Wenren Family,” or “Liang Province Ye Family.” Only a select few like hers went without one. This was a mark of prestige reserved for the most elite of aristocratic clans, earned through both power and legacy.

The only other family sharing this distinction was the Meng Family. Although the Lan Family did not match the Meng Family’s status as the number one ancestral clan, they were undeniably one of the most elite.

Lu Yang exhaled in relief. This trip went quite smoothly—we didn’t have to kill Fusion cultivators or confront Transcendent Tribulation cultivators.

“Senior Brother Lu, these ten million spirit stones...” Tao Yaoye clutched the storage ring, looking at Lu Yang with unease. The sheer ease of acquiring such wealth left her unsettled.

I didn’t do anything, yet ten million spirit stones landed in my lap—with another forty million pending.

Lu Yang waved dismissively. “You earned this with your abilities. Keep it.”

“Oh.”

“One more thing.”

“What?”

Lu Yang’s eyes narrowed as several burly men stood up nearby and began approaching. He reminded her calmly, “Never show your wealth when you’re out. It’ll invite trouble.”

Tao Yaoye suddenly realized she hadn’t been speaking with Lu Yang through auditory messages earlier. Any cultivator paying attention could have overheard her. To outsiders, I possess ten million spirit stones, a fortune that would take a Divine Transfiguration cultivator a lifetime to amass, yet I’m just a Golden Core cultivator!

Such a glaring mismatch between wealth and strength is destined to attract trouble!

The burly men’s faces were twisted into fierce expressions as they strode over. Their cultivation couldn’t be discerned, but they were at least at the Golden Core Stage, possibly even the Nascent Soul Stage.

Long-distance flight drained cultivators’ spirit energy too quickly, so many cultivators still opted for flying vessels.

The burly men encircled them, ignoring Lu Yang and Lan Ting entirely. Their gazes locked onto Tao Yaoye, thinly veiled with avarice.

“Fellow Daoist, you seem to have a lot of spirit stones, eh?”

“Carrying so many spirit stones around is unsafe, ain’t it? Why don’t we safeguard them for you?”

“What do you want?!” Tao Yaoye demanded warily, her fingers subtly brushing her identity jade tablet, ready to activate her magical treasure any moment.

So what if they could be at the Nascent Soul Stage? I’m not afraid.

The leader of the burly men chuckled coldly and no longer masked his intentions.

“Fellow Daoist, have you considered depositing your spirit stones with our Luodi Merchant Guild? We offer five percent annual interest.”

Chapter 524: Uneventful Journey

Seeing Tao Yaoye still in a daze, another burly man hastily added, “Our merchant guild also offers wealth management products with eight to twelve percent annual returns. You have everything to gain and nothing to lose!”

Tao Yaoye finally understood Lu Yang’s warning about not showing one’s wealth outside to avoid inviting trouble.

Now, trouble has arrived.

One after another, they pitched things like investment plans, private funds, and low-risk high-return schemes—none of which she understood.

“No, I don’t need any,” Tao Yaoye firmly refused.

Twenty percent interest? If I invest these ten million spirit stones into expanding the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage’s scale, the gains would dwarf a paltry twelve percent return.

“I see. That’s really a pity.” The burly men could only regretfully shake their heads and give up.

Such a plump duck—why does it refuse to take the bait?

Fortunately, this was merely a minor episode in their otherwise uneventful journey.

Apart from when bailiffs halted the flying vessel, stating a murderer might be hiding on board and that every passenger’s identity must be identified, only for said murderer to suddenly lash out in a violent attack before being subdued by those same burly promoters from the merchant guild.

The murderer shrieked, “I’ve poisoned the captain. Only I have the antidote. If you don’t let me go, the captain will undoubtedly die. Just wait for doom!”

Before anyone could volunteer their piloting skills, the captain emerged and announced, “I’m a poison cultivator immune to poison,” then calmly returned to steering the flying vessel.

Then there was the Golden Core cultivator who attempted fare evasion. He was originally flying while consuming pills, but eventually grew exhausted. Just then, the flying vessel passed by, and he sneaked aboard the vessel’s tail for a free ride.

However, his concealment skills weren’t up to par. He failed to slip past the ticket inspection array and was caught, so he was forced to pay the fare.

And there was also the pregnant woman going into labor, the pain rendering her unconscious. Fortunately, a pill master among the passengers stepped in, saving both mother’s and daughter’s lives.

“Wife, wake up! We’re almost reaching our stop!” the husband shouted as he gripped the pregnant woman’s hand, but she had already passed out from the excruciating pain.

The surrounding people panicked, though they didn’t know what to do. If the mother fainted, it could cost the lives of both mother and child.

“I’m a pill master. Let me.“ A female voice familiar to Lu Yang rang out.

Lu Yang turned to see a female cultivator with golden pill patterns embroidered on her sleeves. She was clad in official clothing that only pill masters were qualified to wear, and a Dao-Seeking Sect identity jade tablet hung at her waist.

He remembered who she was. This is Senior Sister Mo Li[1] from Pill Cauldron Peak. She once stood in the middle of the line waiting to beat me. Her position in the queue suggests her strength is considered around the middle, in other words, Nascent Soul Stage.

Lu Yang didn’t rashly go up to greet her. He was curious about how she would help the pregnant woman.

Sweeping her spiritual consciousness across the pregnant woman, Mo Li frowned as she assessed the situation.

The pregnant woman has fallen into too deep a coma. Gentle methods won’t wake her, but anything harsh can risk harming the unborn child.

If that’s the case, only one solution remains.

Closing her eyes, Mo Li summoned a tiny person three inches tall from her spirit platform. It swiftly darted into the pregnant woman’s mind to take control of her body temporarily.

Soon, a baby entered the world with a loud cry.

“All done.” Mo Li heaved a sigh of relief as her nascent soul returned to her body.

Seeing both his wife and child safe, the husband was so moved that he grasped Mo Li’s hands. “Many thanks for giving birth to my wife’s baby! I can’t express my gratitude enough!” freewebnovel.com

Mo Li, “...”

If you don’t know how to express your gratitude, you can choose not to say anything.

It took considerable effort for Mo Li to dissuade the man from gifting her a commendation silk banner.

“Senior Sister Mo Li.” Lu Yang finally approached her once the matter was settled.

“Junior Brother Lu? And Junior Sister Tao Too. And isn’t this Junior Sister Lan Ting from the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace? Why are you three together?” Mo Li had a favorable impression of Lu Yang. After all, they once had intimate physical contact—and even drawn blood.

Lu Yang replied, “Well, it was a coincidence. I was on a mission with Junior Sister Tao and bumped into Junior Sister Lan Ting, who happened to be working on the same mission.”

“I see.”

“And you, Senior Sister Mo Li? Are you on a mission as well?”

Mo Li flicked her sleeves with a hint of pride. “I went to take the pill master certification exam. Look, this is the robe I just received.”

“But weren’t you already a pill master long ago?” Senior Sister Mo Li is at the Nascent Soul Stage. It’s odd that she just got certified.

“Hai, that was only recognized within the sect. Outside, it doesn’t count. Practicing medicine out here is considered illegal and could easily get me arrested. I had to treat patients secretly whenever I was out on missions.

“I was pondering about it a few days ago when it struck me. Rather than going through all the hassle every time, I might as well get certified as a pill master.”

“Congratulations on becoming a pill master recognized by the Pill Concoction Alliance.” Lu Yang cupped his hands, which Tao Yaoye and Lan Ting promptly mirrored.

Mo Li waved them off, her face twisted in a grimace at the memory of the exam. “What’s there to congratulate? The whole ordeal was a mess. First, I mixed up the exam date, then I walked into the wrong exam venue. Only after finishing did I realize I had taken the Pill Concoction Alliance’s branch manager selection test. No wonder so many other candidates nearly matched my level. I scored first, but during the post-exam identity verification, they discovered I wasn’t an official pill master. Turns out I wasn’t eligible to take the exam.

“Left with no choice, I had to run to the exam venue for the apprentice pill master exam instead. The whole time I refined pills, a bunch of great pill masters stood behind me, studying my methods. It was so annoying.”

Lu Yang thought, Senior Sister, you should consider the psychological pressure you exerted on the other apprentice candidates.

“As you can see, I’m now a pill master. The Pill Concoction Alliance even asked if I could serve as branch manager. I figured it’d be too troublesome, so I declined. In the end, they foisted some ‘honorary branch manager’ title on me instead.” From her identity jade tablet, Mo Li took out a golden cauldron-shaped badge with her name engraved on the back.

Lu Yang, “...”

Should I say ‘as expected of a senior sister from Pill Cauldron Peak?’ Her way of doing things is simply unlike that of ordinary people.

Fortunately, after the childbirth incident, the remainder of their journey passed without other events, and the flying vessel successfully arrived at the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“See you, Junior Sister Lan Ting!”

“See you!”

Lu Yang and Lan Ting waved goodbye. This flying vessel made stops at the Dao-Seeking Sect and Moon Laurel Immortal Palace.

~~~

As they entered the core area of the Dao-Seeking Sect, they spotted Meng Jingzhou passing by.

“Done with your seclusion?” Lu Yang called out casually.

“Seclusion?” Meng Jingzhou was bewildered.

Tao Yaoye smiled. “Have you forgotten, Senior Brother Meng? A few days ago, I invited you and Senior Brother Lu for a mission, but you were in seclusion, which left only Senior Brother Lu and me to handle the mission alone.”

Meeting Tao Yaoye’s calm gaze, which was laced with threat, Meng Jingzhou showed an expression of sudden realization. “Oh yes! I was indeed in seclusion those few days. I’ve just emerged, so my mind is still a bit foggy.”

Chapter 525: The Nine-Layers Immortal’s and the Qilin Immortal’s Dao Fruits

“Junior Brother Lu, there’s a thank-you letter for you.” Ten days later, a senior male disciple on duty at the Great Mission Hall delivered a letter to Lu Yang, who was currently opening his mouth to devour spirit energy for cultivation.

Lu Yang opened the letter. It was from Squire Song.

The letter primarily expressed gratitude for Lu Yang’s assistance in resolving the incident with the washerwoman, which had allowed the Song Family’s business to get back on the right track.

It also mentioned the matter regarding his youngest daughter and Young Master Zhou. Squire Song wrote that after investigations, it turned out that Young Master Zhou was his biological son, while his youngest daughter, Song Lian’er, turned out to be the steward’s daughter.

As for how such a mix-up had occurred in the first place, Squire Song didn’t elaborate. Lu Yang surmised that the midwife had mixed up the babies during childbirth.

He quietly tucked the letter away. The Song Family’s relationships were so convoluted that they gave him a headache.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented, “This is nothing. Back in ancient times, it was all tribes and clans. Their relationships were far more complicated than this.”

“Which tribe were you from, Immortal Fairy?” Lu Yang asked casually, only to be met with an unusually long silence from her.

“...A small tribe. Nothing worth mentioning,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy muttered softly, her usual vivacity vanished. “It was gone before I came of age, destroyed by a battle between a man and a beast that implicated our tribe.”

Lu Yang fell silent. He didn’t know what to say. Saying something wrong might only make things worse.

The era before the age of the Five Ancient Immortals wasn’t idyllic times. Small tribes being crushed overnight was commonplace.

“Little Junior Brother, come here for a moment.”

Fortunately, Yun Zhi’s auditory message broke the heavy silence.

“Big Senior Sister, what is it?” Lu Yang asked upon finding Yun Zhi. The latter rarely came looking for him.

Could Shifu have been caught again and needs a guarantor for bail?

Or could Shifu have been caught again and has to be visited in prison, but Big Senior Sister is too embarrassed to go herself and wants me to go instead?

Or could Shifu have finally been caught by enemies, beaten until his life is hanging by a thread, and needs someone to save him?

“Wait for the others.”

Soon, the “others” Yun Zhi mentioned arrived at Heaven’s Gate Peak one after another—Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, Man Gu, and Li Haoran.

“Greetings, Big Senior Sister.” The four bowed respectfully upon arriving.

Yun Zhi explained, “Here’s the situation. The Five Great Immortal Sects have a tradition of student exchanges. This time, five disciples from our Dao-Seeking Sect can study at the Five-Elements Sect. You five can go there.”

Originally, the exchange was supposed to be with the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace, but Palace Leader Luo had adamantly refused to let Lu Yang set foot there. Thus, Yun Zhi could only arrange for the exchange to be with the Five-Elements Sect instead.

“Go to the Five-Elements Sect?” Lu Yang and the others couldn’t stop the corners of their mouths from turning upward at the good news, their eyes alight with excitement.

Most of them had never visited another immortal sect before.

Meng Jingzhou was also delighted, not expecting to return to the Five-Elements Sect so soon.

When Qiu Jin’an had used Meng Jingzhou’s body to strike Grandpa Ba with the Single’s Curse Fist, he promised to teach Meng Jingzhou a five-elements spell. Four months ago, Meng Jingzhou had gone to the Five-Elements Sect to learn a powerful spell from Qiu Jin’an, though he hadn’t yet found an opportunity to use it on Lu Yang.

“So who’s coming to our sect this time?”

“Shi Chan from the Hanging Monastery.”

Lu Yang had long heard of Shi Chan. It was said that Shi Chan was still working at a slaughterhouse, butchering pigs. I wonder how that’s going.

“Get ready then. You’ll set off in two days.”

“Which elder is leading us?” Lu Yang asked. Logically speaking, there should be someone leading the team. The sect can’t possibly send five juniors alone. That wouldn’t fit the rules.

“First Elder hasn’t returned since he last impersonated our shifu. Second Elder volunteered, but the Five-Elements Sect refused. Due to unresolved issues from the past, the other elders fear retaliation if they go alone.

“Therefore, you’ll be going to the Five-Elements Sect without a supervising elder this time.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does this trip suddenly feel so perilous? We wouldn’t be walking in and getting carried out, right?

“It’s fine. I’ve been to the Five-Elements Sect before. I’ll lead all of you.” Meng Jingzhou immediately stepped forth, seizing the chance to become team leader.

Lu Yang eyed him skeptically, suspecting that Meng Jingzhou was plotting against him. “Are you even reliable?”

“More than you.”

“Fine then.”

Lu Yang didn’t argue with Meng Jingzhou. After all, we have no better options.

“The Five-Elements Sect’s philosophy contains valuable insights worth adopting. Learn what you can,” Yun Zhi advised.”

The five chorused in agreement.

“Five elements, huh? Speaking of which, the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit is somewhat related to the five elements,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mused.

“What was the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit?”

“The Yin-Yang Dao Fruit. It represents the extremes in the world—scorching heat and bitter cold, rapid speed and utter stillness, strength and weakness, and so forth. Its applications are complex and can’t be explained in just a few sentences.”

“And what about the Qilin Immortal’s Dao Fruit?”

“Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit. Simply put, any technique used against him cannot be used a second time. For example, if you strike him with Cosmos in Palm, slamming him to the ground or absorbing him into your palm, his Dao Fruit would quickly adapt to that technique. If you attempt the same move again, it will no longer be effective.

“Once, when the Nine-Layers Immortal seared the Qilin Immortal with the world’s most scorching flames, the Qilin Immortal wailed in agony. However, the next time this move was unleashed, the Qilin Immortal could dance and bathe within the sea of flames.”

“So the Qilin Immortal won?”

“No. The Nine-Layers Immortal recorded the Qilin Immortal bathing and blackmailed the Qilin Immortal into surrendering.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Why does the way you immortals fight and win not quite like what I’d envisioned?

“Then, was the Qilin Immortal fine after eating your cooking?” Doesn’t this imply that the Qilin Immortal would develop immunity after getting poisoned by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy once?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy was baffled. “What do you mean by whether he was fine?! Are you insinuating that he’d get sick of eating my cooking? No, that’s impossible! As an immortal chef, I strive for innovation and make every meal a unique culinary creation!”

Lu Yang thought, Actually, Immortal Fairy, the Qilin Immortal might have preferred for you not to innovate.

“One more thing. I remember the dragon and phoenix prodigies lost to the Qilin Immortal when vying to become immortals. Were there fixed quotas for immortals?” This had long perplexed him. Is there a need to compete to become immortals? What were those people in ancient times really fighting over?

“No, that’s not the case. It was simply because those two little lasses’ Dao Fruits conflicted with the Qilin Immortal’s.”

“Conflicted?

“One of their Incipient Dao Fruits was called ‘Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit,’ and the other was called ‘Law of the Jungle Incipient Dao Fruit.’ Both embody rules rather close to the Qilin Immortal’s, don’t they?

“It’s just like how only one Everlasting Dao Fruit may exist. As long as I’m around, no Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit can ever become a true Dao Fruit.

“When the rules are similar, only one Dao Fruit can exist. Thus, it was destined that only one among the three could become an immortal. The other two can at best become half-immortals who are infinitely close to immortals, but never true immortals.”

Chapter 526: I Was Wrong, But I’d Dare Do It Again

“So that’s how it is.” Once again, Lu Yang learned another bit of knowledge that was currently useless to him.

He mused, “There’s only one Dao Fruit given a set of similar rules. That is to say that with you around, Immortal Fairy, things like the Undying Dao Fruit, the Indestructible Dao Fruit, or the Eternal Dao Fruit can only remain in their incipient states, never maturing into a true Dao Fruit?

“And with the Epoch Immortal’s existence, does that mean there’s only one mature Dao Fruit related to time as well?”

“That’s the principle,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy affirmed.

Only then did Lu Yang understand. No wonder immortal ascension was a competition. It’s akin to one Dao Fruit occupying the position at the finish line. Everyone wants to race toward it—first come, first served. Latecomers who wish to become an immortal will have to find another endpoint.

Given the overwhelming power of immortals, half-immortals stood no chance of rising up against them.

“Back when I was still a half-immortal, four or five other half-immortals owned Dao Fruits similar to mine, things like the Undying Incipient Dao Fruit, the Indestructible Incipient Dao Fruit, and whatnot you mentioned.

“When they heard I might be a threat, they gathered a whole group and stormed over menacingly. Scary as hell, I tell you.

“Fortunately, I wasn’t some pushover either. Dealing with them was a piece of cake.”

Lu Yang thought to himself, The Immortal Fairy really is impressive. I shouldn’t be fooled by how she usually has fun bullying Foundation Establishment cultivators with her Golden Core cultivation. When she faces opponents of the same realm, she’ll undoubtedly be like me—unbeatable among peers.

Otherwise, she couldn’t have formed the Unbeatable Golden Core.

Generally, the higher one’s cultivation, the harder it became to determine who was stronger among peers of the same realm. Yet the Immortal Fairy had managed to take on four half-immortals single-handedly. Such combat prowess was downright heaven-defying!

“Immortal Fairy, how did you defeat them? By self-detonation?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand smugly. “Why make it so troublesome? I simply called the other four immortals to come help me beat them up. They were already immortals by then.”

Four immortals against four half-immortals—the outcome is a foregone conclusion.

Lu Yang was at a loss for words. Immortal Fairy, don’t tell me you could still use the Unbeatable Golden Core even as a half-immortal?

“Speaking of which, Immortal Fairy, weren’t you the last to become an immortal?” Lu Yang recalled the Everlasting Immortal Fairy once mentioning she was the last to ascend.

Considering that she was at the Golden Core Stage when she fought the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Nine-Layers Immortal at the Foundation Establishment Stage, her cultivation progress should have been faster.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy replied, “Technically, I should have been the first. But at the time, the Epoch Immortal’s words inspired me. I abandoned my original Incipient Dao Fruit and changed course entirely, condensing a brand new one—the Everlasting Incipient Dao Fruit. That’s why I fell behind, letting those four surpass me.”

Just as Lu Yang sank into thought, Yun Zhi’s icy voice jolted him, sending a shiver down his spine.

“Senior, have you been telling Little Junior Brother about matters regarding Dao Fruits again?”

Only then did Lu Yang realize that while he and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy were talking, Meng Jingzhou and the others had already left. Now, only the dazed him and Yun Zhi remained.

And Big Senior Sister is staring at me with clear displeasure.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hands frantically, pointing at Lu Yang. “It wasn’t me! Lu Yang asked first!” Never mind whether it’s true—absolving myself of blame comes first.

Lu Yang wasn’t about to let the Everlasting Immortal Fairy shift the blame. “It was the Immortal Fairy who brought it up first! She told me that seeing the Five Elements reminded her of the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit, and then she started explaining!”

An internal strife had broken out within the Everlasting Lineage.

Yun Zhi was stunned, then asked, “What was the Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit?”

Her knowledge of ancient times came solely from ancient texts. Due to the immortal trait, even explicit records of their battles would automatically omit details of immortal methods. Yun Zhi could only make educated guesses based on fragmented clues. But naturally, her conjectures couldn’t compare to the firsthand account of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy herself.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal possessed the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, and the Qilin Immortal possessed the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit.”

Yun Zhi nodded. “That more or less aligns with my deductions. In other words, among the Five Ancient Immortals, you held the Everlasting Dao Fruit, the Heaven Mandate Immortal held the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit, the Nine-Layers Immortal held the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, the Epoch Immortal held the Epoch Dao Fruit, and the Qilin Immortal held the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit.”

Five individuals ascending to immortals in such close succession spoke volumes about the splendor of that era. It was no wonder people compared the ancient era with the upcoming Great Era.

Yun Zhi reminded Lu Yang, “Also, be mindful when you’re speaking with Senior. You’re only at the Golden Core Stage. Knowing too much about Dao Fruits in advance isn’t good for you. Understanding the cultivation methods of Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators will suffice for now.”

Lu Yang felt that it wasn’t good for him to know about matters of Fusion and Transcendent Tribulation cultivators either. These are simply far beyond what a Golden Core cultivator should know.

~~~

Two days later, with Meng Jingzhou leading the team and Lu Yang bringing up the rear, the five rising stars of the Dao-Seeking Sect’s young generation set off for the Five-Elements Sect.

Considering the dangers lurking within the Five-Elements Sect, the old horse’s strength was deemed insufficient. Instead of riding a carriage, Meng Jingzhou opted to “share the joys and sorrows of common folk,” traveling with Lu Yang and the others on a flying vessel.

“I didn’t expect to board a flying vessel again so soon.” Less than half a month had passed since Lu Yang boarded one.

“Sorry, sorry, I’m late!” Tao Yaoye was the last to arrive, making it right before the flying vessel departed.

Shi Huagu’s promotional illusion had been completed ahead of schedule. She and Sixth Elder had made a trip to the flagship One More Time Barbeque Shop to collect the promotional illusion and the remaining forty million spirit stones.

The spirit stones went to her, while the task of merging the promotional illusion with the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage was handed to Sixth Elder, who enlisted the help of Grandpa Ba and Eighth Elder.

The back-and-forth had nearly made her miss the departure.

Li Haoran was secretly envious. My peers are not only stronger in cultivation and talent, but also successful in their ventures. And even if they aren’t, they have ancestral legacies to lean on, like Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu.

In contrast, I’m dead broke. And if I reclaim my past life’s identity as the Nine-Netherworlds Creed Leader...I’ll probably end up even poorer.

As Li Haoran’s cultivation progressed, he inherited half of Qin Haoran’s memories. The more memories he obtained, the more he empathized with Qin Haoran’s struggles.

Inevitably, among these memories were also Qin Haoran’s...intimate moments with Su Yiren...

At those times, Li Haoran’s empathy evaporated.

Lu Yang consoled him. “Junior Brother Li, don’t put yourself down. Your potential isn’t inferior to mine. If you ever inherit Qin Haoran’s identity, you could rival me in at least one aspect.”

Li Haoran’s eyes lit up with hope as he stared at Lu Yang. “What is it?”

“You’d have roughly as many enemies as I do. Qin Haoran’s enemies were all at the Fusion Stage, and I also often run into Fusion opponents when I’m out.”

Li Haoran, “...”

Please, no. Senior Brother Lu, you’re a scourge with other scourges as your nemesis. Scourges don’t die easily; you always turn disaster into fortune, escaping unscathed. But I don’t have that kind of ability.

~~~

Fortunately, it was an uneventful journey, and the five arrived safely at the Five-Elements Sect.

Before they could disembark, they spotted the Five-Elements Sect’s members standing at the mountain gates to welcome the five of them. Among them were several figures who looked unmistakably like elders wielding magical treasures with fearsome expressions. They gazed steadily—or rather, glared fiercely—at the descending flying vessel.

Chapter 527: The Hospitable Five-Elements Sect

The Five-Elements Sect, one of the Five Great Immortal Sects, was situated upon the Five-Elements Spirit Vein in Yun Province. The spirit vein was naturally attuned to the five elements and considered the finest location in the region.

Under the leadership of Sect Leader Qiu Jin’an, the Five-Elements Sect flourished with talent, presenting a thriving and prosperous scene. Internally, the sect maintained strict discipline, demanded rigorous cultivation, and possessed a competitive spirit for excellence. Externally, they were known for their warm hospitality and amiable demeanor.

Even when disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect came to study, the Five-Elements Sect set aside past grievances. Elders personally led the welcoming entourage with magical treasures in hand, worried their guests from the Dao-Seeking Sect wouldn’t encounter any mishaps.

“We’re really popular, huh? So many people came out to greet us.” Man Gu grinned as he observed the crowd gathered at the sect’s entrance.

Lu Yang’s eyes twitched nonstop. From what the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had told him, those holding magical treasures were all at the Fusion Stage, undoubtedly the sect’s elders.

Do they really need to bring magical treasures when welcoming us?

After the flying vessel docked, Meng Jingzhou led the group to disembark.

Qiu Jin’an stepped forward to warmly greet them, followed by five elders with fierce eyes resembling a tiger’s. One of them held a horizontal banner in their left hand and a weapon in their right, seemingly up to something.

“Welcome to our Five-Elements Sect for your study visit! Are there no supervising elders with you?” Qiu Jin’an counted only five people. None of the Dao-Seeking Nine are here.

Refusing to believe it, he swept the surroundings with his spiritual consciousness, checking for anyone concealing their presence.

“No, the elders had other matters to attend to and couldn’t come,” Meng Jingzhou answered truthfully.

Qiu Jin’an shook his head regretfully. What a pity. Why did no one come walking into the trap today?

Behind him, the five elders activated their magical treasures, the tips glowing ominously. Meng Jingzhou nearly jumped out of his skin. Luckily, their magical treasures aren’t aimed at us but at the sky.

Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom! Boom!

Five attacks exploded in the air, bursting like resplendent New Year’s fireworks across the night sky.

Amid the sounds of detonations, the horizontal banner unfurled: Welcome, Disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect, to Our Sect for Study!

The Five-Elements Sect was meticulous, preparing two contingencies. If the Dao-Seeking Nine had come, they would have greeted them with the magical treasures, then trampled them underfoot while unfurling the banner and setting off fireworks. If Yun Zhi had come, they would have skipped straight to the fireworks and welcome banner.

Although Yun Zhi hadn’t turned up, and only a few juniors came, the banner and fireworks would make do. freewebnovel.com

“Disperse, disperse. The old Taciturn scoundrel and his gang didn’t come.”

“I heard the old Taciturn scoundrel was spotted in Wilderness Province. Should we check it out?”

“Forget it. It’s probably another false lead. When have we ever caught him after catching wind of his whereabouts?”

“This grandson is slippery and runs faster than a rabbit!”

“Person and Sword as One, One Sword Into Ten Thousand Swords—if he unleashes these two moves in succession, he would be gone by the time you find his real body.”

“Actually, if I run into him, I could find him.”

“How?”

“See these eyes of mine? I jumped into a furnace for forty-nine days to smoke them. They’re now comparable to the White Horse Temple’s Demon-Revealing Mirror!”

“That effective? Is it easy to achieve it? Maybe I’ll try burning my eyes too.”

The elders muttered among themselves and went off after displaying the banner and launching the fireworks.

Seeing his targets hadn’t tagged along, Qiu Jin’an cleared his throat and signaled Bai Ming with a meaningful look to take over hosting duties.

The sect leader and elders might have left, but the Five-Elements Sect’s disciples remained.

“Which one is Lu Yang? Point him out to me.”

“It’s that one! The clean-cut guy there.”

“Looks can be deceiving. I heard he challenged beyond his level, defeating Golden Core, Nascent Soul, and Divine Transfiguration cultivators while still at the Foundation Establishment Stage. Now that he’s at the Golden Core Stage, could he defeat a Void Refinement cultivator?”

“You need him to fight a Void Refinement cultivator? Pick a weakened Void Refinement cultivator, and even I could win.”

“Fair point.”

“Which one is the founder of the Dreamlike Bubble Mirage?”

“Are you blind? There’s only one female cultivator; why are you still asking?”

“Truly talented. Why didn’t I think of such a profitable idea?”

“What could you possibly come up with? After eating the skewers at the Dao-Seeking Sect, you wanted to open a shop outside, only to realize the barbeque market was already oversaturated.”

“Is that buff guy from the Ancient Barbarian Tribe? I thought they were already extinct.”

“It’s supposedly a once-in-ten-millenia bloodline atavism which traces back to the origins.”

The Five-Elements Sect disciples rarely interacted with Dao-Seeking Sect disciples, so they were extremely curious about Lu Yang’s group.

After Qiu Jin’an left, Meng Jingzhou was baffled to see Bai Ming. “You didn’t go for the study exchange?”

Bai Ming pouted. “There’s nowhere to go. Shi Chan went to your Dao-Seeking Sect, Yan Tianzhi went to the Hanging Monastery, and the Moon Laurel Immortal Palace doesn’t allow male disciples—two of my junior sisters went instead. I go to the Prison Suppression Sect too often that there’s no point. So I could only stay behind in the sect.”

As they walked, Bai Ming gave Lu Yang’s group an overview of the Five-Elements Sect.

“You probably have seen from the flying vessel that our sect is built upon the Five-Elements Spirit Vein. Based on specialization, we’re divided into five branches according to the five elements. The elders who greeted you with Shifu earlier were the chief elders of each branch. They had some personal grudges with your sect’s elders in their youth and hoped to catch up. It’s a pity your sect elders didn’t come.”

“What personal grudges?”

Bai Ming had heard his shifu mention several conflicts between the Five-Elements Sect and the Dao-Seeking Sect. “There were plenty. Frequent brawls, for one. When your sect elders outnumbered ours, they would overwhelm our sect elders with sheer numbers. When they were outnumbered, they would report us to the authorities.

“Sometimes they’d even use honey traps. Your Fourth Elder once wrote to one of our elders, posing as a female cultivator and claiming she had admired him for a long time. She even said she was shy to meet too many people and requested a private meeting. Our elder went, only for nine people to jump out from behind a boulder. Can you imagine that scene?”

Lu Yang found the tactic uncannily familiar. Did Fourth Elder learn from past setbacks and master this trick?

Li Haoran feared that the Five-Elements Sect’s elders might be eavesdropping and that Bai Ming’s words might rekindle old grudges at their expense, drawing the fire toward them instead. He hastily changed the subject. “Which branch do you belong to?”

“Me? I’m proficient in five-elements spell and don’t belong to any branch. I’m directly under the sect leader’s lineage. Only those adept at all kinds of elemental arts can become the sect leader’s disciple.” Bai Ming’s lips were tugged upward in pride. My talent is extremely rare even in the Five-Elements Sect.

“Then couldn’t I qualify too?” Lu Yang pointed to himself.

My talent in spells is exceptional. For metal-type spells, I know the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body; for wood-type spells, I know the Tree-Planting Mantra; for water-type spells, I haven’t learned any for the time being; for fire-type spells, I know the Three Flavor True Fire; and for earth-type spells, I know Shrinking Earth.

Bai Ming turned, eyeing Lu Yang with slight surprise. “With your talent in spells, you actually could. You’re pretty suitable to become Shifu’s disciple. Why didn’t you join our Five-Elements Sect back then?”

Lu Yang scratched his head awkwardly. “The Dao-Seeking Sect was closer to my house, so I figured I’d try there first. I didn’t expect to get in just like that.”

Bai Ming, “...”

What a plain reason...

Chapter 528: The Meng Family’s Attacking Methods

“This is the scripture library. It houses every book available on the market. Disciples are free to peruse the first floor, but accessing the second floor and above requires completing missions in exchange for entry.”

The Five-Elements Sect also had a Great Mission Hall. Unlike the Dao-Seeking Sect, where disciples could freely study cultivation techniques of their cultivation stage once they reached the required level, the Five-Elements Sect disciples had to complete missions to learn the cultivation techniques they desired.

This was a system established at the sect’s founding, rooted in the principle that “techniques must not be passed on lightly.” Knowledge obtained too easily would instead be undervalued, whereas results earned through effort were more treasured.

“However, since you are visiting disciples studying here, we naturally can’t demand contributions from you. As per custom, each of you may select one cultivation technique. Any more will require completing missions.

“This is the Lecture Hall. Later, the transmission elder will explain the General Principles of the Five Elements. It is a mandatory foundational course for all Five-Elements Sect disciples. Of course, we won’t force you to accept our sect’s doctrines; you can just listen. If there’s anything you don’t understand, you may ask the transmission elder at any time.

“This is the Martial Transmission Hall. Our sect disciples usually spar here.”

Dozens of massive arena stages reinforced with arrays trembled slightly as disciples clad in the Five-Elements Sect’s Daoist robes clashed fiercely with five-elements spells. The spectacle drew cheers from the crowd of disciples below.

Even from a distance, Lu Yang could feel the shockwaves from the battle, his hair fluttering faintly.

On one arena stage, the intense fight had reduced the ground to scattered rubble. A senior disciple pointed to the debris and yelled, “Pointing Stone To Gold!”

The shattered rocks transformed into dazzling gold.

Then, he enveloped all the gold with his spiritual consciousness and cast another spell. “One Throw Thousand Gold!”[1]

The shining gold morphed into a visible force, and even space warped as countless golden projectiles blasted toward his opponent.

“Is this the legendary spell that converts wealth into an attack?” Tao Yaoye gasped in astonishment. She had thought the move was lost to time, not expecting to witness it here.

Bai Ming explained, “One Throw Thousand Gold is an untransmitted spell of the Metal Branch. Its power is devastating, and Senior Brother Zhang innovated further, linking it with Pointing Stone To Gold to form a spell combo.

“However, it also has a flaw. After all, gold is a worldly item and not inherently valuable. Senior Brother Zhang could only compensate with quantity to amplify the effectiveness of the attack.”

“Great line of thinking,” Lu Yang marveled. To see such an unconventional yet brilliant idea so soon—it looks like I’ll get to learn a lot at the Five-Elements Sect.

Old Meng, do you want to learn this spell?” Lu Yang felt that Meng Jingzhou was best suited to learn One Throw Thousand Gold. Since gold, silver, jewelry, and spirit stones can be transmuted into gold, just imagine the destructive potential if Meng Jingzhou could unleash it.

Meng Jingzhou shook his head with a frown. “Our Meng Family knows One Throw Thousand Gold too. But our ancestral teachings forbid us from learning this spell. It’s a forbidden spell.”

“Why?” Lu Yang was bewildered.

“Can you imagine a son arguing with his father and suddenly blowing through his father’s entire fortune of spirit stones with One Throw Thousand Gold?

“That fellow put on a show flashier than the New Year’s fireworks. It was in the middle of the night, yet the imperial city looked like it was daytime. And the noise was so insanely loud that no one could fall asleep. Eventually, an angry mob surrounded our Meng Estate.”

Normally, the Meng Family offended one household at a time. But this time, they had offended the entire imperial city in one go. Even the Meng Family couldn’t withstand that many enemies.

Lu Yang, “...”

When I visit the imperial city in the future, I’ll definitely say I don’t know you. I don’t want to get beaten up without even knowing who did it.

Meng Jingzhou continued, “Moreover, our Meng Family has more sophisticated spells. There’s no need to learn this one.”

“More sophisticated spells?” Lu Yang grew increasingly curious.

The Meng Family to the imperial city was like the Taciturn Daoist Priest to all Fusion cultivators—they made so many enemies that one would go bald trying to count them. Despite that, they stood unshaken for a hundred thousand years and bore the title of “number one ancestral clan.” Clearly, the saying that “scourges last ten thousand years” was true.

“I don’t understand the specific principles behind this spell, but I can explain how it’s used. Basically, you throw a pile of spirit stones at your opponent during battle, transferring the ownership from the Meng Family to them. Then, you demand immediate repayment. If they refuse, heavenly punishment will descend with thunderous force that strikes them dead!”

Lu Yang’s expression turned peculiar. Why does this sound so familiar?

“Oh right, the heavenly punishment is called ‘Pay-Your-Debts-With-Your-Life Lightning.”

Lu Yang found the name of the heavenly punishment rather familiar too.

He glanced at Meng Jingzhou, then at Li Haoran, who was still watching the spectacle completely unaware. Could it be that Qin Haoran had borrowed money from the Meng Family back then?

Lu Yang ultimately chose not to expose this matter, lest it damage the camaraderie between these two senior and junior brothers. This is my duty as Big Senior Brother.

Based on the memories Li Haoran inherited from Qin Haoran, either Li Haoran hasn’t recalled who Qin Haoran had borrowed from, or the Meng Family had used false identities when lending the money as loan sharks back then.

Forget it, it has been so long. Qin Haoran is already dead, and the debt now belongs to Vice Creed Leader Shi. Let bygones be bygones.

Bai Ming looked at Meng Jingzhou with a strange expression. “No wonder your Meng Family made so many enemies. Just this combat method alone is truly wicked.”

Meng Jingzhou retorted with righteous conviction, defending the Meng Family’s dignity. “What nonsense! This is called making reasonable use of heavenly punishment. Is there anything wrong with utilizing natural laws? Hasn’t every advancement of mankind come from understanding and applying natural principles?”

Bai Ming led the five to a scorching hot area, where flames occasionally spurted from the ground. “Can I cultivate here?” Li Haoran felt this place was practically tailor-made for him.

Bai Ming showed a troubled expression and said hesitantly, “Your shifu is Elder Zhou Xin, right?”
