Chapter 529: Artifact Refinement Competition

Compared to Lu Yang, Li Haoran had always counted himself lucky to have a relatively dependable shifu. Although this reliable shifu had once tossed me into molten lava, it had solely been to help me better understand the arcane wonders of my Fire Spirit Root.

Never in my wildest dreams had I imagined my great shifu would have enemies within the Five-Elements Sect.

And an entire Fire Branch at that.

Bai Ming patted Li Haoran’s shoulder. “Don’t worry, this is just an exception. I’ve heard Elder Zhou Xin is well-connected in the artifact refinement community and gets along with many people.”

This was the truth. Fifth Elder’s artifact refinement skills were unparalleled in the cultivation world, and his reputation was impeccable. Artifact-refining masters were often evaluated by the number of patents registered under their name, and Fifth Elder held the record for most patents secured. These patents had amassed him staggering wealth, and even Seventh Elder, a pill-concocting master, couldn’t rival Fifth Elder when it came to spirit stones.

Of course, Fifth Elder’s wealth still paled beside the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s. It wasn’t because the Taciturn Daoist Priest currently owned a fortune, but simply that his bounty on the black market was worth a fortune.

“What are those people doing?”

Lu Yang spotted several near-naked senior male disciples lying prone on the scorching earth, eyes closed in concentration. Their bodies glistened under the sun, seemingly coated with a layer of liquid.

A severed tree branch was planted in the ground beside them. The last time he had seen such a sight was during beach sunbathing in his previous life.

“Oh, them? Is it so hard to understand? They’re comprehending the meaning of the sun. Through the Fire Branch Elder’s research, it was discovered that greater skin exposure to sunlight increases the probability of epiphany.

“That tree branch was brought back by Shifu from Wilderness Province. Apparently, it’s a fragment of the Fusang Tree, spoils from defeating an archaic cultivator. It is tremendously helpful for comprehending the essence of the sun. What you see coated on their bodies is a specially formulated ointment.”

“An ointment that enhances comprehension of the sun’s meaning?”

“It’s sunscreen.”

Lu Yang quietly withdrew his gaze. The Five-Elements Sect’s cultivation methods are certainly unique...

“Come, I’ll show you the Water Branch’s cultivation grounds.”

Before they could set off, cultivators bearing flame symbols on their foreheads strode toward the group in an imposing manner.

“Which one is Li Haoran?”

“What are you trying to do?” Meng Jingzhou frowned slightly, stepping forward to shield everyone else.

“So you are Li Haoran?” The cultivator with the flame mark eyed Meng Jingzhou.

Bai Ming interposed himself between both parties, his tone displeased as he addressed the senior male disciples from the Fire Branch. “Senior Brother Yuan Gang and other senior brothers, what are you trying to do?”

“Nothing much. We just heard Elder Zhou Xin’s prized disciple was visiting and wanted to see what he looks like.”

“They’re our guests,” Bai Ming stated.

Yuan Gang replied lazily, “I know. I wasn’t planning to fight.”

“I am Li Haoran.” Now that the matter had escalated to this point, Li Haoran stepped forward without letting others speak up for him further.

“So you are Fire Spirit Root Li Haoran. Never judge someone by their appearance indeed. I heard you’re an exceptional artifact-refining master who has inherited Elder Zhou Xin’s true teachings. Is that true?”

“True or false—does it matter?”

Yuan Gang’s eyes gleamed sharply. “It doesn’t matter. My cultivation surpasses yours by a minor realm. Beating you would be meaningless. How about we compete with our artifact-refining skills instead?”

“Senior Brother Yuan Gang, Li Haoran is a guest,” Bai Ming reminded him again.

Yuan Gang chuckled. “Exchanging artifact-refining techniques lets him learn our Five-Elements Sect’s artifact-refining methods. What’s wrong with that?”

“Compete in artifact refinement? Sure.” When it came to artifact-refining skills, Li Haoran feared no one.

“See? Even Li Haoran himself agrees.”

“When do we compete?”

“There’s no time like the present. Everyone can be a witness.”

As tensions rose between both parties, more Five-Elements Sect disciples gathered; even those sunbathing came over.

“Well, well, what’s happening?”

“It's probably Yuan Gang standing up to win back honor for the Fire Branch Elder with an artifact-refinement duel.”

“Did the other party accept?”

“He did.”

“This will be exciting to watch. Even the elders praise Yuan Gang’s artifact-refining skills all the time, saying he’s a future artifact-refining grandmaster.”

“Absolutely.”

Yuan Gang smiled while surveying his surroundings, then fixed his gaze on Li Haoran. “Well? Shall we begin now, or should I give you preparation time?”

“What preparations? We can begin now. Say it, what are we competing in?”

After some consideration, Yuan Gang said earnestly, “Artifact refinement ultimately serves cultivators, and what cultivators value most is power. Why don’t we compete to see whose creation unleashes greater power?”

“How is the power measured?”

Yuan Gang pointed at a few red boulders in the distance. “Those are Lava Essence Stones, formed when lava from volcanic eruptions is condensed by a mighty expert’s great power. They are extremely sturdy. The winner will be determined by who deals greater damage to them, with a maximum charging time of no more than one hundred breaths.”

The longer a magical treasure was charged, the greater its destructive power. Without a limit on its charging time, the competition would simply become a test of whose artifact could be charged the longest.

“It’s a deal then.”

“Say, can the two of us participate as well?” A soft chuckle rang out as Yuan Gang noticed Lu Yang raising his hand with a smile and Meng Jingzhou standing beside him.

“You two know artifact-refining techniques too?” Yuan Gang eyed them skeptically. While he certainly recognized Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou, he had never heard of them being adept at artifact refinement.

“We’re passable. Defeating you shouldn’t be a big problem,” Meng Jingzhou replied cheerfully.

Yuan Gang laughed in his fit of anger. “Impressive courage! It’s my first time hearing someone claim they can beat me in artifact-refining skills! Well then, let me see what you’re really capable of!”

Bai Ming was perplexed and secretly transmitted an auditory message to Man Gu and Tao Yaoye. “Do they really know how to refine artifacts?”

Man Gu shook his head blankly, while Tao Yaoye remained silent, her thoughts drifting back to their sect’s entrance trials two years ago.

Their ambiguous responses only deepened Bai Ming’s confusion.

Yuan Gang signaled one of his lackeys, who produced an extensive collection of artifact-refining materials from his identity jade tablet: refined steel, ironwood, agate, pure yin water...

“These are raw materials for artifact refinement, available for use during the competition. Common materials are unlimited, but the precious materials aren’t sufficient, so it will come down to who grabs them first.”

Lu Yang quipped, “I’ve never seen such a fair competition before. You’re the one who proposed it, set the terms, and now say there aren’t enough materials and we have to fight for them. I trust you won’t mind if I use some minor spells?”

Yuan Gang acted as if he didn’t hear Lu Yang’s sarcasm and replied calmly, “Up to you. Are you still competing or not?”

Lu Yang’s smile didn’t waver. “Of course, we’ll compete! How else would you witness our amazing artifact-refining skills? Since it’s a competition, what are the stakes? Surely not mere pride, right?”

“If I lose, you may choose any true fire from our Fire Branch’s cultivation grounds.

“If you lose, you shall not cultivate in the Fire Branch’s territory for your entire stay at the Five-Elements Sect!”

Chapter 530: Shattered Stones!

The artifact refinement competition began.

Yuan Gang had long decided what magical treasure he wanted to craft and was the first to act, swiftly snatching several extremely precious materials.

Li Haoran closed his eyes in deep contemplation, mulling over the kind of weapon he should forge to unleash devastating power.

Meng Jingzhou picked out a few materials from the pile with an air of solemnness.

Lu Yang cast a sidelong glance at the frantic Yuan Gang and sneered, then hoisted a log from the pile of materials onto his shoulder.

News of the four competing quickly reached the higher-ups of the Five-Elements Sect. The elders of the five branches and Qiu Jin’an appeared at the scene, though they concealed their presence and went unnoticed by everyone else.

“Old Song, Yuan Gang is your arrangement, isn’t he? This is going a bit too far.” Qiu Jin’an frowned at Fire Branch Elder, Song Duantian.

Song Duantian, portly and clad in a bright red Daoist robe, looked almost comical, but no one dared laugh, knowing his temper and battle achievements.

“Don’t speak nonsense, Sect Leader. Yuan Gang is just a filial disciple acting on his own. How is it my arrangement?”

Qiu Jin’an chuckled dryly but said nothing more. Do they really think Yuan Gang is guaranteed to win?

The conflict between Zhou Xin and Song Duantian ran deeper than just fighting over a true flame. Over a thousand years ago, both had fallen for the same female cultivator and pursued her ardently. With the guidance of the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Zhou Xin successfully won her heart, and the two later had a daughter named Zhou Lulu.

Time alone couldn’t resolve the rift between them.

Of course, Zhou Xin flaunting his wife in front of Song Duan Tian every day, especially in the past few decades after Zhou Lulu’s birth, and bringing his whole family to visit during the New Year is admittedly a bit much.

Time passed second by second. The venue was almost draped in silence, the only sounds being the clanging of hammers and crackling of true flames as the four were fully absorbed in forging their magical treasures.

“Done!” Yuan Gang felt a burden was off his shoulders. Though he appeared arrogant and provocative earlier, he was wholly focused and meticulous when crafting his magical treasure. Even with full concentration, he hadn’t been entirely confident in completing his planned magical treasure.

But now that it’s completed, victory is certain.

In his hands was a cylindrical object forged primarily from bronze. It was hollow in the center, and its inner and outer walls were carved with intricate inscriptions.

“What magical treasure is this?”

“It looks so strange.”

“Has anyone seen it before?” freewebnovel.com

The Five-Elements Sect disciples whispered among themselves as they discussed this creation they had never seen before.

“I call it the Meteor Cannon.” This was a weapon he had designed, now unveiled in public for the first time.

Li Haoran acted as if he didn’t hear Yuan Gang’s words and continued crafting his magical treasure with single-minded focus.

The flame in his palm writhed like a fire serpent, melting and shaping every inch of the magical treasure. This was the Extreme Calculation True Fire he had mastered, not the most powerful, but the most suitable for refining artifacts. Its flexible nature enabled the greatest precision in forging his planned magical treasure.

Yuan Gang was disappointed that he didn’t break Li Haoran’s concentration. Standing firm, he hefted the cannon and continuously channeled spirit energy into it. The inscriptions along its surface flickered, gathering the spirit energy and directing it to the base, which turned from green to red as a terrifying force brewed within.

Thirty breaths...forty breaths...ninety breaths...one hundred breaths!

Standing nearby, Bai Ming felt his hair stand on end as he sensed the impending threat. If I take a direct hit, I’m afraid I’ll be severely wounded.

“Let me show you the mighty power of the Meteor Cannon!”

Boom!

The cannon roared like thunder, immediately drowning out Yuan Gang’s laughter. Searing spirit energy shot forth, seeming to carry the force of ten thousand thunderbolts as it smashed into the Lava Essence Stone.

Cracks like a spider’s web instantly spread across the boulder.

Gasps erupted from the crowd.

“Oy my Heaven, what kind of power is this?!”

“A Basic Nascent Soul cultivator could damage a Lava Essence Stone?!”

“What an incredible magical treasure!”

“This fellow Yuan Gang really made us proud.” Song Duantian grinned smugly, feeling that the cannon’s destructive power brought him pride.

Yuan Gang shot a triumphant look at Li Haoran, who had also finished forging his magical treasure. It was a needle as thin as an ox’s hair and nearly invisible to the naked eye. Alongside it was a millstone-sized disk engraved with intricate and complex inscriptions that made Yuan Gang dizzy at just a glance.

Li Haoran placed the ox-hair needle at the disk’s edge and infused it with spirit energy to activate it.

Rings of inscriptions lit up as the needle levitated above the disk’s rim, slowly circling, as if an invisible force was tying it down.

“That’s all...?” Yuan Gang sneered. But before he could finish, he saw the ox-hair needle’s speed increase with each round.

At sixty breaths, the needle was almost a blur. At seventy breaths, Yuan Gang could no longer track it.

Eighty breaths...ninety breaths...one hundred breaths!

At the hundredth breath, the disk’s spirit energy vanished. Now unrestrained, the ox-hair needle shot toward the Lava Essence Stone at a blinding speed!

Ssshk!

A soft sound rang out as the needle pierced clean through three stones before embedding itself in the fourth, its tail not even quivering. Three Lava Essence Stones were skewered in a row, each with a hole no wider than a strand of ox hair!

“Senior Brother Yuan Gang, thank you for letting me win.” Li Haoran cupped his hands with a faint smile.

Yuan Gang refused to admit defeat. “The competition is about who deals more damage. My cracks formed such a huge spider web, while you’ve only managed such a tiny hole. That’s worse than me.”

Li Haoran was just about to argue with him when Meng Jingzhou’s laughter cut in. “Comparing the damage, eh? Then let me have a go. Don’t pull any tricks and wiggle your way out this time.”

Yuan Gang frowned. Meng Jingzhou isn’t even holding an artifact—just a rope. What is he planning?

Without explaining anything, Meng Jingzhou tied the rope around the essence stone, gripped one end of the rope, and then flew higher and higher until he vanished from sight. Only an indistinct voice from the sky could be heard.

“I wonder how high I need to fly to drop and break this stone.”

Yuan Gang bellowed in rage, “You only have a hundred breaths!” He never imagined someone could smash the stone with brute force.

Meng Jingzhou’s unhurried voice replied, “But I’m not using a magical treasure. The time limit of a hundred breaths only applies to magical treasures, not me.”

It was unclear how much time had passed until a meteor streaked down from the sky, blazing with heat and light as it hurtled straight toward Yuan Gang. The visual impact alone was staggering.

Yuan Gang hastily dodged.

Boom!

The essence stone shattered into fragments. The collision kicked up a cloud of dust and created a massive crater in the Fire Branch’s grounds, causing Song Duantian’s face to twitch in pain.

Meng Jingzhou landed, clicking his tongue as he shook his head. “Aiya, and here I thought your ‘Meteor Cannon’ could actually shatter stars. I overestimated you.”

Yuan Gang’s face was stormy. This brat had aimed for me on purpose!

Meng Jingzhou turned around. “Lu Yang, you done yet?”

“Finished ages ago. I was just waiting for the stone to drop.” Lu Yang blew wood shavings off his sword. He had crafted a wooden blade that would snap once anyone tried to bend it.

Yuan Gang’s face was stormy and frowning, unable to fathom what Lu Yang was trying to do.

Lu Yang smiled as he walked toward another essence stone. He raised his sword in a slow and graceful manner, exuding a distinct beauty.

“I heard he’s a sword cultivator. What is he planning? Is he trying to shatter the stone with that sword?”

“Impossible! That stone can’t be broken by a Golden Core cultivator, even if they’re a sword cultivator!”

It wasn’t just the disciples; even the five branch elders and Qiu Jin’an couldn’t discern his intentions, though the movements seemed uncannily familiar.

Lu Yang’s swordplay flowed with immortal elegance. He seemed to have transformed into a different person as a smug smile played on his lips.

Suddenly, sword light flashed, and Lu Yang’s appearance changed completely.

“Haha, you Five-Elements Sect fools! You can’t even recognize me borrowing my little disciple’s identity? And you still want to catch me with such poor eyesight? Why bother cultivating some fiery golden eyes? You’re terribly blind!”

The Taciturn Daoist Priest cackled, mocking the six people hiding in the dark.

Taciturn Daoist Priest Animal Form Fist!

Boom! Boom!

A colossal fireball materialized above the Taciturn Daoist Priest like a second sun, while metallic energies crisscrossed like an armored cavalry charging forward and slaughtering all foes.

The hot-tempered Fire Branch and Metal Branch elders attacked immediately. Fireballs and metallic energies crashed down, burying the essence stones. The essence stones didn’t even get the chance to turn to power—they were simply obliterated into nothingness.

It wasn’t that they couldn’t tell this “Taciturn Daoist Priest” was a fake, but they couldn’t help themselves.

Especially this tone. It’s too much like him.

Chapter 531: Ten Suns High in the Sky

Under the relentless bombardment of fireballs and metallic energy, the entire Fire Vein trembled as if on the verge of collapse. A fierce gale swept past, dispersing the smoke and dust, revealing a massive crater in the ground. All the Lava Essence Stones had been annihilated into nothingness; even the Taciturn Daoist Priest had disintegrated.

“Your Five-Elements Sect elders are really ruthless, huh?” Lu Yang clicked his tongue, appearing beside Meng Jingzhou. What on earth did Shifu do to provoke such fury from the Five-Elements Sect?

Yuan Gang nearly jumped out of his skin when he saw Lu Yang, as if he had seen a ghost. “How are you here? Who was that just now?”

Lu Yang lazily replied, “A clone, obviously. Couldn’t you tell? It was a wooden clone. Isn’t a wooden clone a perfect match for a wooden sword?”

If not for that, the Fire Branch and Metal Branch elders wouldn’t have attacked with such overwhelming force.

Had I used my real body to turn into Shifu, I wouldn’t even know how I’d died.

“Heh, as expected of disciples from the Dao-Seeking Sect. They’re quick-witted.” Song Duantian’s hearty laughter echoed from an isolated space as the Fire Branch elders and Qiu Jin’an emerged one by one.

“Yuan Gang, you must know that beyond every person is a greater person, and beyond every sky is a higher sky. Learn from this lesson and never let your arrogance get the better of you.”

Setting aside Meng Jingzhou’s manipulation of the continent’s gravity and Lu Yang’s provocation by transforming into the Taciturn Daoist Priest, even Li Haoran’s infinitely accelerating ox-hair needle showcased a concept of artifact refinement that far surpassed Yuan Gang’s capabilities.

“Yes, Shifu. Your disciple will remember this lesson.” Yuan Gang tactfully retreated.

“This match goes to your Dao-Seeking Sect,” Song Duantian conceded. “That foolish disciple of mine promised you could freely pick a true fire here, and that prize still stands. This is your fated opportunity. You may select from our Fire Branch, but each of you has only one chance. Whether you succeed in mastering it and whether you comprehend its arcane meaning depends entirely on you.” He chuckled, not thinking much of it.

What’s true fire? They’re something even Golden Core cultivators struggle to grasp. Even if gifted individuals could grasp true fire, with a hundred and eight varieties in existence, how could they possibly learn them all?

The only way to grasp true fire is by finding one most suited to themselves. As for what’s considered “most suited,” that’s not what humans can decide—it’s completely up to fate.

Song Duantian snapped his fingers. The ground cracked open, crimson soil crumbling inward as plumes of white smoke surged out, and the air grew blisteringly hot.

Clusters of true fires emerged—some ethereal and shrouded in mist, some emitting the mellifluous cry of a phoenix, and others resembling blooming crimson lotuses and concealing mysterious profundities...

“Hundun-Chaos True Fire, Nirvana True Fire...” Li Haoran muttered the names in awe. These true fires have immense power and solid foundations, a tier higher than those Shifu commands.

Song Duantian smirked with pride. “How could the true fires collected by the likes of Zhou Xin compare to this esteemed one’s? These are the accumulations of my Five-Elements Sect’s Fire Branch over a hundred thousand years!”

Indeed, a single individual’s collection couldn’t rival an entire sect’s accumulation of a hundred thousand years.

The Five-Elements Sect disciples watched with envy. How many missions would we have to complete to earn just one true fire?

“Although you two didn’t compete, you are still disciples of the Dao-Seeking Sect. Come and choose.”

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu hadn’t expected to be included. However, they were neither fire-type cultivators nor did they possess Lu Yang’s heaven-defying comprehension. They weren’t certain whether they could obtain a suitable true fire.

“Is this the Six Ding Divine Fire?” Li Haoran paused before a ball of flame, his eyes sparkling with excitement.

The Six Ding Divine Fire is another true fire ideal for artifact refinement. The martial and civil fires it encompasses, combined with its Qimen Dunjia[1] momentum, can devour impurities. It’s unparalleled for engraving inscriptions!

Fifth Elder also possessed the Six Ding Divine Fire, passed down through generations of peak masters. Li Haoran had originally planned to learn it from his shifu after returning from the Five-Elements Sect, but now that fate had presented the opportunity to learn it, he couldn’t let it slip away.

With Golden Core cultivation, one could at most master two types of true fires. Any more would become a burden instead. Since Li Haoran had already grasped the Extreme Calculations True Fire, he naturally reserved his second slot for the Six Ding Divine Fire!

“Luna True Fire?” Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou were still browsing the true fires when a white and chilling true fire caught their attention.

“Old Meng, you should learn this. With your Pure Yang True Fire, adding the Luna True Fire would complete your yin and yang!” Lu Yang nudged Meng Jingzhou with a mischievous grin.

“Get lost! With my measly cultivation, wielding both yin and yang would make me explode!”

“Phoenix Nirvana Fire?” The two soon found another location where the cries of a phoenix could vaguely be heard.

“It’s said that this is a bloodline true fire of the phoenix race, capable of rebirth through nirvana.” Meng Jingzhou studied the Phoenix Nirvana with keen interest.

But as it was a bloodline true fire, mastering it as an outsider would be fraught with difficulties.

“Don’t get your hopes up about rebirth through nirvana. That’s just a rumor,” Lu Yang said upon recalling the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s story about a phoenix’s rebirth.

“But while nirvana is fake, its healing properties are real. It suits you well.” Since Meng Jingzhou often fought with his body and suffered injuries, he could use the true fire to compensate for his vulnerabilities.

“I’ll go with this then!” Meng Jingzhou declared firmly.

That left only Lu Yang. His gaze was drawn to a blazing flame, within which the faint silhouette of a Jinwu golden crow flickered in and out of view, as if it was sentient—this was the Sun True Fire.

Also known as the Jinwu Golden Crow True Fire, it stood alongside Meng Jingzhou’s Pure Yang True Fire as one of the two supreme yang-attribute true fires, renowned for its devastating offensive power.

Ancient legends spoke of ten suns high up in the sky. Ten Jinwu golden crows took flight together, scorching the earth barren. As calamity and destruction spread, an immortal couldn’t bear to see the world in suffering and shot down nine, leaving one to illuminate the land. This alone attested to the perils of the Jinwu golden crow.

“Since my Three Flavor True Fire lacks offensive power, the Sun True Fire can make up for it,” Lu Yang murmured to himself.

“Ah, Jinwu golden crow. The Nine-Layers Immortal loved those,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy suddenly remarked.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal?”

“Mmm. Back then, he was researching the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit but hit a bottleneck, so he went around trying all sorts of methods. One of them was to find the supreme yang Jinwu Golden Crow and the supreme yin Jade Rabbit,[2] then let them mate. He wanted to see if their union would birth insights into the Dao of Yin and Yang.

“Worried that one pair wasn’t enough, he gathered ten Jinwu Golden Crows and ten Jade Rabbits. Those ten Jinwu Golden Crows had to mate day and night until they couldn’t bear it anymore. One night, they all fled, and ten Jinwu Golden Crows took flight together. The heat was unbearable! The Nine-Layers Immortal saw his test subjects escaping and thought it was disastrous. Thus, he grabbed his bow on the spot and shot down nine, though he didn’t kill them because he still needed them for his experiments.

“Back then, I was right beside him. I pointed to the tenth crow and said I’d never tasted one before, suggesting he shoot the tenth one too so that I could prepare a feast for the four of them. The Nine-Layers Immortal’s hand trembled, and the arrow missed, letting that Jinwu Golden Crow get away. What a pity.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head, still lamenting the lost opportunity.

1. It’s an ancient Chinese divination principle. ☜

2. In Chinese mythology, the Jade Rabbit is said to live on the moon with Chang’e. ☜

Chapter 532: Mastering the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame

Lu Yang couldn’t help but be curious. With nine Jinwu Golden Crows returning, how would the ten Jade Rabbits be distributed? Would they all mate together, or would the extra one be roasted by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to poison the Four Ancient Immortals?

I feel like I don’t need to know so many scandals and dark histories. Not only are they useless for cultivation, but they may also cost me my life when encountering the Four Ancient Immortals in the future.

Lu Yang currently had no positive impressions of the Four Ancient Immortals in his mind. If I ever meet them and try to cozy up by saying, “I’m on close terms with the Everlasting Immortal Fairy; she tells me stories about you every day...”

...I’m afraid there’d be no saving my life then.

“Well? After listening to my story, doesn’t it greatly aid your comprehension of the Jinwu Golden Crow True Fire?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy asked.

It was an official consensus in the cultivation world that understanding the stories behind spells and techniques allowed deeper comprehension of their essence. Unfortunately, most techniques’ histories were too distant in the past to trace, leaving their origins shrouded in mystery.

But for Lu Yang, listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s stories about spells and techniques would only diminish his comprehension of them.

“Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame...” He summoned a tiny wisp of his power, letting it bloom at his fingertip. Even if this flame was minuscule, it contained immeasurable energy. He stared at the flame and slowly closed his eyes to comprehend its essence.

“Which flame should I choose?” Man Gu was conflicted. Ideally, I want to learn the Three Flavor True Fire, but when I asked Lu Yang to teach me, I couldn’t master it—or should I say that I didn’t even know where to begin.

“Should I choose the Nirvana True Fire like Senior Brother Meng?”

Watching Meng Jingzhou gradually refine the Nirvana True Fire, with tendrils of fire energy flowing in and out of him, Man Gu shook his head. “No, no, it’s not suitable. This is a demon race’s true fire. Not only is it incompatible with my bloodline, but my comprehension ability is also not as strong as Senior Brother Meng’s to transcend racial barriers.

“Luna True Fire? It’s not suitable. My blood qi is too vigorous. Comprehending this true fire will suppress my blood qi and weaken my power.

“Hundun-Chaos True Fire? It’s not suitable. I know nothing about hundun primal chaos. There’s no way to comprehend it.

“Purple Star Heavenly Fire? It’s not suitable. With the stars gone, this heavenly fire that originated from the Purple Star becomes baseless. No matter how powerful it is, it’d be hard to sustain.

“This flame seems familiar. I can give it a try.” Man Gu lit up with joy, sitting cross-legged before a flame.

It was the Three Esse True Fire.

Tao Yaoye also struggled with her choice. She passed by the Jinwu Golden Crow True Fire, Luna True Fire, and Extreme Calculation True Fire, but none resonated with her.

Finally, she settled down cross-legged before a flame that emitted bird-like cries.

It was the Nanming Li Fire.[1]

Lu Yang’s meditation entered an ideal state. He envisioned himself as the sun, suspended high in the sky, shining upon the land and nurturing all life, when suddenly, a large hand grabbed him and placed him beside a rabbit...

“Look at Lu Yang! He’s clearly comprehending the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame, yet both luna and sun energies have manifested in him, and they seem to be merging!”

The Five-Elements Sect disciples gasped. To comprehend the power of the moon from the power of the sun—what heaven-defying comprehension ability is this! Not to mention merging these two opposing forces!

This person’s mastery of true flames is so terrifying!

Even the Five Branch Elders and Qiu Jin’an couldn’t stay composed. Such talent has probably only appeared two or three times in history!

“Old Song, this boy’s talent is terrifying!” The Metal Branch Elder transmitted an auditory message to Song Duantian. Given our deep-seated grudge against the old Taciturn scoundrel, shouldn’t we take this chance to vent our anger now that his disciple has fallen into our hands?

As the saying goes, “a teacher for a day is a father for a lifetime; the son inherits the father’s legacy; and the son repays the father’s debts.” There’s nothing wrong with letting Lu Yang bear the debts!

Song Duantian’s brows were knitted tightly. “If we don’t eliminate this boy, he’ll remember our actions today and become a great menace in the future!”

“A hidden menace instead.”

“What do we do?”

The Metal Branch Elder stared fixedly at Lu Yang, internally wrestling before finally showing a vicious expression, as if he had arrived at a resolution. “If worse comes to worst, we’ll just stop holding grudges against that old Taciturn scoundrel!”

~~~

“Look! Only the power of the sun remains on Lu Yang now!”

Lu Yang was unaware of the thoughts of the Metal Branch and Fire Branch elders. His priority was to quickly forget his earlier epiphany. He had nearly fallen into the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s trap of comprehending the method of sun and moon fusion.

What a close shave.

He began comprehending the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame again, envisioning himself as a sun patrolling the heavens, with all living beings thriving and brimming with vitality.

The sun was like a balloon, expanding and contracting, as if it was ready to burst at any moment, gripping onlookers’ hearts with anxiety.

Suddenly, a melodious and vigorous bird cry came from within the sun.

“Success!” Filled with joy, Lu Yang’s eyes snapped open, glowing bright red like miniature suns.

With a blink of his eyes, they returned to normal, clear and childlike, making observers doubt if everything they had seen earlier was just an illusion.

“You succeeded?” Bai Ming asked incredulously. As someone who had mastered the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame himself, he knew how difficult it was to comprehend such a true fire.

“Let’s test it out.” Lu Yang smiled confidently. I’m certain there’s no problem this time. My comprehension of the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame is thorough.

He opened his left palm, and a flame materialized, sharply raising the ambient temperature. The flame flickered, gradually stabilizing into a form whose outline vaguely resembled a bird.

“True Flame Mimicry?” Bai Ming whispered in awe. Flames are unstable in shape and require exceptional control to mold them into the desired form. Most cultivators need at least fifty years of diligent practice to achieve it.

Yet Lu Yang makes it look so effortless. It doesn’t look like he’s deliberately performing mimicry; it’s more like the true flame was already in this form the moment it manifested!

The corners of Lu Yang’s mouth curved into a confident smirk. He raised two fingers to his lips and pretended to command softly, “True flame, appear!”

The true flame morphed into a Jinwu golden crow so lifelike and detailed that it seemed alive.

“Did the true flame really morph into a Jinwu golden crow?” Bai Ming exclaimed once more. This time, he could no longer contain the shock in his heart and shouted it out.

The Five-Elements Sect disciples and elders had long noticed the situation with Lu Yang.

“Transforming the true flame into a Jinwu golden crow on his first try?”

“Wait, look! The Jinwu golden crow has three legs, but Lu Yang’s only has two!”

“Do Jinwu golden crows with two legs exist?”

“The defining feature of Jinwu golden crows is their three legs. Can it even be considered a Jinwu golden crow if it has two legs?

Lu Yang was also baffled. Why did the true flame automatically morph into a “Jinwu golden crow” that’s completely different from what I’d imagined?

He clenched his left fist to extinguish the flame, then opened his hand to summon it again.

It was still a two-legged “Jinwu golden crow.”

Refusing to give up, he persisted through multiple attempts, hoping for a third leg to grow, but to no avail.

Lu Yang scratched his head. Having never encountered anything like this before, he turned to Bai Ming. “Do you know what’s happening?”

Bai Ming had similarly never encountered anything like this before and was equally stumped. “All Jinwu golden crows have three legs. Yours with two legs is probably a golden-colored bird.”

“So does this count as the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame?”

Bai Ming’s expression grew increasingly strange. “More like it’s the Golden Bird True Flame.”

Chapter 533: A Single’s Spirit Root Cultivator Dares to Learn the Nirvana True Fire?

“Golden Bird True Flame?”

Lu Yang was perplexed. I feel like I cultivated correctly though.

He observed the “Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame.” After listening to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy recount the history of the Jinwu Golden Crows, he visualized himself transforming into a sun, within which a bird’s cry echoed.

The true fire is right before me, an immortal guided me, and my visualization has reached sublimity. This entire process should have been perfect.

So why did a two-legged golden bird emerge?

“There are three possibilities,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy analyzed seriously.

Lu Yang was overjoyed, not expecting the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to be so reliable as to propose three theories. Cupping his fists respectfully, he urged, “Please enlighten me, Immortal Fairy.”

“First possibility: When you cultivated the Three Esse True Fire into Three Flavor True Fire, this bit of difference[1] got transferred to the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame.

“Second possibility: Although the Nine-Layers Immortal didn’t shoot the tenth Jinwu Golden Crow back then, as I was lamenting how he and the others could only watch the Jinwu Golden Crows and Jade Rabbits mate without getting to eat a single crow, one crow voluntarily tore off a leg for me. Just as it was about to regenerate the limb, it got pounced on by a Jade Rabbit.

“The one you’ve refined might be that Jinwu Golden Crow that didn’t have time to regenerate its leg.

“Third possibility: According to clues provided by the Qilin Immortal and research by the Nine-Layers Immortal, the Jinwu Golden Crow race originally only had two legs. To adapt to the harsh environment in ancient times, they gradually evolved a third leg. Both the Qilin Immortal’s Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit and the Phoenix prodigy’s Natural Selection Incipient Dao Fruit drew inspiration from the Jinwu golden crow’s history.”

Lu Yang found none of these explanations credible.

“Whatever. As long as it’s a true flame, it’s fine.”

Wielding the Jinwu Golden Crow True Flame in his palm, Lu Yang could sense its terrifying power. It was a destructive force that outmatched even the Three Flavor True Fire. Once unleashed, few Golden Core cultivators could withstand it.

The second to succeed was Li Haoran. Having inherited half of Qin Haoran’s memories, his life experience far surpassed his peers.

With a snap of his fingers, a wisp of Six Ding Divine Fire ignited at his fingertip. After studying it for a while, he removed his wig, revealing his bald head. He used the heavenly fire to temper the wig, elevating its internal inscriptions to a higher level.

As Yuan Gang witnessed this scene, he was filled with deep respect. Truly a ruthless individual. He even refined his own hair into a magical treasure for the sake of becoming stronger.

Man Gu was the third to comprehend a true fire—the Three Esse True Fire.

He noticed the commotion at Lu Yang’s side, particularly the golden bird cradled in his palm. Shuddering, he murmured, “The first true fire Senior Brother Lu comprehended was the Three Flavor True Fire, and it could enhance barbeque to another tier. And now with his second, he has gone straight to turning the true fire into barbeque ingredients?”

The gap between me and Senior Brother Lu is indeed vast. I have much room for improvement.

Half a day passed again, and it was now late at night.

Meng Jingzhou and Tao Yaoye comprehended their true flames almost at the same time, successfully attaining the Nirvana True Fire and Nanming Li Fire. As these were true flames of demon races, it was understandable that their progress was slower.

The Five Branches’ elders were astonished to see Meng Jingzhou master the Nirvana True Fire.

“This Meng boy isn’t simple. He’s even grasped the Nirvana True Fire.”

“I thought he’d give up.”

“This is the perseverance of those destined for greatness! Due to his Single’s Spirit Root, his Pure Yang Body must remain intact. Yet the Nirvana True Fire belongs to the phoenix race and has yang-boosting and blood-nourishing properties. For someone with a Single’s Spirit Root to master this true fire, the yang-boosting effects will likely become unparalleled among all Single’s Spirit Root cultivators in history!”

“To resist temptation and preserve his chastity under such circumstances, such willpower is admirable!”

“Combining the Single’s Spirit Root with the Nirvana True Fire will raise the strength of his Single’s Spirit Root to another tier, and his cultivation speed will become faster!”

Despite having lived all these years, this was the first time they had heard of a Single’s Spirit Root cultivator being so merciless to themselves, driving themselves to such extremes with a do-or-die approach.

Meng Jingzhou turned to glare resentfully at the whispering Five Branches elders.

You should’ve said it earlier! If I’d known, I wouldn’t have chosen the Nirvana True Fire.

My body is already reacting, and I’m afraid even pouring water might not calm it down.

Although Song Duantian was displeased that all five had comprehended true fires, he made no comments. After all, he had resolved to let go of his grudge against the Taciturn Daoist Priest.

After the Five Branch elders and Qiu Jin’an departed, the fissured earth sealed shut as the true fire seeds returned to dormancy beneath the Fire Branch.

Bai Ming cleared his throat. “Shall we continue the tour?”

“Tour at this hour?” Lu Yang was surprised. At this time in the Dao-Seeking Sect, our senior brothers and sisters would already be partying and having a whale of a time.

Bai Ming was equally bewildered by Lu Yang’s reaction. “As cultivators who don’t sleep, what difference does day or night make?”

Lu Yang looked around. That’s true. The Fire Branch senior brothers are still sitting in meditation, though the near-naked sunbathing senior brothers from daytime are gone.

Without sunlight at night, sunbathing isn’t an option.

Meng Jingzhou recalled, “They say the Dao-Seeking Sect also used to cultivate day and night without rest. But ever since Grand-Shifu retired and our shifus and elders took over, they changed their approach. The sect promoted work-rest balance, cultivating by day and playing by night; there’s no need to make things unnecessarily difficult for ourselves.”

After this shift in policy, excluding the Yun Zhi factor, the Dao-Seeking Sect’s overall strength hadn’t declined but showed subtle improvement, proving the policy’s feasibility and effectiveness.

“This is the Water Branch.” Bai Ming led the five to a misty lakeshore devoid of people, with only aquatic plants breaking through the water's surface.

“Where's everyone?”

Bai Ming stood on the water and pointed downward. “All below. Follow me.”

The six held their breaths and enveloped themselves in spirit energy to keep their clothes dry as they submerged themselves in the water.

Underwater, their view expanded drastically, revealing a bustling scene—spirit plants, fish that had yet to gain spirit intelligence, strange stones, whirlpools... It was an underwater world in every sense.

“Unfortunately, none of you have a Water Spirit Root. Otherwise, it would have been much easier for you to sense the distinct spirit opportunities here.”

The Five-Elements Sect disciples moved effortlessly underwater, clearly accustomed to training here. Some spun in circles, forcibly creating underwater tornadoes. Two disciples even collided with their whirlpools, churning the waters violently.

The Dao-Seeking Sect also had a cultivation area for those with a Water Spirit Root. It was a massive lake so deep that even Heaven’s Gate Peak would disappear beneath its surface. However, no one from Lu Yang’s group had a Water Spirit Root, so they never needed to visit such a place.

“Originally, the Water Branch was just a lake. A past Water Branch Elder traveled to the East Sea and realized oceans and lakes were entirely different environments. Thus, he stole lots of seawater from the East Sea with storage rings and relocated it here. freewebnovel.com

“Upon further contemplation, he realized seawater alone wouldn’t work. Without sea tribes, the environment still differed from the actual East Sea. Hence, he went to the East Sea again and got in touch with various sea clans to ask if they were willing to relocate to the Five-Elements Sect.

“Most declined, but a few desiring a change of environment followed him back to the sect. Then, he had to register their household and handle residency paperwork. The procedures were extremely tedious.”

Bai Ming pointed ahead. “That’s the seawater we ‘transplanted’ from the East Sea, along with its sea tribes.”

1. If you still remember, the two characters are 昧 and 味. As you can see, the difference is just a stroke. The original text describes that the missing ‘dot’ had been transferred. ☜

Chapter 534: Sea Tribes and Ice Region

The sea tribes were a subset of the demon race; they had long made the oceans their home. One notable example was the dragon race. While dragons could be found in the Demon Region, many also dwelled in the East Sea, where they were regarded as part of the sea tribes.

As soon as the six entered the Water Branch’s sea region, darkness enveloped their vision. Only when the massive shadow gradually moved away could they discern what it was.

“That’s a whale, a creature unique to the East Sea. It has yet to gain spirit intelligence.”

Next, they encountered a group of living beings with fishtails, all female with exquisite features. Their voluptuous figures had key areas covered by seashells, and their eyes were a sea-blue hue.

“These are jiao-folk,[1] also known as fishfolk.[2] Legend says they originated from ancient humans and great fish demons after shapeshifting. They move in groups, with females going out to hunt while males tend to domestic affairs.”

Suddenly, another merfolk swam past, her undulating tail more elegant than the previous fishfolk. After casting a brief glance at the group, she continued on her way.

“Is that a lone jiao-folk being ostracized?”

“No, that’s Senior Sister Tang Fuling, a Water Spirit Root cultivator. She’s researching how Water Spirit Roots can spray seawater. Lately, she often dresses up as a member of the sea tribes.”

Lu Yang grew more curious. “What’s difficult about spraying seawater from a Water Spirit Root?”

“Of course it’s difficult! A Water Spirit Root is formed by water; how could it generate salt?”

Lu Yang had to admit that it was indeed difficult.

“Wait, but why research this at all?”

Bai Ming looked embarrassed. “Dirty linen shouldn’t be aired in public. I can tell you, but please keep this to yourselves. We can’t let this reach the imperial court’s ears.”

“Don’t worry, our lips are sealed,” Meng Jingzhou guaranteed with sincerity. It is true. Our identities as the young creed leader and four holy sons of the Heavenly Court Creed remain undisclosed to this day, a testament to our strict confidentiality.

Of course, from another perspective, this secrecy stemmed from self-preservation. They feared for their lives should their hidden identities be revealed.

“Senior Sister Tang likes money. She heard smuggling salt can earn quick bucks, so she’s planning to do just that.”

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

No wonder you were afraid of this reaching the imperial court’s ears.

“With so much seawater here, why not just evaporate and dry it to produce salt?”

“Senior Sister Tang said that one should take responsibility for their own actions. Using seawater to produce salt would make it too easy for the imperial court to trace back to our sect.”

“Damn, she’s thought this through so thoroughly,” Li Haoran marveled. She’d even considered the potential consequences. Such meticulous planning is almost catching up with Qin Haoran’s.

“Those are the turtle tribe, shark tribe, and clam tribe.” Bai Ming pointed to each of the sea tribes in turn.

The turtles carried heavy shells, the sharks bore gills on their faces, and the clam maidens were singing. These sea tribes recognized them as guests of the Five-Elements Sects and nodded in greeting.

“It’s a pity supreme sea tribes like the dragons and kunpeng fish-bird[3] refuse to leave the East Sea and live in our sect. Even when they’re willing to come, it’s merely to sightsee and broaden their horizons before returning,” Bai Ming lamented. He never had the opportunity to meet these sea tribes.

“The Kunpeng Tribe once asked me for a favor,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked casually. I’ve naturally met them before. Even their old ancestor would have to bow respectfully before me.

“What kind of favor?”

Favor in sparing their lives or making them more delicious when cooked?

The Unbeatable Golden Core’s warning made Lu Yang bite back his remark.

“Have you heard people’s description of the Kunpeng Tribe? ‘In the northern sea is a fish; its name is Kun. The Kun’s size—no one knows how many thousand li it spans. It transforms into a bird; its name is Peng. The Peng’s back—no one knows how many thousand li it spans.”[4]

In ancient times, when celestial bodies still existed, the Kunpeng Tribe inhabited a planet called the “Northern Sea.”[5]

“I’ve heard those lines before. What about it?”

“Back then, the Kunpeng Tribe’s old ancestor came looking for me, saying inconsistent measurement standards between tribes—particularly regarding ‘li’ and ‘meters’—made it impossible to accurately ascertain the size of the Kunpeng Tribe's members. Thus, he asked if we Five Ancient Immortals could standardize the measurement system. Since we’d been thinking about this anyway, we granted his request.”

Lu Yang, “...”

Are you sure this is how that passage is supposed to be interpreted?

“Why does it feel a little cold?” Tao Yaoye asked after they had been swimming for some time.

While Golden Core cultivators were impervious to extreme temperatures, they could still sense the temperature in the outer world.

“Ahead lies the Ice Region. It was constructed through arrays by the first Water Branch Elder. Over the years, successive Water Branch Elders have reinforced it, causing it to expand and the ice to grow ever thicker. Not many people go there usually. Would you like to take a look?”

Ice-type cultivation techniques were a side branch of the water element; Ice Spirit Roots were a variant of Water Spirit Roots. Similarly, the Ice Region was a place essential to cultivators with Water Spirit Roots.

As they spoke, a massive iceberg drifted into view, making even the gigantic whales appear as tiny as ants before it. Ninety percent of the iceberg was submerged beneath the surface, while less than ten percent peeked out.

“It’s a rare opportunity. Let’s go have a look then.” Meng Jingzhou chuckled. The last time he came to the Five-Elements Sect, he was focused solely on mastering spells and didn’t tour the Five Branches properly.

To the north of the Great Xia Dynasty lay a bitterly cold zone called the Extreme North. Hardly anyone from the Dao-Seeking Sect had set foot there, much less Lu Yang and his four companions. With sparse lifeforms and scarce cultivation resources beyond ice, there was little reason to venture there.

As they progressed deeper into the Ice Region, the cold became cold-chilling. Even their golden cores couldn’t protect them. Everyone experienced firsthand what extreme cold meant, their spirit energy circulating thirty to forty percent slower. However, none said to stop as they pressed forward.

“Alright, this is far enough.” Bai Ming couldn’t bear the cold anymore, his teeth chattering uncontrollably.

The group collectively sighed in relief; someone had finally called a halt—they too couldn’t hold out any longer.

“Since the Ice Region was built by the first Water Branch Elder, doesn’t that mean this place is filled with millennia-old, ten-thousand-year-old ice, and maybe even hundred-thousand-year-old ice?” Man Gu mused aloud with sparkling eyes. Having lived in the perpetually hot western side of the continent, he had never seen this much ice.

“Of course, ten-thousand-year-old and hundred-thousand-year-old ice are plenty around here, but they’re practically useless.”

“Useless? I heard they’re very valuable.”

Bai Ming waved his hand and cleared up Man Gu’s confusion. “That’s just unscrupulous merchants hyping it up and inflating its value by cooking up flashy nonsense, claiming it has a historical foundation and ten thousand years of cold energy that is immensely beneficial to cultivation. It’s all a scam—as if the older something is, the more valuable it becomes. Think about it, the spirit qi we inhale has been around for millions and billions of years, but why isn’t anyone selling it?

“And this water and these stones too. They’re far older than a hundred thousand years.”

Lu Yang nodded to Bai Ming’s points. He inadvertently noticed Meng Jingzhou staying silent and was bewildered. “Old Meng, what’s wrong? Don’t you love to speak at times like this?”

Meng Jingzhou transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang. “Shh, don’t say anything. It was our Meng Family that hyped up the ten-thousand-year-old ice.”
