Chapter 535: Time Suspension

Lu Yang looked at Meng Jingzhou with a strange expression. Your Meng Family really gets creative when it comes to making money, huh?

“Why are you looking at me like that? It’s not like I was the one who hyped up the price of ten-thousand-year-old ice. It was the Meng Family, the one from tens of thousands of years ago.” Although Meng Jingzhou always referred to the Meng Family as “our Meng Family,” this matter involved his personal reputation, so he was quick to draw a line.

While the Meng Family had maliciously hyped up ten-thousand-year-old ice, it was targeted at ordinary ice. Things like Mystic Ice Marrows or Ice Embryos were still more valuable the longer they aged. For instance, archaic slumbering cultivators often used Mystic Ice Marrows that were more than ten thousand years old to freeze themselves and awaken in the current era, only to fall into the hands of the Great Xia Dynasty.

Some were even more unfortunate. Those who used either inadequately aged or outright fake Mystic Ice Marrows were forced to awaken in advance due to the ice melting prematurely. The archaic Fusion cultivators Lu Yang had encountered in the horrifying rule incident of Buyi Town were prime examples.

“Who needs ten-thousand-year-old Mystic Ice Marrows? If it were up to me, a single Everlasting Immortal Fruit could keep them asleep till the end of time; there’d absolutely be no risk of awakening early.”

“But Immortal Fairy, isn’t your Everlasting Immortal Fruit meant to prevent decay of corpses?”

“Not much difference. Those fellows frozen with Mystic Ice Marrows are hardly any different from corpses. How else do you think they bypassed lifespan limits to sleep until now? Isn’t it because they entered a feigned death state when frozen?”

“Well, a ‘feigned death state’ isn’t entirely accurate. The precise term would be ‘near-total time suspension.’”

“Time suspension?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy nodded earnestly. Suddenly, she recalled Yun Zhi’s warnings. She warned me not to tell Lu Yang too many matters beyond his level.

But then, she remembered her glorious past, where she roamed the world carefree in ancient times. A mere Lass Yun isn’t worthy of my notice! I’ll speak my mind!

“What I’m about to tell you is top secret. You mustn’t let Lass Yun know!” Ever smart, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy devised a win-win solution.

“Feel free to speak, Immortal Fairy. Do you not know me? My lips are sealed!” Lu Yang patted his mouth to vouch for his credibility. Although he still remembered Yun Zhi’s warnings, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s stories always ignited his curiosity.

Of course, if she wishes to veer into ancient dark history and scandals, that’d be another matter.

The first-in-command and second-in-command exchanged a tacit grin, already forgetting their internal strife from three days ago.

“If you cultivate a Heavenly Eye and attain extraordinary vision, you will realize that all matter in this world is in motion, be it people, objects, dust, or even the tiniest particles composing them.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal wielded the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit and grasped extreme temperatures. He discovered that motion isn’t absolute. If the temperature drops to its limit, even the tiniest particles freeze and become immobile.

“When the Nine-Layers Immortal consulted the Epoch Immortal about this, the Epoch Immortal’s research concluded that if the Nine-Layers Immortal harnessed the extreme cold, he could also achieve a time suspension.”

“Also? The Epoch Immortal could suspend time too?”

“Of course. The Epoch Immortal could suspend the entire world’s time, the range much wider than the Nine-Layers Immortal’s.

“Later, the Nine-Layers Immortal discovered that the tiniest particles accelerated at high heat. He adjusted the temperature to the highest, beyond that of the sun. Under extreme heat, the speed of the tiniest particles reached its limit—in other words, the speed of light. This falls under the domain of the Epoch Dao Fruit.”

Lu Yang mulled over the story he had just heard and suddenly felt enlightened. “Immortal Fairy, are you saying that all Dao Fruits ultimately lead to the same destination?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy stared at Lu Yang for a moment. “Yes, that’s exactly the principle I wanted to tell you! I didn’t expect you to comprehend it on your own!” Actually, the ten-thousand-year-old Mystic Ice Marrow simply reminded me of this matter. I didn’t think so much.

As they spoke, the group arrived at the Metal Branch.

As soon as they stepped in, everyone felt a tingling sensation on their skin. Their golden cores automatically protected their masters, covering their bodies with a thin membrane of spirit qi. Only then did the numbing sensation disappear.

“This is the unique intangible metal qi of the Metal Branch. According to Elder Tong, the Metal Branch Elder, the Metal Branch is made up of countless precious essence stones and mineral veins. These precious ores possess their own pride that doesn’t allow them to coexist with other minerals. The collision between these ores and minerals causes metal qi to leak out, resulting in this unique phenomenon at the Metal Branch.”

The land of the Metal Branch rarely saw vegetation. Even when spirit plants grew there, they would have been converted by the Metal Branch’s influence, taking on a metallic luster. To flourish in an environment suffused with metal qi was a testament to the sheer resilience of these spirit plants.

Lu Yang’s Sword Spirit Root was a variant of the Metal Spirit Root, making him particularly sensitive to the vibrant metal qi of the Metal Branch. If this metal qi was refined, it would become the most basic form of sword qi.

Man Gu noticed many Five-Elements Sect disciples sitting in meditation on the Metal Branch with numerous magical treasures floating above their heads, bobbing up and down as if they were floating on the sea’s surface. Some paired up, competing with each other to control magical treasures, which could coordinate to form powerful arrays. Such exquisite manipulation demonstrated the strength of their spiritual consciousness.

Bai Ming smiled. “The Metal Branch is most adept at metal manipulation. It can be likened to sword control techniques.

“If we’re talking about the individual most skilled in metal manipulation, that would be the first Metal Branch Elder. His cultivation was heaven-defying, and his every movement was in perfect harmony with nature’s laws. He was truly formidable. If he hadn’t moved several mineral veins here during the sect’s founding, the Metal Branch couldn’t have achieved its current state.”

“...So your Five-Elements Sect’s Metal Branch was stolen from elsewhere?”

“You can’t call it stealing,” Bai Ming corrected. “It’s called illegal mining.

“Besides, the first Metal Branch Elder studied law. At that time, the Great Xia Dynasty had just been established. Its legal system wasn’t yet complete, and even the penal code hadn’t been drafted. He took advantage of this gap to make contributions to the sect by bringing a few mineral veins back to the sect.”

Without even a draft of the penal code, there was no way to convict him of any crime.

Lu Yang, “...”

“The first Metal Branch Elder stated that as cultivators, their every word and action should conform to nature’s laws. This implies that cultivators themselves are a part of nature’s laws. Therefore, his moving the ore veins to the Five-Elements Sect isn’t considered illegal mining, but rather ‘natural migration of mineral veins.’ It was a course of nature, and he merely accelerated the process. Hence, it shouldn’t count as a crime.”

“And then?”

“The imperial court didn’t buy it.”

“I thought so too.”

“Later, he took out a loan from the Meng Family and purchased those mineral veins.” Bai Ming glanced at Meng Jingzhou and added, “As for the loan from the Meng Family, it was fully repaid sixty thousand years ago.”

Chapter 536: The Earth Branch Suits Me Quite Well

“It is our Meng Family’s nature to rescue those in distress. There’s no need to thank me for such a trivial matter.”

When the war ended a hundred thousand years ago, there wasn’t even a trace of the Luodi Merchant Guild yet. Back then, the Meng Family was one of the two great ancestral clans vying for supremacy. They were an entity so formidable that only the imperial court could rival their might. freewebnovel.com

However, the imperial court took no action to purge the Meng Family, not even trimming their wings of influence. This was a testament to the imperial court’s trust in the Meng Family.

“Speaking of which, what exactly happened in that battle between the Meng Family’s founding ancestor and the founding Xia Emperor? How did your ancestor lose? What cultivation realm were they at then?” Li Haoran’s question piqued everyone’s curiosity about his historical clash.

Meng Jingzhou shook his head. “Don’t look at me, I genuinely don’t know. It’s not just me; even my dad and grandpa aren’t sure either. You’d have better luck asking Big Senior Sister.”

Everyone immediately waved their hands, expressing they were not interested.

You must be joking! Who’d dare bother Big Senior Sister with questions? If the questions are related to cultivation, that might still be fine, but if they’re merely to satisfy our curiosity, I’m afraid Big Senior Sister will throw us off from the summit of Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“I know a little about this,” Man Gu said hesitantly.

“You do?”

“Mmm. One of our Barbarian Tribe’s ancestors, a Transcendent Tribulation cultivator, once served by the side of the founding Xia Emperor and witnessed the battle between the Meng Family’s ancestor and the first Xia Emperor. This ancestor of ours left records, but they’re classified, and I’m not qualified to view the contents. I’ve only heard about it from our tribe leader.”

Although the Barbarian Tribe’s influence couldn’t match the Meng Family’s, only a few races from the Demon Region could match the length of their history.

Man Gu continued, “In terms of military power, the Meng Family was stronger, and in terms of one-on-one combat, the odds were also in the Meng ancestor’s favor. I believe both parties ultimately chose not to engage in a full-scale war with their military strength to prevent unnecessary bloodshed. But what our tribe leader can’t figure out is how the first Xia Emperor eventually won.

“Anyway, the first Xia Emperor prevailed. Both parties made a pact during their duel, promising the victor wouldn’t punish the loser. Judging by Brother Meng’s situation, the agreement has held to this day.”

Soon, Bai Ming led the five to another location and jumped into a deep pit. “This is the Earth Branch.”

Stepping on the Earth Branch brought a sense of weight, as if one’s entire being was merging with the land. Clearly, the soil here wasn’t ordinary.

“The Earth Branch is renowned for its defense. When one has mastered their cultivation techniques with major success, stepping on the earth will cause an endless stream of energy to surge forth.”

“So they just have to fight in the air?”

Bai Ming shook his head with a proud smile. If it’s really so easy to find a countermeasure, how could the Earth Branch have held its ground in the Five-Elements Sect?

He pointed to the ground two meters above them. “Do you know what this is?”

“Is it not an earth pit?” Man Gu was baffled.

“Jump out and you’ll know.”

Everyone followed his instructions and leaped out of the pit effortlessly.

Midair, they looked down at the pit again, and their pupils constricted.

How is this an earth pit? It’s clearly a footprint!

As far as the eye could see, the Earth Branch was riddled with these “earth pits!”

“Earth Branch cultivators never fight in the air,” Bai Ming explained. “They master Heaven-Earth Manifestation and Size At Will to enlarge their bodies. Why bother flying into the sky when you can simply grow tall enough to reach your enemies?”

Lu Yang found the Earth Branch’s cultivation method aligned well with his nature.

“Make way please! Don’t stand beside the footprints!” A voice rang from a distance.

Hearing this, Bai Ming hastily leaped out of the pit.

Just as he did, the ground swelled upward. The once compact earth became “loose and soft” as the “earth pit” magically filled itself in.

“Senior Brother Kong, you almost buried me!” Bai Ming complained to the approaching figure.

“But you didn’t get buried, did you?” The voice belonged to a two-meter-tall burly man who resembled an iron tower. “Who are these five?” He asked, noticing the unfamiliar faces.

“They are guests from the Dao-Seeking Sect.

“This is Senior Brother Kong Ling, the Big Senior Brother of the Earth Branch. He’s currently comprehending the threshold between the Void Refinement and Fusion stages and attempting to break through. All those footprints you saw were made by him.”

“Greetings, Senior Brother Kong Ling.”

“Good, good. How’s Old Dai these days? Still in the Great Mission Hall?”

“First Elder is away all year round, so Senior Brother Dai has taken over all the affairs of the Great Mission Hall.”

“Old Dai is truly talented. He’s already at the Fusion Stage while I’m still a bit behind,” Kong Ling remarked with envy.

His cultivation realm was indiscernible as it fluctuated wildly, falling to the detectable Foundation Establishment Stage, then soaring to a stage beyond what Lu Yang and the others could perceive.

“This kid’s about to break through to the Fusion Stage,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy observed.

After bidding goodbye to Kong Ling, the six arrived at the Wood Branch. It was similar to the Dao-Seeking Sect’s herb garden, a place brimming with spirit herbs. The verdant vegetation exuded an inexplicable spiritual charm that made one feel as light as clouds.

It was a scene of spring with lush trees thriving everywhere and teeming with life. Towering trees stretched to the firmament, their crowns blocked by layers of leaves as if they hid secrets within.

“The unique trait of the Wood Branch is its vitality and strong regenerative power. This is somewhat similar to Fellow Daoist Meng’s Nirvana True Fire.”

“The young fellows from the Dao-Seeking Sect have arrived?” A youthful female voice chimed from the top of the towering trees.

The girl flipped down from the branches and landed steadily on the ground, a twig still clamped between her teeth.

It was none other than the person Grandpa Ba had wanted to see at the Five-Elements Sect—Shangguan Yu.

“Not bad, kid. Your cultivation foundations are pretty solid.” Shangguan Yu patted Lu Yang’s shoulder. She had already taken notice of this little fellow who’d managed to become the acting sect leader during her last visit to the Dao-Seeking Sect.

It had been over a year since, and Lu Yang’s progress exceeded her expectations.

“Greetings, Old Ancestor Shangguan,” Lu Yang and the others said respectfully, not daring to be impolite to Sect Leader Qiu’s elder.

Hearing them call her “old ancestor,” Shangguan Yu frowned. “What ‘old ancestor?’ Am I that old? Call me jiejie.”

However, they didn’t dare comply. They were afraid that even if they could get past Shangguan Yu, they wouldn’t make it through Qiu Jin’an’s side.

“Call me jiejie, and jiejie will give you something good.” Shangguan Yu produced a small wooden plaque pulsing with vitality.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s eyes lit up as she hurriedly urged, “Lu Yang, quick! Call her! This is good stuff!”

Caught between Shangguan Yu and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang had no choice but to accede and risk his life as he obediently called out, “Shangguan-jiejie.”

Shangguan Yu was all smiles, standing on tiptoe to pat his head. “Good boy. This protective talisman is yours now.”

Lu Yang finally obtained the wooden plaque as he had wished. “Immortal Fairy, what exactly is this wooden plaque?” Lu Yang could sense vibrant vitality from it but couldn’t identify what kind of tree it had originated from.

“Jianmu wood.”

Chapter 537: Jianmu World Tree

“Jianmu wood?” Lu Yang’s eyes widened as he stared at the wooden amulet incredulously. “But isn’t that the true form of the Epoch Immortal?”

Most people couldn’t recognize immortal times, often attaching the label “immortal” to anything rare and extraordinary. For instance, the common folk typically referred to little herb kings as “immortal herbs,” peerless swords as “immortal swords,” and unfathomable Dao arts as “immortal spells.”

But in truth, neither the little herb kings nor the peerless swords had reached the level to be considered “immortal.”

The Jianmu World Tree was different. It was undeniably an immortal object.

“I knew this thing looked familiar!” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared. “This must be a part of the Epoch Immortal. It’s just too small, else I’d have recognized it right away!” No one knows the Epoch Immortal better than I do.

Lu Yang had an odd expression. “Then how did this small piece of Jianmu wood come to be? Did the Epoch Immortal pick it off like dead skin from his feet?” An immortal’s body is indestructible. Who could possibly have hewn a chunk of wood from the Epoch Immortal’s body?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shot Lu Yang a disdainful look. “What are you saying? An immortal’s body is without contamination. How could we possibly shed foot skin like mortals?”

“Then this small piece of Jianmu...”

“It might have been blasted off by me.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“Though it’s also possible that the Heaven Mandate Immortals and the others had done that. Before becoming an immortal, the Epoch Immortal had claimed that he would undoubtedly ascend while the others wouldn’t. That incited mass anger and provoked multiple ambushes and retaliation from the rest. But this fragment of wood is too small. I can’t determine who exactly was responsible.”

Lu Yang pointed out, “If memory serves me right, Immortal Fairy, didn’t the Epoch Immortal only say those words to you? You were the one who spread it to the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the others.”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy waved her hand dismissively and tried to educate Lu Yang, “The outcome’s more or less the same. Don’t get hung up on the details. You should learn from me in this regard.

“Also, ask this little lass if she has more Jianmu wood.” The fact that she could give Lu Yang a small piece of the Jianmu implies she has more of it.

“Shangguan-jiejie, may I ask what this thing is? Why haven’t I seen it before?” Lu Yang inquired politely.

“Never seen it, have you? This is only a small piece. A far larger one lies beneath the Wood Branch. It’s a charred giant tree that maintains the Wood Branch’s vitality. Our sect’s founder nearly jumped out of his skin when he discovered that giant trunk. This tree’s vibrant life force has sustained the Wood Branch for ten thousand years without decline, a testament to its formidable power.

“Our founder realized this too. The sheer vitality contained within the giant tree was unimaginable, far beyond anything the cultivation world could understand. No spirit tree recorded in ancient texts matched its properties. Thus, our founder made a bold conjecture—this was a part of the Wood Immortal’s body!” The current cultivation world was unaware of the Epoch Immortal’s title and only knew he had manifested from a tree, so they called him the “Wood Immortal” out of habit.

“Wood Immortal?!” Everyone gasped. Even Bai Ming, who had never heard of this matter, was surprised to learn that the Wood Branch’s vitality stemmed from a giant chunk of wood.

“Shangguan-jiejie.”

“Shangguan-jiejie.”

Now that everyone knew Lu Yang was holding a piece of the legendary Wood Immortal, they began addressing Shangguan Yu with “jiejie,” with even Bai Ming joining in.

“Calling me that now? It’s too late.” Shangguan Yu turned her head away to hide her growing smirk. Then, she turned back and feigned seriousness. “You’ll need to call me more times than that.”

The choruses of “Shangguan-jiejie” echoing through the air brought a wide smile to Shangguan Yu’s visage. “Come come come, one for each of you. They can keep you safe. Little Bai Ming, you get one too.” She produced five small wooden plaques and distributed them to the group.

“Keep us safe?” Lu Yang recalled how the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned that the Epoch Immortal’s ability to ward off misfortune and evil could rid Meng Jingzhou of his karmic backlash.

If the Epoch Immortal’s body were truly effective in keeping one safe, why would Qiu Jin’an have needed to borrow the national fortune’s power from Wilderness Province’s governor?

He entered his mental space, planning to consult the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, only to find her already making a decision and expanding her immortal consciousness. Initially, she wondered whether she would offend the Five-Elements Sect, but upon hearing Shangguan Yu’s words, she was on the same page as Lu Yang and couldn’t be bothered about offending anyone.

Her immortal consciousness scanned the Wood Branch. Just as she had thought, she discovered the giant trunk segment Shangguan Yu had described.

The wood was enormous, stretching through the entire Wood Branch. Though Lu Yang’s group could casually tour the Five Branches, this was only because they walked near the convergence areas of the Five Branches, shortening distances considerably.

In truth, the Five-Elements Sect’s territory was only slightly smaller than the Dao-Seeking Sect’s, spanning a full eighty thousand li. The Five Branches formed the bulk of the sect. One could only imagine how vast the Wood Branch was and how long the giant tree running through it must be. However, compared to the sky-reaching Jianmu World Tree in the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s memories, this chunk of wood was much shorter and almost diminutive.

Within the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy conjured the giant tree’s image as she had seen it. The tree was charred black with burns from fire and lightning. Its aged bark had peeled away in multiple layers, and one attack had even pierced straight through its heartwood.

“What happened here?” Lu Yang was startled. Even an outsider like him could sense how brutal the assault on this giant tree had been.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy fell silent for a while before speaking slowly, devoid of her usual playful demeanor. “The Epoch Immortal was attacked. The assailant used common attack methods to conceal their identity.

“At first, I thought that when I self-detonated, the Epoch Immortal had used methods like ‘Withered Tree Spring Revival’ and ‘Cicada Sheds Its Carapace,’ leaving behind a clone while his real body escaped. But that didn’t make sense. The Heaven Mandate Immortal warned us not to leave clones behind in the world, for it could be a blessing or a source of calamity. Therefore, there shouldn’t be any clone of the Epoch Immortal here.

“Seeing this Jianmu segment confirms it—this is indeed the Epoch Immortal’s true body, and much of it has already turned into nothingness!”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had no recollection of a battle of such magnitude when she was alive. This is a battle where immortals can perish.

“After I died, the Epoch Immortal engaged in a great battle against an exceedingly powerful opponent.” The Epoch Immortal wielded the Epoch Dao Fruit, capable of observing the past and foreseeing the future. It could also restore his body to an undamaged state. The fact that he was reduced to this condition despite everything shows how strong and terrifying his opponent must have been.

Lu Yang’s heart shuddered. “The Epoch Immortal...has passed away?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy shook her head slowly. “It’s hard to say for certain. An immortal’s life force far surpasses your imagination. Even without their original body, they can still survive. But in the Epoch Immortal’s case, even if he’s still alive, without his true form, his situation is unlikely to be favorable.

“The Epoch Immortal and I are different. With the Everlasting Dao Fruit, I can casually create a true body to house an immortal soul. However, the Epoch Immortal can’t do that. To an immortal, their body is of utmost importance, but in this world, it’s hard to find anything that can replace or reconstruct an immortal body.”

If even the Epoch Immortal’s true form is in such ruins, his life or death unclear, what blessings or protection can still be spoken of?

Chapter 538: Granny-Shifu

All this time, a question had plagued Lu Yang’s mind.

If simply uttering the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s name could resurrect her, why had it taken three hundred thousand years, only for her to be revived by chance?

Drawing parallels from the Imperial Preceptor’s Karma Incipient Dao Fruit techniques, the culprit who assassinated the Immortal Fairy could have relied on similar methods to erase all memories of her from the world.

But could such a method also work on immortals?

No one can say for sure.

Now, the Epoch Immortal’s body is buried under the Wood Branch, and his immortal soul has vanished without a trace, his fate unknown.

If this is the state of the Epoch Immortal, what about the Heaven Mandate Immortal, the Nine-Layers Immortal, and the Qilin Immortal? What role had they played in the Epoch Immortal’s fall?

Were they culprits or victims?

“Immortal Fairy, do you really not remember what happened before your demise? Did the culprit have any distinguishing traits?”

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy frowned, struggling to recall what had transpired back then.

“My memories from that period are extremely blurry. I only remember sleeping that day, and in a haze, I felt my soul drifting upward. It felt comfortable, like I was going to melt. I can’t remember anything that happened afterward. The next time I woke up was when you called my name. My soul reformed, and I was successfully resurrected.”

Lu Yang sighed. It looks like I won’t be getting any useful information out of her.

For the Everlasting Immortal Fairy to proclaim herself the head of the Five Ancient Immortals, she must have possessed some skills. It’s impossible that she was ambushed without her knowing. Either the assailant was too powerful, or she wasn’t in the right state then.

“Killing me was one thing, but they didn’t even spare the Epoch Immortal and the others. They better not let me find out who they are. Watch me beat them to death!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy seethed.

Dying once doesn’t matter much to me. Over the endless passage of time, someone will eventually call out my name by accident. But it’s different for the Epoch Immortal. With his original body buried here, I’m afraid his fate is grim.

The Epoch Immortal helped me a lot when I was condensing my Everlasting Dao Fruit. I must repay his favor.

“I’ll inform Big Senior Sister about this when we return and let her decide.” Lu Yang hung his head, dejected that he couldn’t offer any help to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy for now. “If the Epoch Immortal’s condition is unknown, how is the Jianmu still able to radiate vitality?” Lu Yang pointed to the wooden plaque they had just received.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy gazed at the phantom image of the Jianmu she had conjured, her expression complicated. With a soft sigh, she explained, “A marvel like the Jianmu only needs the tiniest remnant to restore its vitality gradually, completing the conversion from death to life. It could be considered another form of resurrection, though it would be an entirely new Jianmu, no longer related to the Epoch Immortal.

“The Jianmu beneath us is in the process of regenerating its vitality. In tens or hundreds of thousands of years, it will fully revive and rise from the earth, becoming a brand new Jianmu World Tree that reaches the sky.

“See that tree that Lass Shangguan was standing by earlier? It shouldn’t have grown so tall, but it was influenced by the Jianmu’s vitality. If my guess is correct, its roots must be very close to where the Jianmu is.

“The Epoch Immortal once said that the Jianmu suffered a great tribulation in the past and was severed at the waist, its vitality extinguished. The new Jianmu grew from the remains of the old one, and that became him.”

“Alright, you young fellows have toured enough for today. Rest tonight.” Shangguan Yu clapped her hands and instructed Bai Ming to lead them to their accommodations. Tomorrow, they will begin studying General Principles of the Five Elements.

Although she hadn’t discerned that the Epoch Immortal’s original body lay beneath the Wood Branch, she recognized the Jianmu’s value. She didn’t give things away easily; she believed these five were destined for greatness and would leave indelible, colorful marks in the annals of cultivation. This was her way of forging good karmic ties with the juniors.

The lodging arranged by the Five-Elements Sect was at the convergence of the Five Branches—in other words, Qiu Jin’an’s territory, comparable in status to Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“Yo, you’re all back. It’s been a long time since we last met, Sect leader Lu.” A familiar voice teased Lu Yang.

Lu Yang turned to see Lin Shaoyou, Qiu Jin’an’s eldest disciple. He had a Wood Spirit Root, and his combat prowess at the Basic Fusion Stage already rivaled Advanced Fusion cultivators, placing him in the same tier as talents like Dai Bufan.

During the Five-Elements Sect’s last visit to the Dao-Seeking Sect, Acting Sect Leader Lu Yang had hosted Lin Shaoyou.

Assuming Yun Zhi was still serving as acting sect leader, Lin Shaoyou had proposed a challenge against someone of the same generation, only for Yun Zhi to step forward silently and for Lin Shaoyou to step back silently. And that was the end of it.

“Greetings, Senior Brother Lin.” The five cupped their hands in salute.

“Alright, alright, don’t be so stiff. Relax. I just needed a break from spell practice and saw you coming back, so I figured I’d say hello.

“Eh, Granny-Shifu[1] gave you wooden plaques?” Lin Shaoyou noticed the wooden tokens hanging from their necks.

Suddenly, Bai Ming’s expression changed. He swiftly pulled Lu Yang and the others aside.

A loud crack echoed through the air as lightning struck Lin Shaoyou, charring him to a crisp inside and out, black smoke curling from him.

Bai Ming whispered, “Senior Shangguan hates hearing others call her old. If someone knowingly does it anyway, this will be their end.” freewebnovel.com

“Ahem ahem, just a trivial matter, no harm done.” The charred corpse stirred to life, its eyes twinkling like snow.

A faint crackling sound followed as countless fissures spread across the charred corpse. Lin Shaoyou stepped out of the dried husk unscathed, his robes pristine as if nothing had happened at all.

Bai Ming whispered again, “Big Senior Brother’s robes are formed by refining leaves sprouted from his body into garments. Most people can’t notice this subtle process. I only found out after my shifu told me.”

Meng Jingzhou’s eyes lit up. Lin Shaoyou belongs to the same generation as Senior Brother Dai Bufan, which means he’s also a peer of Big Senior Sister. And most importantly, we’re not in the Dao-Seeking Sect now.

“Senior Brother Lin, this year...”

Before he could finish, Lu Yang suddenly realized the danger and clamped a hand over Meng Jingzhou’s mouth from behind, yanking him backward.

If you want to court death, don’t drag the rest of us down with you!

Everyone else exchanged perplexed glances, thrown off by Lu Yang’s abrupt reaction.

Lin Shaoyou asked directly, “Did you have a question, Junior Brother Meng?”

“No no, not at all. He was sleep-talking just now,” Lu Yang answered on behalf of Meng Jingzhou.

Bai Ming changed the subject. “By the way, Big Senior Brother, didn’t you recently master a new spell? Why are you practicing another one?”

“Hehe, don’t you know how talented your Big Senior Brother is? When there are new ideas, isn’t it perfectly normal to cultivate new spells?

“So this time you’re cultivating...”

“A fusion of the Tree-Planting Mantra and Draw Ground as Prison to enhance the latter’s strength. It’s troublesome to explain; let me demonstrate once, and you’ll get it.”

Lin Shaoyou took out several tree seeds and scattered them in a circular pattern. The seeds took root instantly and grew rapidly to surround him, the trees’ branches and leaves curving inward to form a birdcage-like structure. The trees gleamed with a metallic luster, resembling the trees from the Metal Branch.

“Watch, just like this.” Lin Shaoyou hammered the iron tree with a punch.

The iron tree didn’t tremble.

He stamped the ground forcefully.

The ground didn’t tremble.

The roots had interwoven beneath the ground, creating an indestructible and sturdy formation.

“That’s amazing!” Bai Ming gasped. This move alone can catch opponents off guard. Trapping peers of the same level won’t be a problem. “Big Senior Brother, your execution seems flawless. Why do you keep practicing it? Is there something you haven’t perfected?”

“This composite spell still has one tiny problem that hasn’t been resolved.”

“What is it?”

“I still don’t know how to dispel it.”

Bai Ming, “...”

He slowly raised his hands and cupped his fists tightly. “Big Senior Brother, please take care.”

With that, Bai Ming ushered the group away, leaving Lin Shaoyou to sigh forlornly. Looks like I can only count on myself.

“GRANNY-SHIFU, SAVE ME!”

Boom! Boom! Boom!

Three bolts of lightning descended, yet Lin Shaoyou remained completely intact.

“Eh? How does that work?”

1. Shinai is the wife of one’s shifu and the wife of one’s grandshifu. ☜

Chapter 539: Useful Ancient Knowledge

“The Five Elements interact through mutual generation and restraint, nourishing and promoting one another. For example, wood begets fire, fire begets earth, earth begets metal, metal begets water, and water begets wood. These constitute the fundamental basis of the universe. The emergence of the five sounds, five flavors, five colors, five transformations, five organs, and five senses is no coincidence; they all correspond to the five elements...”

In the lecture hall, the transmission elder stood upon the podium, expounding on the General Principles of the Five Elements with such fervor that his head swayed and spittle flew. At the most exhilarating points, he would even gesticulate wildly.

Inside the mental space, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy yawned, her eyes glistening with tears as sleepiness tugged at her. The transmission elder’s lecture was far less engaging than the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s storytelling abilities; it was utterly dry and lifeless.

“So boring. The Nine-Layers Immortal had covered all this before.”

“Doesn't the Nine-Layers Immortal wield the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit? How is that related to the five elements?”

“Have you forgotten the Nine-Layers Immortal’s cultivation technique?”

Lu Yang pondered for a moment. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had mentioned it once in the Everlasting Creed, but he couldn’t recall the exact name, except that it involved a lot of numbers.

“Numbers Immortal Art?”

“It’s not exactly wrong, but to be precise, it’s called Primal Chaos, One Qi, Two Origins, Four Divisions, Six Directions, Eight Corners, Nine Lands, Ten Heavens, Only I Reign Supreme Immortal Art.”

As expected of the first individual to become an immortal, even the name of his cultivation technique outshone others in length.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal had delved deeply into subjects like primal hundun chaos, yin and yang, and the five elements. He spent all his time at the Transcendent Tribulation Stage deliberating between which of these Dao Fruits he should choose before finally settling on the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.”

“Why didn’t he choose the other two?”

“In the words of the Nine-Layers Immortal, it’s probably fate, ordained by the heavens even without us knowing.”

“Fate?” Lu Yang could sense the helplessness in the Nine-Layers Immortal’s words, a resignation to fatalism.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy said that some immortals believed in fate while others didn’t. She belongs to the latter, and now it seems like the Nine-Layers Immortal belongs to the former.

“Mmm, the Nine-Layers Immortal struggled with the choice. Each of the three Dao Fruits had its merits and drawbacks. In the end, he resorted to drawing lots.

“The preparation for drawing straws wasted so much effort. First, he exhausted all kinds of secret treasures to construct a great array that blocked spiritual consciousness in the cosmos, with stars serving as its nodes. Then, he summoned the rest of us to act as protectors to guard him. Finally, he closed his eyes and sealed his five senses and seven perceptions to eliminate all external influence before being reassured to proceed with drawing lots.

“The result was the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal was still uneasy after the first draw. He reshuffled everything and drew two more times. Both times, it was the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit.

“A single occurrence might be an accident, but three identical outcomes could only be destiny.”

Lu Yang remarked inwardly, Isn't that just a one-in-nine probability?

But this could be the difference between me and immortals, so I'd better not question.

“Although he chose the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, the Nine-Layers Immortal was still well-versed with primal hundun chaos and the five elements.

“Don’t assume that a Dao Fruit is everything there is to an immortal. As immortals, we often gathered to exchange cultivation insights, experiences, and discoveries. It could be said that our collective reserve of cultivation knowledge was unparalleled!” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy grinned proudly, her smile brimming with wisdom.

Lu Yang nodded. That is true. I’ve heard that the higher one’s cultivation, the more essential it is to confer with peers. A single interaction with those of the same level could equal a hundred years of solitary cultivation. Given how frequently the Five Ancient Immortals gathered, their accumulated knowledge must have reached a terrifying realm, equivalent to a million years of cultivation insights.

“Lu Yang, stand and answer this question.” The transmission elder fixed him with a stern glare. Although my lecture may be dull, I’ve never seen someone like Lu Yang who so blatantly zones out in class.

Lu Yang scrambled to his feet. Having been engrossed in ancient secrets, he had missed the transmission elder’s lesson. He hastily transmitted an auditory message to Meng Jingzhou.

Fortunately, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy could mask the communication, preventing detection by the elder.

“What did the elder say just now?”

“Don’t ask me. I wasn’t listening either.” Meng Jingzhou broke into a cold sweat, dreading being called next.

His mind had also drifted off earlier when the transmission elder mentioned “earth,” leading him to mull over the question: If people are going to be buried after execution anyway, why not just skip straight to burying them alive?

“Man Gu, do you know?”

“No.”

Man Gu was preoccupied with the question: As the last Ancient Barbarian, will I face reproductive barriers with the modern barbarians?

Lu Yang asked everyone he could, but no one was reliable.

“Lu Yang, answer the question. Don’t tell me you weren’t paying attention in class.” The elder transmission continued staring at Lu Yang sharply.

Lu Yang took a deep breath. Now that things have come to this, there’s no other way.

“The Nine-Layers Immortal’s Dao Fruit was the Yin-Yang Dao Fruit, which embodied the power of polarity. The Heaven Mandate Immortal’s Dao Fruit was the Tribulation Mandate Dao Fruit; most tribulations faced by cultivators are its doing. The Epoch Immortal’s Dao Fruit is the Epoch Dao Fruit, which commands the power of time. The Qilin Immortal’s Dao Fruit was the Survival of the Fittest Dao Fruit; any attack that has already been used against him will be rendered ineffective!”

A hush blanketed the lecture hall.

“Elder, is my answer correct?”

The transmission elder blinked, his mind in a haze. I recall Lu Yang rattled off a whole lot, but I just can’t remember a single word.

What did he say?

“Elder? Elder?” Lu Yang called twice before the transmission elder snapped back to his senses.

“Ah? Ah?”

“Elder, don’t tell me you were distracted?”

The transmission elder cleared his throat, pretending he didn’t hear Lu Yang’s remark. “Ahem, Lu Yang’s answer was close enough. Let me repeat: ‘Five’ is nature’s most stable number.

“Consider the central dynasty and the four cardinal regions, the Five Great Immortal Sects, the Five Branches of the Five-Elements Sect, and the Four Great Diabolic Creeds and the enigmatic Heavenly Court Creed. According to the Five-Elements Theory, the Heavenly Court Creed may well become the fifth great diabolic creed, completing the ‘five.’

Meng Jingzhou stealthily transmitted an auditory message to Lu Yang. “That was impressive! How did you pull that off? I heard you spout a bunch of things, but I remembered nothing.”

Lu Yang replied solemnly, “This is an ancient secret spell. Only I can cast it.”

He heaved a sigh of relief. The immortal trait of oblivion really saved me.

The transmission elder soon moved to the key topic of today. “Next, we’ll be talking about five-elements spells. Who among you is most familiar with them?”

“Him.”

Four fingers unanimously pointed at Lu Yang, who took a while to register what had happened.

The transmission elder was stunned but glad. “Oh? I heard you have a Sword Spirit Root. I didn’t expect you to be proficient in five-elements spells. How did you cultivate them? Could you tell me?”

Lu Yang scratched his head awkwardly. How am I supposed to tell you? Cultivating spells comes to me effortlessly. I haven’t even encountered bottlenecks.

“I just followed my instincts. I practiced it a bit here and there, and somehow it succeeded.”

Although the results of the spells were unpredictable, it’s true that the spells themselves somehow succeeded after I practiced a bit here and there.

Chapter 540: Learning the Water-Splitting Technique

“Don’t spout nonsense! How could five-elements spells be that easily mastered?” The transmission elder rebuked Lu Yang. If five-elements spells were really so simple to cultivate, what purpose would our Five-Elements Sect serve?

“Don’t think that just because you lucked into cultivating one or two five-elements spells, you can belittle the study of spells. Which of the five-elements spells have you learned? Show me.”

In the transmission elder’s view, Lu Yang had probably only grasped rudimentary and easy-to-learn spells like Fireball Technique or Earth Wall Technique, thus giving him the mistaken impression that elemental spells were simple.

Lu Yang had no choice but to demonstrate all the spells he had learned one after another.

He opened his right hand, and a golden firebird materialized in his palm. It was lifelike and radiated terrifying heat, igniting the pop quiz booklet the transmission elder had placed on the podium.

He then opened his left hand, and the Three Flavor True Fire blazed fiercely.

The transmission elder was so focused on Lu Yang’s palms that he didn’t notice this minor incident.

“What is this?”

“Golden Bird True Fire and Three Flavor True Fire.”

“What?”

Why haven’t I heard of these two true fires?

Since when did the 108 True Fires become 110?

“What spell is this?” The transmission elder’s eyes nearly popped from their sockets. This is totally unheard of.

“Tree-Planting Mantra.”

Whose Tree-Planting Mantra is like that?!

Before the transmission elder could voice his thoughts, Lu Yang retracted his clones and began burrowing through the earth with ease, even casually opening his mouth to take a few bites of soil.

The transmission elder’s cheek twitched. I’ve never seen a single one of Lu Yang’s five-elements spells. These are certainly no beginner spells.

The transmission elder was flabbergasted. He mastered four out of five elemental spells, all while attaining profound proficiency in sword spells and maintaining cultivation progress.

Could this kid Lu Yang really be that gifted in five-elements spells?

He needs to be reincarnated... It’s such a waste that he joined the Dao-Seeking Sect!

Man Gu scratched his head. I can’t help but feel there are undertones to their words. Or is it just my imagination?

Forget it, I’ll just swim with the tide.

Only Tao Yaoye didn’t speak.

Treacherous intentions!

How could Lu Yang possibly turn down an opportunity to learn a new spell? “Please enlighten me, Elder.”

“Water-Splitting Technique?”

“The Water-Splitting Technique is a water-type spell that is extremely hard to master. Even those with water-aligned Dual Spirit Roots may not succeed. But conversely, its high difficulty hints at the tremendous power it contains. It can be said that once mastered, it will be able to counter all water-type spells!”

Everyone gasped in unison, surprised by how formidable this technique was.

The transmission elder stroked his white beard with a smile. “Legend has it that during the late Great Yu period, ancestral clans and feudal lords rose in rebellion, plunging the world into chaos and bringing misery upon the common folk. However, a great adept led an entire town’s civilians to seek refuge, only to be blocked by a massive river that reached the heavens. Its waves were vast and wild, its currents turbulent and unrelenting, making passage by boat impossible.

“The great adept could naturally cross the river himself, but the commoners behind him could not. He stood by the riverbank, holding his staff, and tapped the ground three times. The sky-reaching river split down the middle, revealing an eighty-meter-wide path, with the waters on both sides rising high to form walls of water. After all the civilians had crossed the enormous river, the water walls on both sides collapsed with a loud crash, and the river returned to its original state.

“This is the Water-Splitting Technique!”

It’s able to split the river into two. Before this mighty ability, no water-element spells would be effective.

“At your current cultivation realm, splitting a river would be too difficult; your body wouldn’t be able to withstand it. However, against water-element spells of the same cultivation stage, there should be no threat.”

Lu Yang drew a sharp breath. This Water-Splitting Technique sounds incredibly powerful.

“Or like this.” The transmission elder took out a cup filled with water and gently drew a line on it.

Instantly, the water inside the cup cleanly separated into two distinct parts. He tilted his head back and drank half the water, while the remaining half remained in its original state.

“Please teach me, Elder.” Lu Yang cupped his fists once more.

“Alright.”

The transmission elder didn’t give Lu Yang special treatment, instead explaining the Water-Splitting Technique to all five of them. This is also a chance to discern Lu Yang’s aptitude for five-elements spells.

“To learn the Water-Splitting Technique, you must calm your breath and focus your mind, concentrate spirit energy in your hands, and form a five-elements water seal with the pads of your thumb and little fingers touching while the other three fingers are extended...” freewebnovel.com

The transmission elder truly lived up to his role as the initiation mentor of the Five-Elements Sect disciples. Though his explanations might seem dry and dull, one would find them clear once they understood the relevant information.

In less than four hours, Lu Yang had grasped the trick to the Water-Splitting Technique, while Meng Jingzhou and the others were limited by their talents in spells, especially those that required a Water Spirit Root. Their learning had progressed very slowly.

“Elder, I’d like to try.”

With a thought from the transmission elder, a water ball hovered before Lu Yang.

“If you can split this water sphere into two, that means you have succeeded.”

Lu Yang formed the five-elements water seal with both hands and silently recited the incantation. “The five lakes and four seas return to the source; nine rivers and eight lakes open in four paths... Split!”

He brought his right middle and index fingers together and pointed at the water sphere. He let out a soft cry, and the water sphere vanished without a trace!

The transmission elder: “...”

This isn’t right. Where’s the water sphere?

“Try again.” He conjured another water sphere and motioned for Lu Yang to give it another attempt.

Lu Yang performed the Water-Splitting Technique, and once again, the water sphere disappeared into thin air.

He was also bewildered. How could a water sphere just vanish out of thin air? It's not like I’m learning void spells.

He sought out the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, “Immortal Fairy, can you see what I just did?”

Hearing Lu Yang was learning spells, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy naturally didn’t miss this scene, having been carefully observing from the mental space all this while. “I saw it. After you cast the Water-Splitting Technique, the water sphere didn’t disappear—it just became too small to see.”

“Too small to see.”

“Mmm, it split into two gases. In one gas, a small sphere orbits around another small sphere. In the other gas, eight small spheres orbit around a small sphere. Both these gases exist in the air and are very common.”

Lu Yang, “...”

So basically, I split water into hydrogen and oxygen?

Chapter 541: Li Haoran’s Strength

The transmission elder had cultivated a Heavenly Eye long ago. When Lu Yang performed the Water-Splitting Technique for the second time, the elder finally discerned its principle. “Ah, you have decomposed the water into two gases—light gas and active gas. Normally, this only occurs when water is struck by lightning spells. I didn’t expect you to achieve the same effect with a simple spell. That’s truly remarkable.

In the cultivation world, even spells like Touching Stone To Gold, which altered matter at the atomic level, could be casually cast. The composition and classification of atoms had long been thoroughly analyzed. The transmission elder could pick up any stone and transmute it into radioactive material.

For cultivators who had attained a first-grade golden core or were at the Great Perfection Nascent Soul Stage, their cultivation had reached a complete and flawless state, rendering them impervious to radioactive substances.

Soon after, the transmission elder’s expression turned peculiar. He stroked his beard as he recalled the most critical question. “However, the technique I taught you was supposed to split water apart and grant immunity to water-type spell attacks. Why does it produce this effect instead?”

Lu Yang replied earnestly, “But this is the Water-Splitting Technique. Look, it splits water apart, separating them into two gases, which are also immune to water-type spell attacks.”

The transmission elder pondered for a long while. He couldn’t shake off the feeling that something was wrong, yet he couldn’t pinpoint what it was exactly. Whether it’s the name or the effect, it’s no different from the Water-Splitting Technique.

This is the Water-Splitting Technique.

After spending half a day trying to learn the Water-Splitting Technique without success, he simply gave up on it altogether.

The transmission elder hesitated but finally nodded. “Since you’ve mastered the five types of elemental spells, you can now combine them according to the Five-Elements Theory and form powerful combination spells through mutual promotion of the five elements in endless cycles.”

Then, the transmission elder fell silent. Over a thousand years of instructing disciples of the Five-Elements Sect, I’ve seen all kinds of five-elemental spells. I can guide any disciple in combining the spells based on the elements they’ve grasped.

But someone like Lu Yang...

Truth be told, I’ve never seen any of the five-elements spells Lu Yang has mastered...

“The five-elements spells are proof of your dedication to spells. As an outsider, it would be presumptuous of me to dictate your cultivation path. Cultivation emphasizes following one’s true self. Why don’t we do this? After class, you can practice how to form composite five-elemental spells on your own.

“Next, we’ll proceed with the pop quiz. No cheating.”

The transmission elder turned to retrieve the pop quiz papers from the podium, only to find them reduced to a pile of ashes. While the transmission elder wasn’t paying attention earlier, Lu Yang’s Golden Bird True Flame had spat out a flicker of fire and incinerated the papers.

Despite their vast experience in acting, the five struggled to suppress their smirks.

With a stormy expression, the transmission elder dismissed the class.

~~~

“Junior Brother Li, do you really want to challenge me?” Lu Yang looked at Li Haoran with an unreadable smile, surprised that the latter had sought him out.

This wasn’t a reckless decision. Lu Yang’s strength is clear to all, but I’m not firing arrows blindly. I possess half of Qin Haoran’s memories, which include numerous formidable spells. Unlike others, I don’t have to decipher the usage of these spells painstakingly; I can cast them right away

This was the source of his confidence in challenging Lu Yang.

“Good! I’ve been looking for a chance to test my combination spells. I’ll agree to your challenge then!” Lu Yang flashed an excited smile, brimming with eagerness.

First, he had the Everlasting Immortal Fairy expand her immortal consciousness to inspect the surroundings and ensure no one, such as the transmission elders, would see him using five-elements spells, particularly metal-type ones.

“Fight! Fight! Fight!” Meng Jingzhou egged them on, wishing the spectacle would be bigger. I can’t wait to see what sneaky ideas this grandson Lu Yang will come up with again this time.

Tao Yaoye and Man Gu also stood nearby. Man Gu had procured a lamb from the dining hall and was using Corpse-Driving Techniques to make the lamb’s corpse dance atop the Three Flavor True Fire. The trio tore off chunks of crispy and fragrant roasted mutton every now and then.

In fact, with Lu Yang’s Three Flavor True Fire, they didn’t even need seasoning; the flavor was a tier higher than what they had at the Corpse-Driving Sect.

Enjoying a meal while watching a battle—what a splendid life.

Although Li Haoran didn’t know why Lu Yang was immune to curses, he trusted the latter wouldn’t lie to him in this regard.

That makes one less method I can use.

The fact that Qin Haoran could transfer his debts to Shi Huagu shows that he must be proficient in karmic spells. It’s just losing one method; not a huge problem.

The purple divine lightning erupted, ionizing the air as it morphed into a snarling lightning dragon lunging at Lu Yang.

Lu Yang seemed to have anticipated his move, sidestepping the last moment and evading the attack. The lightning dragon missed and crashed into the ground, leaving it charred.

“Wind Borrowing!”

A gale howled, whipping up flying sand and stones. The cloud of dust stirred up obscured one’s vision and even blocked spiritual consciousness. However, Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness far surpassed that of ordinary cultivators. Though its range was limited, he detected three attacks concealed within the duststorm.

“Golden Bird True Flame.”

Two golden birds circled Lu Yang, forming a whirlwind of flames. The three attacks collided with the fiery whirlwind and vanished without even changing the direction of the wind.

Li Haoran remained unperturbed. “I know. Single attacks are ineffective against you, Senior Brother Lu. But what if the numbers increase?”

“Palm Lightning!”

Four bolts of lightning shot forth simultaneously.

Lu Yang’s expression sharpened as he controlled the two golden birds to transform into two streaks of light. They collided with the four lightning bolts, resulting in a deafening boom. freewebnovel.com

“How’s that, Senior Brother Lu?” Li Haoran smirked, his four arms moving around as new attacks gathered in his palms.

“Four arms?” Lu Yang was stunned.

Blocked by the dust earlier, Lu Yang hadn’t noticed how Li Haoran managed it. But Meng Jingzhou and the others had witnessed everything clearly.

While Lu Yang was preoccupied with the attacks, Li Haoran had ripped off his two arms partially, leaving the bones connected. Then, he used the Rebirth Golden Core to regenerate the two arms while simultaneously sprouting two additional arms from his armpits.

With that, he had four arms.

Li Haoran knew ordinary spells wouldn’t suffice against Lu Yang. If one or two ordinary techniques are ineffective, what about casting four types of spells with four arms at the same time?!

If not for the immense strain of his four-armed state, Li Haoran would have gladly grown six arms for this battle. Although he couldn’t perform Three-Heads Six-Arms, he could still replicate its effects through other means.

Chapter 542: Five-Elements Spell Combination

Meng Jingzhou and the other two watched while eating roasted lamb, applauding Li Haoran’s ingenious move.

“Brilliant idea! You can’t use conventional methods against Lu Yang!” Meng Jingzhou praised heartily. As Lu Yang’s long-time rival, he knew ordinary means wouldn’t work; only unorthodox strategies with the element of surprise stood a chance.

“The skin tastes pretty good; it’s even more flavorful than the meat.” Meng Jingzhou smacked his lips. He had been eating the crispy and fragrant lamb skin, which crackled between his teeth and left a lingering aroma. Paired with chives to alleviate the greasiness, the flavor was perfection. The meat beneath the skin pales a tiny bit in comparison.

Meng Jingzhou’s gaze inadvertently fell on the blazing Three Flavor True Fire, and he punched his palm. “I’ve got an idea!”

He flicked a wisp of Nirvana True Fire into the Three Flavor True Fire. The two true fires merged with a crackle.

Under the Nirvana True Fire’s influence, the lamb carcass gradually regrew its skin. As the regeneration was slow, the Three Flavor True Fire could sear it meticulously, making the flavor even more incredible.

Man Gu’s eyes lit up at this scene. I never imagined the Nirvana True Fire could be used this way.

As he hadn’t encountered the Three Flavor True Fire in the past, it was understandable that he hadn’t associated it with barbecue. However, every cultivator knew of the famed Nirvana True Fire.

How could I have failed to realize it could be used in barbecue? This is totally unacceptable!

I’m an utter disgrace as the successor to the Barbarian Clan’s barbecue legacy!

I knew I could learn real skills by following Brother Lu and Brother Meng!

As a Confucian cultivator, Man Gu adhered to the sages’ teachings: “In a company of three, all are my teachers” and “One should reflect on themselves three times daily.” He constantly engaged in introspection to compensate for his shortcomings.

The Palm Lightning likewise dissipated upon impact.

Lu Yang no longer held back and delivered a brutal punch. As Li Haoran was an artifact cultivator, he couldn’t compete in close quarters with Lu Yang. When it came to close combat, only top-notch physique cultivators like Meng Jingzhou or Confucian cultivators like Man Gu could suppress Lu Yang.

Li Haoran reacted swiftly. He knew he couldn’t face the Arhat Fist head-on, so he immediately ripped the two arms off his armpits and hastily refined them into magical treasures to hurl at Lu Yang.

Crash! Crash! Crash!

The silver lining for Li Haoran was that he was wearing a wig, so he wouldn’t suffer hair loss.

Lu Yang summoned a golden body resembling himself, which descended from the sky and encased Li Haoran.

Lu Yang burrowed into the ground, and seeds sprouted, producing two Lu Yangs.

This was the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body’s flaw—its base was unsealed. One could flee with the Earth Escape Technique.

Just then, Lu Yang’s clone arrived underground, tracing a circle around the golden body’s base.

“Draw Underground Prison.”

The ground beneath the golden body became an underground prison, blocking off Li Haoran’s escape route and forcing him back to the surface.

Henceforth, the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body would have no more weakness.

Li Haoran sneered. “I’d like to see what a clone can do to me!”

Lu Yang’s clone emerged from the soil and entered the interior of the golden body.

Li Haoran’s arms turned jade-white, piercing clean through Lu Yang’s clone with a squelch.

The clone was completely unaffected, as if the body wasn’t its own.

“Sleeve Cosmos.”

An endless stream of lake water gushed out from the clone’s right hand, flooding the golden body instantly.

Lu Yang must have stored water in his palm before the battle began and transferred it to his clone during the high-five.

I was careless!

“Water-Splitting Technique!”

Within three breaths, the water that filled the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body disappeared, decomposing into hydrogen and oxygen.

Along with a bird’s cry, golden flames flashed inside the golden body, and the massive explosion cracked even the golden body’s interior.

Tao Yaoye analyzed earnestly, “It’s not just that. Senior Brother Lu split the water into two gases that seemed to have amplified the explosion.” The Golden Bird True Flame alone shouldn’t have caused such a huge blast; there must be other factors at play.

Lu Yang dispelled the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body and found only two charred corpses.

In the split second before the explosion, Li Haoran had performed a teleportation-like technique to swap places with his clone.

Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness had long detected Li Haoran’s clone buried underground. He surmised it was originally meant for an ambush. Though it went unused, it ended up saving his life.

Pop! Li Haoran emerged from the ground behind Lu Yang.

“Of course I want to con—” Li Haoran was not ready to admit defeat, but his vision suddenly blurred, causing him to stagger and nearly collapse.

“Poisoned...? No, what is this?” Li Haoran realized something had gone wrong with his body, preventing him from continuing to battle. But I don’t remember breathing in any poison though.

What’s going on?

“Junior Brother Li, do you know that while active gas is essential for living beings to survive, inhaling it in excessive amounts would instead result in symptoms like dizziness and chest tightness.

“From the start of the battle, I’ve been casting the Water-Splitting Technique to break down the water in the air into light gas and active gas. As the concentration of active gas rose, you naturally couldn’t keep up.

“Junior Brother Li, if you had paid closer attention, you would have noticed that I was holding my breath the entire time.

“Well, do you still want to continue fighting?”

“I admit defeat.”

Chapter 543: It’s Perfectly Normal for Disciples of the Righteous Path to Know How to Concoct Bone-Dissolving Water

Seeing Lu Yang emerge victorious, Tao Yaoye’s eyes sparkled as she led the applause.

“What a spectacular battle!”

Meng Jingzhou and Man Gu pondered a moment, then wiped the grease from their lips and hands before joining the applause.

“It wasn’t easy winning this match,” Lu Yang lamented.

Li Haoran was a formidable opponent. After the fight, Lu Yang was exhausted, his whole body aching. If not for Li Haoran’s lack of combat experience and limited exposure, my chain five-elements spells wouldn’t have forced him into performing the Shadow-Swap Teleportation technique, draining his spirit energy and leaving him in a state of oxygen intoxication.

“Junior Brother Li, you’ll need to pay more attention in your next battle. If I’d faced Old Meng, I wouldn’t have dared to use this trick against him. That grandson’s too much of a crafty trickster to be tricked by something so simple.”

Li Haoran, “...”

I’ve inherited half of Qin Haoran’s memories, so how did I become someone who lacks combat experience and has limited exposure in Senior Brother Lu’s eyes?

Qin Haoran was a full-fledged Fusion cultivator. Since I’ve received half of his legacy, I should be considered a Half-Step Fusion cultivator, right?

Fine. Compared to Senior Brother Lu and Senior Brother Meng, Qin Haoran’s memories and legacy are indeed not that useful.

Li Haoran stood before the charred remains of his clone, lost in thought before letting out a soft sigh. “Senior Brother Lu is truly stronger.”

Lu Yang understood how Li Haoran felt. That clone was a fallback that Li Haoran had carefully prepared, yet it ended up being sacrificed with the Shadow-Swap Teleportation technique. If his real body had been inside the Sixteen-Foot Golden Body and got blasted, what would have happened?

Lu Yang stepped forward and patted Li Haoran’s shoulder to console him. “Don’t be discouraged, Junior Brother Li. The spells you’ve mastered are more than enough. It’s just that your line of thinking isn’t correct—it’s too straightforward and honest. You’ll easily lose out if you run into someone cunning and treacherous.”

“...I’m not discouraged. I’m just wondering how to deal with my corpse. Senior Brother Lu, your clone is made of wood. Once the spell is lifted, it will automatically merge back with the earth. But my clone is made from my own flesh.”

The same problem applied to the two extra arms Li Haoran had grown.

Lu Yang mulled over it and realized Li Haoran was right. Dealing with Junior Brother Li’s corpse is indeed a complicated matter.

“Never mind. As much as it pains me, there’s only one way.”

Li Haoran fished out a small vial of liquid from his identity jade pendant. Upon uncorking it, a pungent odor immediately assaulted their nostrils. With a poker face, he poured out the dark green liquid onto the clone. Thick white smoke rose as the clone rapidly dissolved before their eyes.

Man Gu inhaled a sharp breath. “Junior Brother Li, what is this?”

“Bone-Dissolving Water. It’s from Qin Haoran’s memories. I concocted a few vials of it.”

The ingredients were complex, and he had spent considerable contribution points to gather all of them. The last time he failed in controlling his clone to participate in the finals, this was how he had disposed of it.

I have no other way. I can’t possibly dig a grave for myself at such a young age and bury my clone. Even if I don’t believe in fate, that feels inauspicious.

“Hey, the five fellows there, what are you doing?!”

“Oh no, it’s the transmission elder.”

The commotion from their battle had been loud enough to draw the attention of the transmission elder, who headed over to investigate. By the time he arrived, the battle had concluded, and he happened to see Li Haoran pouring out the liquid as white smoke billowed.

Man Gu was worried the transmission elder would misunderstand, so he hastily came forward to explain. “Don’t misunderstand, Elder! Junior Brother Li was just disposing of a corpse and erasing all traces—nothing else!”

The transmission elder nearly struck down the reincarnation of a former diabolic creed leader in the name of justice.

Fortunately, Lu Yang and Meng Jingzhou managed to clarify the situation with their eloquence.

Li Haoran stared at Man Gu with an aggrieved look.

“Ah, so Lu Yang has successfully combined five-elements spells and was testing them in actual combat.” The transmission elder nodded, extremely pleased.

To think that after my lecture this morning, Lu Yang has already figured out how to form combination spells by evening.

What astonishing speed.

Lu Yang also felt the Unbeatable Golden Core’s proposed solution had worked astonishingly fast.

The transmission elder didn’t press for details on how Lu Yang had combined the spells. Since Lu Yang didn’t seek my guidance, it means there are things he prefers to keep private. That’s perfectly understandable.

“Wait a minute, where did you get the Bone-Dissolving Water formula?” The transmission elder suddenly realized another problem.

They’re disciples of the righteous path, so why do they know the formula of the Bone-Dissolving Water?

Li Haoran’s eyelid twitched, unsure how to explain. I can’t possibly say I am Qin Haoran’s reincarnation. While the Dao-Seeking Sect is able to accept this identity of mine and believe that past and present lives are unrelated, the Five-Elements Sect’s stance is unclear.

As the team leader, Meng Jingzhou offered a serious explanation. “Our Dao-Seeking Sect annihilated the Everlasting Creed with the imperial court and confiscated some of their resources, like pill formulas. The Bone-Dissolving Water formula was one of them.

“As members of the righteous path, the eradication of diabolic creeds ought to be our foremost duty. The diabolic creeds are cunning, treacherous, deceitful, and full of stratagems and underhanded means. Only by understanding their methods can we better eliminate them!”

“So that’s how it is. I thought you had learned it from that old Taciturn scoundrel. Alright, as long as you’re fine. I was wondering whether an accident had happened with all that noise. Get some rest; there’s another lesson tomorrow.”

“Yes.”

~~~

“We will be learning the Five-Elements Combat Tactic. Essentially, it aligns each of you with one of the Five Elements based on your personal traits, enabling the five of you to combine forces in battle and unleash even greater power.”

Hearing that, the five of them perked up, their eyes twinkling. Today’s lesson is far more interesting than yesterday’s.

“According to the records provided by the Dao-Seeking Sect and my own observations, I’ve ascertained that the five of you each correspond to a different element, making you ideal for this combat method.
