“Wood governs change, existing between illusion and reality. Tao Yaoye, whether it’s your proficiency in illusions or your Metamorphic Immortal Physique, both relate to change. You correspond to the Wood position.

“Water governs restoration. Meng Jingzhou, I initially thought you could serve as a support with the fire element. But since you’ve mastered the Nirvana True Fire, which can heal injuries, it’s destined that you fit the water element better. You correspond to the Water position.”

“Wait, Elder,” Meng Jingzhou protested. “I have so much yang energy. How can I stand in the Water position?” From Meng Jingzhou’s perspective, water represented yin, which was completely at odds with him.

The transmission elder was bewildered by Meng Jingzhou’s question. “But don’t you have a Single’s Spirit Root? Your kidney water is abundant.” With Meng Jingzhou’s yang-boosting Nirvana True Fire, his kidney water had only grown more plentiful. Furthermore, thanks to his Single’s Spirit Root, there was absolutely no risk of water leakage.

Meng Jingzhou, “...”

Don’t think I can’t beat you...even if it’s true that I can’t beat you!

“Fire governs support. Li Haoran, you have a Fire Spirit Root. You are also a disciple of Zhou Xin and an artifact-refining master. The Fire position suits you perfectly.

“Earth governs defense. Man Gu, as an Ancient Barbarian, you’re a natural-born physique cultivator. The Ancient Barbarian Tribe was renowned for their defensive power. You correspond to the Earth position.”

Chapter 544: Five-Elements Combat Tactic

After finalizing their positions, the transmission elder led the five of them outdoors and had them stand according to their assigned five elements. With his hands clasped behind his back, he spoke in a clear and resonant voice.

“If you wish to achieve perfect coordination, you must first know yourselves and each other. The five of you are of similar age and cultivation realm, which should make this process much easier. Release your auras and carefully sense the cultivation realms of the other four.

Lu Yang and the other four sat cross-legged and closed their eyes, releasing their aura waves while perceiving the external world with their spiritual consciousness.

“Hmm? Such strong spiritual consciousness,” the transmission elder exclaimed softly. He noticed that Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s spiritual consciousness stood out the most, significantly stronger than the others. And Lu Yang’s spiritual consciousness is even stronger than Meng Jingzhou’s; the difference is apparent.

“Spiritual consciousness is the hardest to cultivate. To this day, I've never heard of any method of cultivating the spiritual consciousness at this stage. How did these two kids manage it?

“Ah, yes. Meng Jingzhou has a Single’s Spirit Root. The documents provided by the Dao-Seeking Sect showed that he formed the unprecedented Double Single’s Golden Core. His yang energy is abundant, and his desires are stronger. However, as a Single’s Spirit Root cultivator, he must constantly restrain those urges. Such tempering would naturally lead to a powerful spiritual consciousness.

“But what about Lu Yang? Did Yun Zhi impart an untransmitted spell to him? Or did that old Taciturn scoundrel stumble upon a fluke solution like a blind cat finding a dead mouse?”

Having endured the relentless torment of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, Lu Yang was especially skilled with his spiritual consciousness. Without any concealment of auras, he could sense the cultivation realms of three junior brothers and sisters and one “grandson.”

All four had reached the Advanced Golden Core Stage. Even Li Haoran, the slowest among them, had successfully broken through before their departure. Li Haoran had spent a year soaking in lava during the Qi Training Stage, delaying his progress. But now, with his accumulated strength, he had finally caught up with the others.

Lu Yang also sensed Meng Jingzhou’s overflowing qi, blood, and yang energy, so terrifying that ordinary ghosts would be scorched with a mere glance.

Of course, not all ghosts fear Meng Jingzhou. Female ghosts like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy aren’t scared of him at all.

After roughly an hour, everyone opened their eyes, now fully aware of each other’s capabilities.

“Next, we’ll proceed with the second step—spirit energy transmission.”

The transmission elder had the five lined up in the order of Metal, Wood, Water, Fire, and Earth. Starting with Man Gu, each placed their hands on the back of the person in front, channeling their spirit energy in sequence until Tao Yaoye transmitted the combined spirit energy, including her own, to Lu Yang.

Lu Yang’s eyes instantly turned bloodshot. Though he had prepared himself, the sudden surge of overwhelming spirit energy still exceeded his expectations, pushing him dangerously close to his limit.

“Release all of it!” the transmission elder commanded loudly.

Lu Yang sheathed his Qingfeng Sword and merged his essence, qi, and mind into one. Sword qi expanded explosively, resembling a sash of white silk.

“Slash!”

The combined spirit energy of the five morphed into sword qi, cascading down like a flood that breached a dam.

Boom!

A ten-meter-long sword qi cleaved downward like a waterfall, crashing into the pool with boundless power. In a split second, the winds and clouds shifted, a deafening impact shook the earth, and the ground split into a fathomless fissure.

Huff... Huff... Huff...

After unleashing that sword strike, the five’s spirit energy was completely drained. Their legs trembled and eventually buckled. They sat on the ground, staring at the chasm they had created and grinning like fools.

Even Lu Yang was stunned by the sheer power of that attack; it was the strongest sword strike he had ever executed. “Did you see that sword strike of mine? I knew it would contain such mighty power!”

“That sword strike of yours was nothing. The surge of aura waves Man Gu and Li Haoran channeled nearly crushed me. I was using the Nirvana True Fire to repair my meridians while dispersing the energy at the same time!

“Man Gu, you transferred way too much spirit energy.”

“I just wanted it to be more powerful.”

The five chatted animatedly, their faces brimming with excitement as they recounted the process of unleashing the attack.

The transmission elder handed each of them a bottle of Great Rejuvenation Pills and nodded in approval. “For a first joint attack, that sword strike was not bad. Next time, be careful not to expend all your energy at once; keep some in reserve.

“The Five-Elements Combat Tactic has been around for many years. Old Song and the four other branch elders use it frequently, but even they have only unleashed their full power seven or eight times. And when they did, it was truly savage—they held nothing back and left no path of retreat for themselves.” freewebnovel.com

“Was it because they faced formidable enemies?”

“They faced your Dao-Seeking Sect’s elders.”

Everyone was speechless.

“Oh, and the old Taciturn scoundrel.” The transmission elder emphasized the keynote figure.

Everyone was speechless once again.

The transmission elder clicked his tongue, shuddering at the memory of those battles.

Truly exhilarating.

“Did the sect leader cause trouble again?” Tao Yaoye asked. For the five branch elders to unleash the full might of the Five-Elements Combat Tactic, just how deep was the grudge?

“That was seven to eight hundred years ago. The old Taciturn scoundrel took your Fifth Elder and Eighth Elder to the Golden Buddhist Kingdom and built a temple there. Whether it was legal or not is unclear, but anyway, the temple was successfully constructed. It thrived with visitors and received incredibly abundant incense offerings. I bet they used some marketing tactic, given how many worshippers flocked there.”

Tao Yaoye was still bemused. “Was there a problem with that?"

“The problem was that the old Taciturn scoundrel named the temple the ‘Five Organs Temple,’ enshrining and worshipping the five branch elders. The Golden Buddhist Kingdom mistakenly thought our Five-Elements Sect was trying to steal their business; they were just short of sending a cross-border arrest order to the imperial court.

“Fortunately, Old Qiu figured out the situation in time and intervened to clarify. Only then did the Golden Buddhist Kingdom withdraw the arrest order.

“When the old Taciturn scoundrel was getting beaten up, he claimed it was an experiment—to see if Old Song and the others could sense the power of faith.

“Old Song roared back, asking why he didn’t offer himself up as the object of worship. The old Taciturn scoundrel said he was afraid of becoming wanted.”

Tao Yaoye, “...”

The sect leader absolutely deserved that beating.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy observed the tremendous power in Lu Yang’s sword strike and chuckled with amusement. “This Five-Elements Combat Tactic is quite something. It’s creative; the Nine-Layers Immortal came up with something similar.”

Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. The Five-Elements Combat Tactic is already incredibly powerful. Given that the Nine-Layers Immortal was an immortal with a broader vision, just how terrifying must his creation have been?! “Please elaborate, Immortal Fairy.”

“When we Five Ancient Immortals gathered to exchange cultivation insights, the Nine-Layers Immortal proposed an idea to merge yin-yang and the five elements to provide future generations a reference. If later generations could comprehend the marvelous mysteries within, they would surely make considerable improvements in the study of yin-yang and the five elements.

“Did the Nine-Layers Immortal succeed?” Lu Yang asked hurriedly.

“He did. It’s called Five in a Row. Haven’t you played it before?”

Lu Yang, “...”

Once the five had mostly recovered, the transmission elder had them resume transmitting spirit energy, with Lu Yang as the output. However, they were to hold back their power to avoid the overexhaustion they experienced the first time.

After several attempts, the five quickly learned how to control the amount of energy transferred.

“Next, we’ll begin the second step. Stand in the same order, but form a circle. Lu Yang, place your hands on Man Gu’s back. You will channel spirit energy to the person in front of you. Control both the speed and quantity of spirit energy. If it’s too fast or too much, the recipient won’t be able to withstand it.”

Chapter 545: No Trade, No Slaughter

The five of them channeled spirit energy to the person in front. Since the transmission of spirit energy inevitably incurred losses, it would eventually drain them completely.

Fortunately, Lu Yang had taught the other four the Swallowing Heaven cultivation method. While transferring energy, they opened their mouths wide to devour ambient spirit energy, making the transmission elder wonder if they had been possessed.

Transmitting the spirit energy also allowed them to achieve the realm of “me within you, you within me.” By now, Lu Yang’s spirit energy hardly belonged to him anymore; it was intertwined with the other four’s, and vice versa. Their spirit energy had merged seamlessly.

The transmission elder hadn’t anticipated them reaching this state so quickly.

“Next, we’ll begin with the third step—practicing combination abilities...”

~~~

“Speaking of which, the Five Great Immortal Sect’s exchange should be underway,” Dai Bufan murmured while sorting intelligence reports. “Junior Brother Lu Yang and the other four have already arrived at the Five-Elements Sect, so why hasn’t Shi Chan from the Hanging Monastery shown up yet?

“Could something have happened?”

~~~

A handsome monk strode out of a slaughterhouse, heading toward the nearest docking point for flying vessels.

“What a fragrant aroma.”

The monk’s nose twitched as he passed a bustling restaurant at noon, the peak hour for business. The wafting aromas of dishes halted him in his tracks.

A meal wouldn’t delay boarding the flying vessel. He changed his itinerary at the last minute and entered the restaurant.

“Waiter, are there seats available?”

“Master, you’ve come to the right place! Our Thousand-Li Fragrance Restaurant’s vegetarian dishes are the best!”

“I don’t want vegetarian dishes. Bring me two jin of braised beef in soy paste,[1] a portion of red-braised pork knuckle in soy sauce,[2] and a bowl of lamb offal noodles.”[3]

The waiter sized up the monk in surprise, wondering if he had misheard. Many people pretend to be monks these days, but I’ve never seen such a blatantly fake one. This has nothing to do with me though. I just serve whatever customers order.

“One moment, guest.” freewebnovel.com

Soon, a platter of beef, a portion of pork knuckle, and a bowl of noodles were served.

Shi Chan enjoyed his meal at a leisurely pace.

“Guest, that’ll be sixty-six copper coins in total.”

The monk wiped his mouth and said placidly, “My shifu often tells me: ‘no trade, no slaughter.’ If no one ate meat, no one would have to slaughter livestock. This restaurant of yours also wouldn’t serve meat dishes, only vegetarian dishes. He warned us never to order meat at restaurants, for it will foment improper practices.”

The waiter was utterly flummoxed by his speech. “Guest, so you want to...”

“Dine and dash. No payment means no trade.”

~~~

At the Dao-Seeking Sect’s mountain gate, two disciples on guard duty yawned idly, chatting about recent events.

“Finally, no more marriage proposals for Junior Brother Lu. Peace at last.”

“Right? I’d never seen a queue of people come knocking for marriage. It was truly an eye-opener.”

A tall figure approached, palms pressed together, and asked in a clear voice, “May I ask if this is the Dao-Seeking Sect?”

The visitor was handsome and draped in a worn-out kasaya robe. His eyes shone brightly with spirit, clear as pond water, and his head was smooth with no hair. If not for the kasaya robe, the disciples might have mistaken him for a victim of Lu Yang’s Arhat Fist coming to seek revenge.

“Junior Brother Shi Chan of the Hanging Monastery?” one disciple probed tentatively, recalling Dai Bufan’s notice about the immortal sects’ exchange period, where a monk from the Hanging Monastery would visit the Dao-Seeking Sect for a study exchange.

“That is me. Apologies for my tardiness. Washing dishes proved time-consuming.”

Baffled by Shi Chan’s words, the disciple said politely, “Please wait here a moment. I’ll fetch Senior Brother Dai.”

One disciple left to look for Dai Bufan, while the other continued guarding the gate.

Soon, Dai Bufan rushed over to find Shi Chan sitting in meditation at the gate.

Noticing Shi Chan’s dignified bearing, thick brows, righteous-looking countenance, and rock-solid foundation, Dai Bufan nodded inwardly. All these signify real skills—as expected of the disciple groomed by Master Jiesha.

Hovering in a lotus position midair, Shi Chan sensed Dai Bufan’s presence and rose to bow. “Greetings, Senior Brother Dai.”

“Junior Brother Shi Chan, you’re here alone?”

“My senior brothers in the monastery are occupied and couldn’t escort me.”

“Occupied?”

“Yes. Shifu received news of your esteemed sect leader’s whereabouts in Wilderness Province and led my senior uncle and all my senior brothers there.”

Dai Bufan, “...”

If memory serves me right, my shifu values the code of brotherhood and is currently impersonating the Taciturn Daoist Priest to spin tales through storytelling in Wilderness Province.

Could the so-called news Master Jiesha received be about Shifu?

Never mind. Shifu has his own fortune; there’s no need for me, his disciple, to fret. At worst, he’ll get a beating—he won’t die.

“Please enter, Junior Brother Shi Chan.”

Dai Bufan personally hosted Shi Chan. I hope my hospitality will move Master Jiesha and persuade him to go easier on Shifu when he beats him.

Crossing the River Spirit’s territory, the two arrived at the heart of the Dao-Seeking Sect, where Shi Chan was stunned to see the vibrant bustle. Compared to the Hanging Monastery, the Dao-Seeking Sect is way too lively.

“Junior Brother Shi Chan, how much do you know about our Dao-Seeking Sect? What do you wish to learn here?”

“When my shifu could still speak, he told me a lot about your esteemed sect. He mentioned you have abundant cultivation resources and numerous cultivation techniques, especially the scripture library’s troves.

“There are two abilities I would like to learn.”

“Speak your mind, Junior Brother.”

“I heard that Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s Arhat Fist can make victims lose their hair. May I learn it?”

“Umm...” Dai Bufan showed a troubled expression. Of all people, why choose to learn from Lu Yang? Is that even something that can be learned? “To be honest, Junior Brother Lu’s Arhat Fist is truly unique. No one else in the sect can perform it, and he’s currently at the Five-Elements Sect for exchange.”

“Then what about Fellow Daoist Meng Jingzhou’s Single’s Curse Fist, which encompasses karma. May I learn it?”

Dai Bufan, “...”

Kid, are you sure you’re not here to stir trouble? You insist on learning whatever’s unavailable.

“Neither?” Shi Chan was visibly deflated.

He had long admired these two fist techniques, believing them to be the true mighty abilities of Buddhist sects—even the Deliverance Sutra and Sixteen-Foot Golden Body couldn’t compare.

It’s a pity the people who can execute them are absent.

“Perhaps fate has yet to arrive; forcing it would be inappropriate. Senior Brother Dai, do carry on with your work. I will take a stroll through the sect. Despite the Dao-Seeking Sect’s long-standing reputation, I have yet to witness it myself. This is the perfect opportunity for me to broaden my horizons.”

Dai Bufan was indeed swamped. As the de facto head of the Great Mission Hall, even a day’s rest would accumulate a mountain of work.

“Hold on to this token—having this is as good as my being present. You may move about the sect as you please, including places such as the scripture library. If you have any questions, you can ask the nearby disciples, and they will gladly assist you.”

Shi Chan accepted Dai Bufan’s token and thanked him.

~~~

Dai Bufan returned to the Great Mission Hall but didn’t attend to the matters at hand. He pondered for a moment and produced a jade disc—a magical treasure used for communication between him and First Elder.

He wrote on the magical treasure: Shifu, Junior Brother Shi Chan said Master Jiesha has led everyone in the Hanging Monastery to Wilderness Province in search of the sect leader. Since you’re impersonating him there to tell pingshu stories, you might encounter them. Please be extra careful.

Dai Bufan tapped the middle of the jade disc to send the message.

First Elder’s reply came swiftly.

Say sooner next time

Dai Bufan fell silent for a bit as he analyzed the message. “He didn’t even write the punctuation. Looks like the battle is fierce.

“Shifu is Shifu after all—plotting strategies with keen foresight. He must have predicted this calamity long ago. No wonder he built all those tombs.”

Chapter 546: Real Knowledge Comes From Practice

Immersing himself in the Dao-Seeking Sect’s atmosphere, Shi Chan felt a surge of emotion. He could sense the entire place pulsing with positivity and vitality—a stark contrast from the Hanging Monastery.

This kind of lively atmosphere is exactly what our Hanging Monastery lacks.

“No wonder the word on the street is that the Dao-Seeking Sect is the number one great immortal sect. There’s indeed some substance to the rumors.”

The so-called “word on the street” referred to the pingshu story, Saga of the Dao-Seeking Sect.

He lingered by the arena stages, watching disciples exchange dazzling techniques, whose spectacular duels elicited cheers and applause from the audience. Since the Dao-Seeking Sect disciples knew each other, his unfamiliar face stood out, though it didn’t take long for them to deduce who he was.

“Are you Junior Brother Shi Chan from the Hanging Monastery? Care to step onto the stage for a sparring match?”

Shi Chan smiled and shook his head in refusal, stating forthrightly that he had come to the Dao-Seeking Sect to seek Buddhist spells, not to engage in strife—that would go against his original intent.

You must be joking! Every one of you is at least at the Nascent Soul Stage. If I could win, pigs would fly. That’s not called a sparring match—it’s called a beating.

“Shifu often said the Taciturn Daoist Priest possesses both Buddha and diabolic natures. Left unchecked, he would bring calamity to the mortal realm. The Taciturn Daoist Priest’s cultivation advanced too swiftly, and only Shifu could suppress him. I wonder what the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s disciples are like.”

He inquired with people nearby for information on Lu Yang.

Lu Yang was quite the legendary figure in the Dao-Seeking Sect. His tenure as acting sect leader for two months and three days had thrust him into the spotlight. Whenever his name was brought up, any disciple would have something to say about him.

“I didn’t expect Lu Yang to abuse his authority as acting sect leader to force his own victory—truly contemptible! However, his reputation here in the Dao-Seeking Sect is surprisingly not bad. No wonder he could cultivate the Arhat Fist. It seems that Fellow Daoist Lu Yang’s Buddha nature is deep, and he is destined for a bright future. I suppose his misuse of the acting sect leader's authority was due to being possessed by a great devil, which led him astray. May he be forgiven and blessed. Sādhu, excellent.”

Compared to the Taciturn Daoist Priest, Lu Yang is upright and aboveboard, and his reputation in the Dao-Seeking Sect is excellent.

“Based on what I’ve heard from all the senior brothers and sisters, the Taciturn Daoist Priest has four disciples, and Lu Yang is the fourth. The second and third disciples are away from the Central Continent, leaving only the eldest disciple to look after Heaven’s Gate Peak.

“Shifu always warned me not to provoke the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple. But as they say, ‘real knowledge comes from practice.’ Scriptures are merely the experiences of those before us. How can I copy them directly? Let me test it first.”

~~~

Following the directions, Shi Chan arrived at Heaven’s Gate Peak, where he found Yun Zhi in the middle of cultivation.

Yun Zhi retracted her powers and eyed Shi Chan with slight bemusement. Why is a disciple from the Hanging Monastery looking for me?

“This little monk is a disciple of the Hanging Monastery. My Buddhist name is Shi Chan. Senior, may I ask if you’re the Taciturn Daoist Priest’s eldest disciple?

“Yes, I am. What brings you here, Junior Brother Shi Chan?”

“I’ve heard that your cultivation is peerless and unbeatable among peers at your realm, Senior Yun Zhi. Would it be possible for you to suppress your cultivation to the Advanced Golden Stage and spar with me?”

“Sure.”

“To be honest, I’ve never been defeated since I began my path in cultivation. I’m rather confident in my cultivation. Feel free to strike as you please, Senior Yun Zhi. Don’t worry about whether I can withstand it.”

~~~

Not long after, Shi Chan limped down Heaven’s Gate Peak, his face bruised and swollen.

“Looks like Shifu was right. Senior Yun Zhi indeed can’t be provoked.”

Next, he wandered into the commercial district. He could sense that from the shop owners to the staff, the area abounded with talented dragons and tigers in hiding.

“It seems at least a third of this street are experts.”

In truth, everyone in the commercial district was an expert. It was just that the remaining two-thirds had returned to a state of simplicity, and he couldn’t discern anything.

Suddenly, he halted in his tracks, his expression one of vigilance.

Ahead was a cultivator exuding palpable baleful energy. One could only imagine the number of lives he had taken.

Diabolic Creed?!

I should follow him to check.

He gingerly trailed the cultivator, tailing him halfway down the street before stopping.

That cultivator stopped before a barbeque shop.

Shi Chan’s nose twitched as it sniffed the aroma of the fusion between cumin and lamb, fully stimulated by the flames. It whetted his appetite and caused him to swallow his saliva involuntarily.

“Lamb skewers! Fresh, authentic lamb skewers!”

“Old Gao, Old Liu, I’ve brought you more meat.”

At his words, Chef Liu cheerfully passed his skewers to Chef Gao to be roasted while he accepted the storage ring from the creed leader. Inside were freshly butchered cuts of beef and lamb, so fresh that the muscles still quivered as if they were dancing.

“This little master here, you’ve followed me the entire journey. Is it because you wanted to eat roasted skewers?” The creed leader turned. He had noticed Shi Chan long ago.

“Two skewers for you, little master?” Chef Gao offered kindly.

Shi Chan shook his head firmly. “This little monk didn’t bring money.”

Eating at restaurants isn’t expensive, and if I can’t dine and dash successfully, I can wash the dishes. These barbeque skewers here are pricey, and the bill has to be settled with spirit stones. It’s clearly not something a few days of scrubbing plates could make up for.

“It’s fine. You’re from the Hanging Monastery, right? All visitors are guests. These two skewers are on the house—consider them our treat.”

Shi Chan shook his head again. “I cannot accept it for free. Why don’t we do this? Since you seem to run a breeding farm, and I’ve worked in one before, I could assist you there.”

In fact, Shi Chan had been working in a slaughterhouse before this. If not for Senior Uncle telling me to come to the Dao-Seeking Sect for studies, I would still be in the slaughterhouse. Since there’s an opportunity in the Dao-Seeking Sect, I might as well seize it to continue my cultivation.

“Umm...” The creed leader hesitated. This little monk is clearly a senior monk from the Hanging Monastery. If the Dao-Seeking Sect finds out I let him go to the slaughterhouse, I’m afraid they won’t let me off.

Shi Chan fished out the token given by Dai Bufan. “Senior Brother told me that this token grants me access to any part of the Dao-Seeking Sect.”

Seeing Shi Chan’s unwavering attitude, the creed leader relented, and Shi Chan finally enjoyed the barbeque skewers as he had wished.

He led Shi Chan through the sect's central zone and arrived at a grassland. This was his slaughterhouse. Livestock, such as cows and sheep, were everywhere, and the water and grass were fresh and beautiful.

“Boss, you’re back!”

Three Alluring Ghosts—Little Five, Little Six, and Little Seven—stared in surprise at the monk accompanying the creed leader.

A diabolic creed leader running a breeding farm is already bizarre enough, and now a monk is also joining?

Shi Chan was equally surprised. I didn’t expect the Dao-Seeking Sect to offer shelter to three Alluring Ghosts. Is this their way of embodying the sages’ doctrine of ‘education for all, regardless of background?’

“Shi Chan greets all three female benefactors."

The three female ghosts hurriedly returned the courtesy.

Shi Chan quickly settled into the rhythm of his work. The butcher’s knife in his hand rose and fell as it sliced along the fibers of the beef, dividing the meat into a dozen precise cuts in the blink of an eye.

“Sādhu, excellent. Namo Amitabha-granny nights. Odāta-many nights...”[1]

Setting down his butcher’s knife, Shi Chan chanted the Rebirth Requiem, dispelling the cow’s lingering resentment. This was why no trace of resentment clung to him despite having slaughtered countless cattle. He had long advocated for all butchers to learn the Rebirth Requiem, though progress was unfortunately limited.

If every butcher followed my example, foolish acts like that Great Yu cultivator refining a Soul-Summoning Banner with the resentment of livestock wouldn’t have happened.

“Little master, please cease your powers!” the three Alluring Ghosts beseeched. We are merely at the Foundation Establishment Stage. How could we withstand his high-level Rebirth Requiem?

Shi Chan immediately stopped chanting. He had forgotten that three ghosts were here.

Guilty, he offered graciously, “If you ever get sick of living one day, just tell me. I’ll perform deliverance rituals to help you move on in peace.”

The three Alluring Ghosts hastily declined.

Chapter 547: Master Shi Chan

As a disciple of the Hanging Monastery, the price Shi Chan could command for a single deliverance ritual was astronomical.

In the Central Continent, the Hanging Monastery stood as one of the Five Great Immortal Sects and represented the strongest Buddhist legacy. They could be said to be the leader of all temples in the world—in both practice and spirit.

Therefore, anyone from the Hanging Monastery was held in high esteem in the outside world. Though Shi Chan called himself a “little monk,” people outside addressed him as “Master.” Moreover, his Advanced Golden Core cultivation alone was enough to earn him reverence.

But since these three Alluring Ghosts have rejected my kind intentions, I shouldn’t say anything more.

He pressed his palms together with a compassionate demeanor and approached a cow, speaking solemnly. “We cultivators often say, ‘My fate is mine to command, not Heaven’s.’ We refuse to believe in destiny and rise in defiance. Some have indeed carved out a grand path for themselves, but such cases are ultimately the minority. And whether their resistance against destiny truly succeeded or was itself part of destiny’s arrangement—that remains unknown.

“Perhaps everyone in this world is unknowingly shackled by the chains of destiny. None can resist—not this little monk, not these three female benefactors, and not you.”

One hand was pressed to his chest while the other stroked the back of the cow’s neck.

How could cattle reared in the Dao-Seeking Sect be ordinary? The cow’s lineage was exceptional; the grass and water it fed on daily were likewise exceptional. Its hair was sleek and smooth to the touch, far superior to that of the cattle in the breeding farm Shi Chan previously worked at.

“You were born to be slaughtered, to sate mankind’s gluttony. Your flesh is offered to satisfy human greed. It may appear noble, yet in truth, it is but the outcome of your helplessness.

“This little monk shall give you a chance. If you refuse to be shackled by destiny and wish to escape your fate of slaughter, cry once. If you are willing to sacrifice yourself for mankind, cry twice.”

The cow stood motionless and didn’t cry even once.

Shi Chan sighed. “As I thought. You were born dull-witted, lacking innate wisdom, unable to understand human speech or grasp Buddhist teachings.”

Then, Shi Chan quietly recited abstruse and cryptic scriptures. “Within the primordial azure skies in times bygone, the blue firmament echoes vacant hymns, the vast floating land...”

The cow still showed no response.

Shi Chan shook his head helplessly and bent down to pick up the butcher’s knife from the ground. With one swift stroke, the cow breathed its last.

“Sādhu—excellent, excellent.”

The three Alluring Ghosts stared dumbfounded at this scene.

“Young friend, might I ask what you’re doing?” A benevolent voice spoke, deep and infectious.

Shi Chan turned his head, not recognizing who it was. “Benefactor, you are...?”

“You may call me Boss Bu. This breeding farm belongs to me.”

The Everlasting Immortal had seen from afar how Shi Chan had been acting mysteriously, fussing over a cow for half a day before finally slaughtering it with one chop. Shi Chan’s actions left the Everlasting Immortal perplexed.

“Ah, Benefactor Bu. This little monk is a disciple of the Hanging Monastery, with the Buddhist name Shi Chan. What I just did was to edify the cow’s spirit, allowing the cow to make its own choice.

“The scripture I recited is called the Cow Deliverance Sutra.”

“Cow Deliverance Sutra?” The Everlasting Immortal mumbled. I’ve never heard of it.

“This is a sutra I composed. There’s also the Pig Deliverance Sutra and Sheep Deliverance Sutra. At the previous slaughterhouse, I would recite these sutras before slaughter to let the livestock choose their own fate. Though so far, not a single case has been successful.

“After slaughter, I’d also recite the Rebirth Requiem to dispel the livestock’s lingering resentment for them to pass peacefully.”

The previous cow had been slaughtered by the creed leader, with Shi Chan only responsible for butchering. Only this cow had gone through the complete procedure.

The Everlasting Immortal found Shi Chan’s reasoning sound. Our breeding farm is essentially a slaughterhouse, which people will easily associate with scenes of bloodshed. This is detrimental to our reformed and rehabilitated image. If we follow Shi Chan’s approach—explanation first, slaughter after, then deliverance rituals—Yun Zhi, the first-in-command, and second-in-command will surely see us in a new light.

Only the three of them within the Dao-Seeking Sect knew the true identity of the Everlasting Immortal. More people knew the identities of the creed leader and the others—Dai Bufan and First Elder, in addition to the three of them.

In terms of their approach to matters, the Everlasting Immortal was much like his big boss, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy. They were bold and decisive individuals who acted without hesitation once an idea struck them.

The Everlasting Immortal immediately issued notices to the creed leader and Vice Creed Leader Jin at the breeding farm, as well as to Chef Liu, Chef Gao, and several former Everlasting Creed’s elders at the barbeque shop.

~~~

At night, after the barbeque shop closed, Chef Liu and the others came to the breeding farm.

“Is everyone here?”

“Everyone’s here,” Little Wu and her two companions replied. Although they weren’t members of the Everlasting Creed, they now served as the creed leader’s right-hand assistants and thus needed to attend meetings.

The Everlasting Immortal nodded and recounted Shi Chan’s actions during the day.

The creed leader and the others fell into deep thought. “Immortal, you mean...”

“Everyone here is one of us, so I’ll speak plainly. We’re all prisoners of the Dao-Seeking Sect. There may come a day when they turn against us and have us executed. I believe we should make changes—not just operating the barbeque shop and breeding farm, but creating a completely new image. Shi Chan’s arrival presents an opportunity.

“When studying Buddhist teachings, the greatest taboo is veering off course. Shi Chan comes from the Hanging Monastery and represents orthodox Buddhism. His Buddhist spells must be exquisite and authentic. We should learn from him—cultivate our character and develop a Buddha nature. Only then can we demonstrate that we have truly been reformed.”

The creed leader and the others nodded repeatedly. As expected of an immortal! His level of thinking is different from ours. While we are content with the status quo, the Immortal is already planning the next move.

“Since no one objects, this matter is settled.”

“Umm...” Little Five timidly raised her hand. Since the three ghosts were only at the Foundation Establishment Stage, they found meetings with the creed leader and the rest stressful.

"Feel free to voice your questions.”

“Can we ghosts also study Buddhist teachings?”

The Everlasting Immortal stroked his chin and hissed. “That’s indeed a problem. We’ll ask Shi Chan tomorrow.”

~~~

Early the next morning, all members of the Everlasting Creed sought out Shi Chan.

After hearing them out and pondering briefly, Shi Chan felt these people possessed a strong Buddha nature and had affinity with Buddhism. “Buddha saves those with affinity. Since you wish to learn from this little monk, I will not conceal my skills.

“As for the three female benefactors, don’t worry. There are precedents of ghosts studying Buddhism and even legends of ghosts building temples and reconstructing physical bodies with the power of faith after they mastered Buddhist teachings. It’s no problem.”

The three ghosts finally relaxed. It’s fine as long as we don’t end up sending ourselves off to the next life through our studies.

And thus, they went about their daytime tasks separately, then gathered at night to study Buddhist spells and discuss Buddhist scriptures, maintaining a strict and regular schedule. Shi Chan also gained new insights and epiphanies through these discussions and teachings.

~~~

Dai Bufan looked at the intelligence report just handed to him by a disciple, completely stupefied.

Why did Shi Chan go work at the breeding farm?

Why are those people from the Everlasting Creed starting to learn Buddhist teachings?

How would the Hanging Monastery react if they learn of these matters?

Dai Bufan couldn’t make sense of Shi Chan’s actions. As his shifu’s fate was unknown, Dai Bufan couldn’t count on him. That left only Yun Zhi.

~~~

“Big Senior Sister...”

Dai Bufan explained in detail what Shi Chan was doing and consulted Yun Zhi on how the Dao-Seeking Sect should handle the situation.

After a moment of silence, Yun Zhi slowly said, “When Junior Brother Shi Chan first arrived, he came to challenge me.”

Dai Bufan’s pupils contracted in shock. Is he tired of living?

Even if newborn calves don’t fear tigers, this is too much. Even an old calf like Master Jiesha wouldn’t dare do such a thing.

“Big Senior Sister, you mean...”

“If he dared challenge even me, nothing he does should surprise us.”

“True.”

Chapter 548: The Origins of the Five-Elements Combat Tactic

“Finally, it’s done.”

Lu Yang stretched lazily. Under the transmission elder’s guidance, their progress had been rapid, and the Five-Elements Combat Tactic was beginning to show results.

The transmission elder stroked his white beard and nodded slightly. “Not bad. There’s nothing more I can teach you.”

Among the disciples he had taught, Lu Yang’s group of five were the fastest in mastering the Five-Elements Combat Tactic. This was partly due to Lu Yang’s and Meng Jingzhou’s powerful spiritual consciousness, which played a dominant role in their cultivation. Another crucial factor was their teamwork, which made their learning twice as effective with half the effort.

“The Five-Elements Combat Tactic is indeed strong.”

Li Haoran nodded inwardly. If the Nine-Netherworlds had mastered this, whereby Qin Haoran and the four vice creed leaders joined hands, they might have been able to repel their debt collectors.

Of course, that would have required the four vice creed leaders to be aware of the Nine-Netherworlds Creed’s deficit and remain united afterward.

“Speaking of which, this Five-Elements Battle Tactic is so miraculous. Which senior invented it? Who possessed such incredible talent?” Lu Yang asked curiously.

“It was created by our Five-Elements Sect’s founding ancestor, Teacher Tiankui. He was a genius of his generation, leaving behind numerous legacies as cornerstones for our sect—the Five-Elements Combat Tactic was one of them.”

Teacher Tiankui was a renowned figure in Great Xia. He was an almighty expert who stood alongside the Dao-Seeking Sect’s Primordial Heavenly Sovereign one hundred thousand years ago and was instrumental in spearheading the establishment of the Five Great Immortal Sects.

The transmission elder’s expression grew nostalgic as he recalled the stories passed down through generations in the Five-Elements Sect.

“Teacher Tiankui was born into a scholarly family during the final years of the Great Yu Dynasty. Deeply influenced by the doctrine of ‘rulers should act like rulers, fathers should act like fathers, sons should act like sons,’ he originally planned to pursue an official title through the imperial examinations, enlist in the military, and lay the groundwork for a future rebellion. When the time came, he could rally the masses and proclaim himself king. Would that not be splendid...? Ahem, the last line was Teacher Tiankui’s own words, not mine.

“Unfortunately, before he could gain honor through the imperial examinations, the Yu Emperor was assassinated on his throne, crushing his plans of joining the army and staging a rebellion.”

“...Elder, wait a moment. You just said Teacher Tiankui was deeply influenced by the doctrine of ‘rulers should act like rulers, fathers should act like fathers, sons should act like sons,’ but he rebelled?” Although interrupting an elder was impolite, Meng Jingzhou couldn’t help himself.

“That’s right. Teacher Tiankui was tired of learning those doctrines and wanted to see what would happen if he disregarded them.”

Man Gu was enlightened. That’s another way of being a Confucian cultivator! He didn’t just study blindly but sought to verify the teachings in the books through action. I was too rigid in my past studies.

“When the world fell into chaos, Teacher Tiankui’s cultivation was insufficient to contend for supremacy, so he focused on cultivation and tempered himself on the battlefield, his cultivation growing rapidly with every kill.

“Despite Teacher Tiankui’s rare talent, by the time he became a regional overlord, the Jiang Family had already seized the throne. He was one step too late. Depressed, Teacher Tiankui wandered the world to lift his spirits. One day, he accidentally stumbled into an immortal domain and obtained a great fortuitous opportunity.”

“Immortal domain?” Lu Yang was intrigued by the term. Such places are typically called “secret domains.” If it were qualified to be called an “immortal domain,” it must be related to immortals.

“It’s simply something related to immortals, why act all jumpy? In the presence of this immortal, what’s a mere immortal domain?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy drawled, utterly indifferent. As an immortal myself, all my actions are related to immortals.

Lu Yang eyed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy skeptically. You make it sound like you know the locations of immortal domains. If only you knew even one.

Sensing Lu Yang’s silent judgment, the Everlasting Immortal Fairy huffed and asserted her worth. “This immortal resides in your mental realm, which makes it an immortal’s mental realm. In other words, this is an Immortal Realm!”

This was the first time Lu Yang had heard the “Immortal Realm” explained in this manner. He rolled his eyes and returned to paying attention to the transmission elder’s story.

“According to Teacher Tiankui’s records, that secret domain contained traces of an immortal’s arrangement that spanned eternity and concealed profound mysteries. He even saw the phantoms of immortals lingering through the ages, as if the ancient past was replaying before his eyes, though the immortals’ faces were shrouded in a blur!

“Two immortals engaged in a game of chess, their pieces divided into black and white. The chess opening was exquisite, and each move was deliberate, with months passing between every turn. It was as if they weren’t playing a mere game of chess but the vast expanse of time and all beings in the world!

“As they played, a third immortal appeared in the guise of a woodcutter, observing the chess game.

“Teacher Tiankui was immersed in the scene, and when he regained awareness, a hundred years had already passed! He saw the ferocious battle of the black and white pieces on the chessboard. They were locked in a stalemate, unable to form five in a row. In that moment, he experienced an epiphany.

“Teacher Tiankui believed the five pieces corresponded to the five elements. Aligning five in a row would achieve the final victory, symbolizing the fusion of the five elements, an immense power that could move even immortals.

“He went into seclusion on the spot and created the Five-Elements Combat Tactic based on this insight. After emerging from seclusion, he founded the Five-Elements Sect.

“Unfortunately, upon emerging from seclusion, the immortals’ shadows had vanished and never appeared again.

“Teacher Tiankui claimed to be dull-witted, only managing to comprehend a fraction of the game’s profundity. He believed the chess match held deeper layers of meaning he had failed to discover. For example, why did the third immortal come to observe the chess game as a woodcutter? What did chopping wood signify? Did it imply that all living beings were firewood ready to be kindled, or was it to express his neutral stance?”

The transmission elder shook his head regretfully. There are too many unanswered questions in this story. The ancient era was mysterious, and even at our current positions, our understanding of ancient times is nothing more than fragments.

Lu Yang, “...”

He remembered the Everlasting Immortal Fairy mentioning how the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal had used a chess game as an excuse, refusing to eat her cooking. The Everlasting Immortal Fairy sent the Nine-Layers Immortal to chop wood to prepare the meal, but after gathering firewood, he went to watch the chess match instead, and the three immortals ended up playing chess for a hundred years.

Lu Yang had assumed that a chess match lasting a century must be something like Weiqi, which embodied the essence of the cosmos.

Turns out they were playing Five in a Row!

“See? What did I say? The Nine-Layers Immortal integrated yin-yang and the five elements into the chessboard to enlighten future generations. Isn’t this living proof?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy declared triumphantly, finally finding evidence to support her claims.

“By the way, Elder, is that immortal domain still around?”

“It is. Although the immortals’ phantoms are gone and no one can comprehend anything from it anymore, Teacher Tiankui thought it was, after all,an immortal domain, so he moved it back to our sect.”

Lu Yang mused, No wonder the first Metal Elder had hauled entire mines back to the sect. Your founding sect leader even relocated immortal domains!

But now isn’t the time for sarcasm.

“Can we enter the secret domain to observe the immortal chess game?”

No matter what, it’s a place where three immortals once stayed. There might be clues.

At Lu Yang’s words, Meng Jingzhou and the others grew excited. This is related to immortals! We mustn’t miss out!

After some thought, the transmission elder said, “I’ll need to consult the sect leader about this, though I expect he’ll agree.”

Chapter 549: Reenactment of History

“They wish to visit the site where the founding ancestor comprehended the Dao?” Qiu Jin’an was momentarily stunned upon hearing the transmission elder’s words.

One hundred thousand years ago, when the founding ancestor first comprehended the Dao, the immortal domain had been a forbidden ground, off-limits to all except Transcendent Tribulation cultivators. As time passed over the next hundred thousand years, countless youth prodigies and unparalleled experts could venture into the immortal domain, seeking fortuitous opportunities and attaining enlightenment. They hoped to replicate the founding ancestor’s magnificent feat, but not a single one had succeeded.

As for the scene of immortals playing chess—a re-enactment of history—it never appeared again. To this day, there was still no consensus on the true identities of those three ancient immortals.

Qiu Jin’an raised his head and happened to catch sight of an old painting hanging on the wall. The artwork exuded an immortal aura, encompassing boundless, profound marvels—unfathomable and inscrutable. Although it was an “old painting,” an explicable power seemed to protect it, making it look nothing like a relic from a hundred thousand years ago.

In the painting, two immortals sat upon stone chairs, deep in thought. Though their features were indistinct, one could easily imagine them lowering their heads in contemplation, brows slightly furrowed. A third immortal carrying firewood had their gaze fixed intently on the chessboard, and this immortal’s appearance was similarly obscured.

On the chessboard, black and white pieces were locked in a stalemate and clashed in a fierce battle—encircling, chasing, blocking, and intercepting one another. However, neither side was able to form a proper row.

Teacher Tiankui was a Confucian cultivator with marvelous painting skills. After emerging from the immortal domain, he painted the scene he had witnessed with his brush and ink.

Beside the painting was another old painting, also Teacher Tiankui’s work. In the second painting, Teacher Tiankui was clad in white Confucian robes, spirited and full of vigor, displaying the bearing of a mighty expert.

Under his feet were two famous, unparalleled experts—the respective ancestors of the Meng Family and Jiang Family. These two mighty experts were covered in wounds, clearly having endured a life-and-death struggle, yet they still failed to be a match for Teacher Tiankui.

Teacher Tiankui was a Confucian cultivator with marvellous painting skills. This painting depicted a scene from his imagination.

Qiu Jin’an withdrew his gaze from the two paintings. After brief consideration, he nodded in agreement. “The children probably haven’t encountered an immortal’s relic before. It’s understandable that they’d want to broaden their horizons. Very well, I shall take them there myself.”

After all, this is the site where the founding ancestor had comprehended the Dao. Although it now only retains commemorative significance, it still warrants due reverence.

~~~

When Lu Yang’s group learned that they had been granted permission to enter the immortal domain and that Qiu Jin’an himself would escort them, their faces lit up with smiles.

This is the legendary immortal domain!

Among all publicly known secret domains, none had ever been confirmed as an immortal domain, a testament to the rarity of immortal domains.

Of course, for Lu Yang, whose body was an immortal realm, the immortal domain was hardly anything extraordinary.

Following Qiu Jin’an’s lead, the five soon arrived at their destination. The immortal domain lay at the convergence of the Fire Branch and Water Branch.

“Such a tall mountain,” Man Gu exclaimed. The upper half was shrouded in clouds, making the mountain’s true height discernible. One thing was certain: this mountain wasn’t shorter than Heaven’s Gate Peak.

Qiu Jin’an casually explained, “The immortal domain is inside a cave within this mountain. The founding ancestor was worried that merely moving the cave would ruin the immortals’ arrangement and the immortal domain’s integrity, so he decided to move the entire mountain.”

For a cultivator of Teacher Tiankui’s stature, relocating mountains and filling lakes was a trivial matter.

Lu Yang noticed a fence encircling the mountain, forming a faint barrier, likely a protective measure to prevent disciples from sneaking in and disrupting the immortals’ chessboard. Near the fence’s entrance, an unassuming, half-torn yellow talisman clung stubbornly to the fence, fluttering in the wind.

“That yellow talisman has an incredibly brilliant seal drawn on it,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy commented. Merely glimpsing half of the talisman was enough for her to deduce its design and purpose.

Lu Yang’s heart skipped a beat. Could it be that the immortal domain holds not just a chess game of immortals but also an unparalleled great devil?

He conjured a scene in his mind:

Teacher Tiankui encountered an unparalleled great devil and clashed in a fierce battle, only to lose by the narrowest margin. With no other choice, he sealed the great devil within the immortal domain, suppressing it with the immortals’ chessboard.

As time passed, the Five-Elements Sect forgot this part of history, while the great devil broke through the seal and escaped from the immortal domain.

Or perhaps the great devil wielded something similar to the Karma Dao Fruit and made others forget his existence?

Judging by Sect Leader Qiu’s reaction, he doesn’t seem to have noticed this half-piece yellow talisman.

Lu Yang pointed at the inconspicuous scrap of talisman. “Sect Leader Qiu, what is that? Is it a seal?”

“It’s a seal strip.”

Lu Yang, “...”

“The founding ancestor was in a hurry when he moved the mountain and didn’t get the imperial court’s approval. The imperial court wasn’t happy and sealed off the immortal domain, pasting a seal strip on it.

“After paying a fine and bailing the founding ancestor out, the imperial court agreed to transfer ownership of the mountain range and immortal domain to our sect. The seal strip became useless afterward.

“They didn’t tear the seal strip off completely, and later generations thought it was a small historical relic, so they left it there.”

A seal strip capable of sealing off the immortal domain was naturally no ordinary item.

Seeing no further questions from the group, Qiu Jin’an led them past the fence and toward the mountain’s base. The closer they got, the more oppressive the mountain felt. Without pause, they entered a damp mountain cave.

The moment they stepped inside, their restless hearts stilled, as if the mental state of the immortals playing chess three hundred thousand years ago still lingered in the air.

The cave was silent, dark, and deep, their footsteps echoing hollowly through the passage. The deeper they went, the drier the environment became, as though the inside and outside of the cave belonged to separate worlds.

“We’re here,” Qiu Jin’an announced.

Before them stood a stone table, its chessboard filled with black and white pieces; not a single empty space remained. Upon closer inspection, neither side managed to connect five in a row.

The immortals’ chess game had ended in a draw.

The stone table, the stone chairs, and the Five in a Row game were all ordinary objects. It was only because immortals had used them for a century that they were tinged with immortal aura, allowing them to endure the erosion of time.

Qiu Jin’an shook his head regretfully. As I thought, no matter how many times one comes in, the scene from back then won’t reappear again. The founding ancestor’s fortuitous opportunity is a rare fate with immortals that can’t be replicated.

What he failed to notice, however, was Lu Yang’s vacant stare, as though his consciousness had vanished. Lu Yang’s head drooped as if he was nodding off, then suddenly jerked back up.

Before his eyes lay an empty chessboard. Two strangers sat across from each other, their hands hovering over the stone containers, preparing to make their moves.

Meng Jingzhou, Tao Yaoye, and the others had vanished, leaving only Lu Yang, an observer of the chess match.

His heart pounded. Why does this seem like Teacher Tiankui’s story?

Before he could react, he heard the two players speak. Their voices carried a peculiar power, soothing one’s mental state and steadying one’s spirit. freewebnovel.com

“Heaven Mandate Immortal, you first?”

“Very well.”

Clack. A white stone landed in the middle of the chessboard.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal had made his move.

Chapter 550: Immortals’ Chess Game

Through the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s accounts, Lu Yang had long been well-acquainted with the Heaven Mandate Immortal and his deeds, from before his rise to fame to the days after his immortal ascension.

But standing face-to-face with the Heaven Mandate Immortal like this was a first.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal wore a pale blue robe with wide sleeves, its lapels adorned with wave-like patterns. He had a dignified and imposing bearing, his golden pupils making him look commanding like an emperor.

“According to the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, the Heaven Mandate Immortal was playing chess with the Qilin Immortal. So the one sitting across from him is the Qilin Immortal?” Lu Yang turned his gaze to the other player.

The Qilin Immortal bore two coral horns upon his head, his cheeks and the back of his hands covered in crimson sales. His eyes resembled those of dragons and tigers, exuding a baleful energy. This wasn’t a sign of an incomplete transformation. Rather, it was his mark of pride as a qilin.

As the sole qilin in the world, taking human form was merely a convenience for interacting with the other four immortals. Therefore, there was no need to fully transform into a human. Retaining his qilin features was his source of pride.

The Qilin Immortal was clad in black robes. Upon closer inspection, one would notice its intricate embroidery depicting myriad beasts. Only he, the immortal of myriad beasts, was worthy to don this garment.

“A historical projection?”

Lu Yang was stunned. This is exactly like the story the transmission elder had told us—accidentally stumbling into an immortal domain and witnessing two immortals playing a game of chess.

Although immortals stood at the pinnacle of the cultivation system, their every action didn’t necessarily leave behind historical projections. Otherwise, wouldn’t the entire world be able to see immortals?

The reason a projection remained here was that this chess game had taken up a hundred years of three immortals’ lives, and their immense power had warped the space.

“Wait, that’s not right either. The transmission elder said Teacher Tiankui only saw the immortals, but their faces were blurry. Why can I see them so clearly?

“Could it be that these two immortals and I...”

“Of course, it’s because of this immortal.” The happy-go-lucky voice of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy rang out.

Lu Yang turned to see her standing beside him. She wore a yellow dress and floated slightly so their eyes were level. Since this was a historical projection, Qiu Jin’an and the others wouldn’t detect her presence.

“Immortal Fairy, you’re here too?” That makes sense. If I can see this historical projection, there’s no reason the Everlasting Immortal Fairy can’t.

“What are you saying? How would you be able to see those two lousy chess players without me? It’s because I resonated with their historical projection that you’re witnessing this scene now.” She pointed at the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal smugly.

As soon as the Everlasting Immortal Fairy appeared, the awe Lu Yang had felt toward immortals instantly evaporated. “Then what about Teacher Tiankui? Did he happen to catch the last scene of the historical projection’s reappearance?”

“It was probably the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s doing.”

“The Heaven Mandate Immortal?” Lu Yang’s expression turned odd. Is it inappropriate to say this right in front of him?

But how could the Everlasting Immortal Fairy bother with this? Forget phantom images, even if the real Heaven Mandate Immortal were here, she would dare say it to his face.

“You’ve got it backward. Teacher Tiankui didn’t comprehend the Five-Elements Combat Tactic because he saw this historical projection—he saw this historical projection because he could comprehend the Five-Elements Battle Tactic in the first place.

“Later generations couldn’t see this historical projection, not because it dissipated, but because none of them could comprehend anything from the chessboard. If word got out, it wouldn’t boost their prestige.”

Lu Yang was speechless. Once again, he recognized the Heaven Mandate Immortal’s painstaking efforts.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal continued their game, each chess piece landing with a soft clack. Just listening to the sound alone cleansed Lu Yang’s mind and heart, as if his soul was elevating.

“They play chess this fast?” At this speed, how could they have played for a hundred years? Twenty minutes would be pushing it.

“What’s so interesting about watching these two lousy chess players? I sped things up,” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy remarked lazily. Who in their right mind would waste a hundred years watching a chess game like that fool Tiankui? freewebnovel.com

“So you two have been playing chess here. I’ve finally found you.” The voice of a third ancient immortal could be heard. It was none other than the Nine-Layers Immortal, the creator of Five in a Row.

Clad in a plain hemp garment and a straw raincoat, the Nine-Layers Immortal strode in, dripping wet as if it was raining outside. He held an axe in one hand and a bundle of freshly cut firewood on his back, looking every bit like an old woodcutter.

The only unusual detail was that the firewood he carried was completely dry.

“Ho, isn’t this wutong wood?[1] Did the Epoch Immortal send you to chop it?” The Heaven Mandate Immortal chuckled.

“How do you two still have the face to say that?! The Epoch Immortal told me to fetch you for dinner, yet here you are hiding away playing chess. It’s been years, and you still haven’t finished?!”

“What’s the rush? It’s rare for us to have a chance to determine a winner between us. Shouldn’t we take this match seriously? Every move requires careful deliberation. You get it?”

“You go ahead and eat. We’ll join you shortly.”

The Nine-Layers Immortal scoffed. At the rate you two are playing, you won’t even finish in fifty years. And you’re asking if I get it? I invented Five in a Row. How could you two know it better than me?

“Never mind, I’ll stay and watch, lest you start another game after this one.” The Nine-Layers Immortal found an excuse to linger with a peace of mind.

“The Epoch Immortal?” Lu Yang murmured with a frown. Why would the Epoch Immortal send the Nine-Layers Immortal to chop firewood and fetch the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal to eat?

Shouldn’t it have been the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

Realization suddenly dawned upon him. Indeed. The ancient mastermind had erased all information about the Everlasting Immortal Fairy through unknown means, and even historical projections aren’t spared—they also have to be erased and replaced.

Take Teacher Tiankui, for example. He might have learned of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s existence from the historical projection.

Completely erasing all traces of the Everlasting Immortal Fairy would have been too difficult and easily left logical loopholes that risked detection. The best solution is to substitute her with another entity of equal standing. That’s why the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had been replaced by the Epoch Immortal in this scene.

However, judging by how Teacher Tiankui couldn’t identify these three immortals, he likely couldn’t understand the ancient language.

Lu Yang had only managed to learn the ancient language under the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s guidance. Due to the cultivation world’s periodization of history, merely translating the ancient language was a feat in itself, let alone speaking or understanding it.

He stole a glance at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, only to see her grinding her teeth in fury. “Which bastard masked my existence?” She even cracked her knuckles, ready to go all out against the mastermind at any moment.

“Who’s there?!” the Nine-Layers Immortal suddenly hollered, turning his head to stare directly at where Lu Yang and the Everlasting Immortal Fairy stood.

For a fleeting moment, Lu Yang even felt their eyes had met.

After the Nine-Layers Immortal’s shouted, the Heaven Mandate Immortal and the Qilin Immortal also snapped to attention, their gazes fixed on the same spot. Although they couldn’t see anyone, they could faintly sense their presence!

The three of them felt guilty about avoiding the Everlasting Immortal Fairy, so they naturally reacted strongly when they detected someone lurking in the shadows.

“Strange. With our capabilities, how could we not see anyone who’s hiding? Even the Epoch Immortal can’t pull it off. Could the Epoch Immortal be observing us from the future through his Epoch Dao Fruit?”

1. Wutong is also known as the Chinese parasol tree. ☜

Chapter 551: Concealment

Sensing someone peering at them across time, the atmosphere in the immortal domain instantly grew tense.

“Could the Epoch Immortal be checking how long we’ll keep playing before using his Epoch Dao Fruit?” The Qilin Immortal’s expression turned peculiar, though he also had to admit that taking months to make a move in Five in a Row was excessive.

The three immortals fell silent, each finding this possibility plausible.

“Immortal Fairy, they can see us?!” Lu Yang jumped in fright. Three hundred thousand years separate us, and I’m simply observing a historical projection, yet they could still detect my presence. Isn’t that too terrifying?

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy side-eyed him. “Don’t flatter yourself and stick gold to your face. They sensed my presence.”

If the three immortals could detect Lu Yang’s cultivation, they would have noticed him the moment the historical projection began. Furthermore, Teacher Tiankui, whose cultivation far surpassed Lu Yang, hadn’t elicited any reaction from the three immortals.

“If we’re talking about ‘seeing,’ only the Epoch Immortal can peer across time and see the future us from the past. This trio just vaguely sensed something, but they can’t identify who’s watching them.”

Even then, Lu Yang found immortals terrifying enough. So not all immortals are like the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy suspected Lu Yang was mentally disrespecting her, but she had no proof.

The Nine-Layers pondered, then proposed another theory. “It may not be the Epoch Immortal. Future immortals could have seen us across time. After all, at the pace you two play chess, we three will be stuck here for a century. That’s plenty of time for a historical projection to form.”

“You mean an immortal has seen our historical projection?”

“Indeed, that’s possible. With only us four immortals now and a bunch of incompetent half-immortals failing to ascend, it’s perfectly normal for a few more immortals to emerge over the eons.”

The three burst into laughter. If a few more immortals emerge in later generations, perhaps they could share the pain brought by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

“Hey! Nine-Layers! Heaven Mandate! Qilin! Can you hear me?” the Everlasting Immortal Fairy yelled, releasing her aura waves, attempting to transmit them over.

The Heaven Mandate Immortal hadn’t detected my presence when I first watched the historical projection. It was only when I mentioned punishing the mastermind and accidentally leaked my aura that he noticed me.

“This aura...”

The three immortals immediately became vigilant. The aura was faint like a candle on the verge of burning out. It was barely perceptible, but they could still sense the other party’s presence from that lingering wisp of aura.

“This aura is ███!”

Recognition flashed across their visages simultaneously.

The Everlasting Immortal Fairy had beaten them since childhood and detonated them after immortal ascension, and she was also the reason they were currently hiding here. They couldn’t be any more familiar with this aura!

Huang Doudou! It’s definitely Huang Doudou!

Cold sweat drenched their backs. We didn’t say anything bad about her just now, right?

Whew. Probably not.

“Can you three hear me?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy made several attempts, but eventually shook her head and gave up in disappointment after the lack of response from the three immortals. Seems like they can’t hear me.

Lu Yang frowned. When the immortals noticed the future Everlasting Immortal Fairy, they’d probably said her name, but I only saw the Nine-Layers Immortal open his mouth—no sound came out, and his lip movements didn’t match the words “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” either.

“The concealment is truly brutal.” Replacing the “Everlasting Immortal Fairy” with the “Epoch Immortal” in this context would have been a major loophole; even a fool would notice something wrong. A direct and crude concealment is the cleaner solution.

“Don’t you find it strange?” The Heaven Mandate Immortal frowned, rotating a chess piece between his fingers. ███ has been releasing aura waves all this time. Is ███ trying to communicate something to us?”

He initially assumed the Everlasting Immortal Fairy had inadvertently seen their historical projection and wanted to tease them by releasing her aura waves.

But if that’s the case, releasing her aura once would be enough. Why do it continuously? Is she just carried away by toying with us, or is she trying to send us a message but is unable to do so due to the vast gap in time?

If it’s the latter, why is the Everlasting Immortal Fairy the one transmitting the information? Wouldn’t the Epoch Immortal be a more effective messenger?

Wait, could an accident have happened in later generations, preventing the Epoch Immortal from passing on the information?

“Nine-Layers, call Epoch over. Tell him to check what’s going on. I suspect ███ needs something from us!”

“Also, don’t let ███ know about this,” the Qilin Immortal added. No one knows what will happen if the Everlasting Immortal Fairy from the past and future meet. Will a tunnel of time be forced open, will they be annihilated on the spot, or will a huge explosion occur—no one knows.

“Alright.” The Nine-Layers Immortal needed no further explanation from the other two immortals. He could figure out these matters himself too.

The Nine-Layers Immortal transformed into a streak of light and ripped space apart. With each step equivalent to tens of thousands of light-years, he crossed countless galaxies and arrived at the North Star, managed by the Everlasting Immortal Fairy.

~~~

The North Star was wreathed in immortal energy. A single breath could extend the lifespans of mortals and sweep away their illnesses.

He saw numerous cultivators kneeling by the river, performing elaborate kowtows to the Everlasting immortal statue erected at the riverbank. After that, they respectfully collected a bowl of river water. This was a specialty of the North Star—the Mother-Child River and the Twins River.

Arriving at the Everlasting Immortal Fairy’s immortal abode, he saw her exchanging culinary arts with the Qilin Immortal’s two wives in the kitchen. The Epoch Immortal shifted in his seat uneasily, likely racking his brain for an excuse to escape.

“Hmm? Nine-Layers is back? You’re done chopping wutong wood?” The Everlasting Immortal Fairy peeked out from the kitchen with a grin, her face caked with patches of flour.

The Nine-Layers froze on the spot. I tried so hard to conceal my aura, yet she still detected me.

“I’m done chopping. It took quite a bit of effort.” As someone who had weathered storms, he swiftly reacted, putting down the wutong wood on his back.

“You’ve worked hard, Big Brother Nine-Layers.” The phoenix prodigy cheerfully hauled the wutong wood to the kitchen, whereupon the kitchen emitted constant sounds of dragon roars and phoenix cries. It was unclear what meal they were preparing.

The Nine-Layers Immortal shouted, “The two lousy chess players, Heaven Mandate and Qilin, kept crying foul, insisting they hadn’t made their move. Epoch, go over there and help be their judge.”

The Epoch Immortal gazed at the Nine-Layers Immortal with gratitude. Good brother, it was worth letting you claim the honor of being the first to ascend to an immortal.

“Sure, I’ll head over now.”

Soon, the Epoch Immortal sensed something amiss upon seeing the Nine-Layers Immortal’s grave expression. It doesn’t look like he’s helping me escape, but rather, he needs my help for something.

What could he possibly need my help with? And he deliberately avoided the Everlasting Immortal Fairy?

The Epoch Immortal vaguely realized something had happened.

The first two immortals retraced their path and crossed countless galaxies, their speed faster than the Nine-Layers Immortal’s alone. After listening to the Nine-Layers Immortal’s recount along the way, the Epoch Immortal’s expression grew somber, and he fell silent.
